 <hr>
  <h3 align="center">Maori Bible: Psalms</h3> 
 <p><a name="an_1:1">1:1</a> ¶ Ka hari te tangata kahore nei e haere i te whakaaro o te tangata kino, a kahore e tu i te ara o te hunga hara, kahore ano e noho i te nohoanga o te hunga whakahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:2">1:2</a> Engari ko te ture a Ihowa tana e whakaahuareka ai; kei tona ture ona whakaaro i te ao, i te po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:3">1:3</a> E rite hoki ia ki te rakau i whakatokia ki te taha o nga awa wai, e whai hua nei i te po e hua ai: e kore tona rau e memenga; a ka pono ana mea katoa e mea ai ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:4">1:4</a> ¶ E kore e pera nga tangata kino; engari ka rite ki te papapa e aia ana e te hau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:5">1:5</a> Ae ra, e kore e tu te hunga kino i te whakawakanga, me te hunga hara i te whakaminenga o te hunga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:6">1:6</a> E matau ana hoki a Ihowa ki te ara o te hunga tika: ko te ara ia o te hunga kino e ngaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:1">2:1</a> ¶ He aha ka nana ai nga tauiwi, ka whakaaro horihori ai nga iwi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:2">2:2</a> Whakatika mai ana nga kingi o te whenua, runanga tahi ana nga ariki, ki te whawhai ki a Ihowa, ki tana tangata hoki i whakawahi ai; me te ki ano,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:3">2:3</a> Kia motumotuhia e tatou a raua here, kia akiritia a raua taura i a tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:4">2:4</a> Ko ia kei te rangi e noho ana, ka kata ia: ka whakahi te Ariki ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:5">2:5</a> Na ka korero ia ki a ratou me te riri ano: ka tino weriweri hoki, ka whakahorere i a ratou,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:6">2:6</a> Ahakoa ra ka whakawahia e ahau taku kingi ki runga ki taku maunga tapu, ki Hiona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:7">2:7</a> ¶ Maku e whakapuaki te kupu, kua mea a Ihowa ki ahau, Ko koe taku tama, nonaianei koe i whakatupuria ai e ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:8">2:8</a> Inoi ki ahau, a ka hoatu e ahau ki a koe nga tauiwi hei kainga mou, me nga topito o te whenua hei nohoanga tupu mou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:9">2:9</a> Ka wawahi koe i a ratou ki te whiu rino, mongamonga noa ratou i a koe, ano he oko na te kaihanga rihi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:10">2:10</a> ¶ Na kia mahara ra, e nga kingi: kia akona, e nga kaiwhakawa o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:11">2:11</a> Mahi atu ki a Ihowa i runga i te wehi, kia hari me te wiri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:12">2:12</a> Kihia te tama kei riri ia, a ka mate koutou i te ara, ka hohoro tonu hoki te mura o tona riri. Ka hari katoa te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:1">3:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri, i tona omanga atu i tana tama i a Apoharama. E Ihowa, ano te tini o oku hoariri, he tokomaha te hunga e whakatika mai ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:2">3:2</a> He tokomaha te mea ana ki toku wairua, hore rawa he whakaoranga mona i te Atua. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:3">3:3</a> Ko koe ia, e Ihowa, hei whakangungu rakau moku, hei kororia moku, hei kaiwhakaara i toku matenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:4">3:4</a> ¶ I karanga toku reo ki a Ihowa: a whakahoki kupu mai ana ia ki ahau i tona maunga tapu. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:5">3:5</a> I takoto ahau, i moe; i ara ake ano; na Ihowa hoki ahau i whakamau ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:6">3:6</a> E kore ahau e mataku i nga mano tini o te iwi, kua whakatika mai nei ki ahau karopoti noa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:7">3:7</a> Whakatika, e Ihowa; whakaorangia ahau, e toku Atua: nau hoki i patu te kauae o oku hoariri katoa; mangungu noa i a koe nga niho o te hunga kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:8">3:8</a> Na Ihowa te whakaoranga: kei runga i tau iwi tau manaaki. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:1">4:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nekinoto. He himene na Rawiri. Whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau, e te Atua o toku tika, ina karanga ahau: i ahau i te pouri i whakaputaina ahau e koe; kia atawhai ki ahau, whakarongo ki taku inoi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:2">4:2</a> E nga tama a te tangata, kia pehea te roa o ta koutou mea i toku kororia hei whakama, o ta koutou aroha ki te horihori, o ta koutou whai i te teka? (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:3">4:3</a> Otiia kia mohio koutou he mea momotu ke na Ihowa te tangata tapu mana: e whakarongo a Ihowa ua karanga ahau ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:4">4:4</a> Kia oho koutou, a kaua e hara: korerorero ki o koutou ngakau i runga i o koutou moenga, me te ata takoto ano. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:5">4:5</a> Patua nga whakahere o te tika, me te okioki ano ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:6">4:6</a> ¶ He tokomaha te mea ana, Ma wai e whakakite te pai ki a matou? Kia ara, e Ihowa, te marama o tou mata ki runga ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:7">4:7</a> Hira ake te hari i homai e koe ki roto ki toku ngakau i to ratou i te wa i hua ai a ratou witi, ta ratou waina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:8">4:8</a> Ka takoto marire ahau, a moe tonu iho: ko koe anake hoki, e Ihowa, hei mea kia au toku noho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:1">5:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nehiroto. He himene na Rawiri. Tahuri tou taringa, e Ihowa, ki aku kupu, kia mohio koe ki toku whakaaroaronga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:2">5:2</a> Whakarongo ki te reo o taku karanga, e toku Kingi, e toku Atua, he inoi hoki taku ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:3">5:3</a> E rongo koe ki toku reo, e Ihowa, i te ata; i te ata ka whakatikaia atu e ahau taku inoi ki a koe, a ka titiro matatau atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:4">5:4</a> Ehara hoki koe i te Atua e pai ana ki te hara, e kore te kino e noho ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:5">5:5</a> E kore te hunga wairangi e tu ki tou aroaro: e kinongia ana e koe nga kaimahi katoa i te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:6">5:6</a> E ngaro i a koe te hunga korero teka; e whakarihariha ana a Ihowa ki te tangata toto, ki te tangata hianga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:7">5:7</a> ¶ Ko ahau ia ka haere i runga i te tini o au atawhai ki tou whare: ka koropiko ki te ritenga o tau temepara tapu, me te wehi ano ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:8">5:8</a> E Ihowa, arahina ahau i runga i tou tika, he hoariri hoki oku; whakatikaia tau ara i mua i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:9">5:9</a> Kahore hoki he pono i o ratou mangai; he kino kau a roto i a ratou; he urupa puare noa o ratou korokoro; e patipati ana o ratou arero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:10">5:10</a> Whakataua te hara ki a ratou, e te Atua; kia hinga ratou i o ratou whakaaro; peia atu ratou me a ratou tini mahi tutu; mo ratou i whakakeke ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:11">5:11</a> Na kia hari katoa te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a koe: kia hamama tonu ratou i te koa, mo ratou e hipokina nei e koe; a kia whakamanamana ki a koe te hunga e aroha ana ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:12">5:12</a> No te mea ka manaakitia e koe, e Ihowa, te tangata tika; me he whakangungu rakau te manako e karapotia ai ia e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:1">6:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nekinoto, he mea Heminiti. He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, kaua e whakatupehupehu mai ki ahau, ina riri koe, kaua ano ahau e pakia ina arita mai koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:2">6:2</a> E Ihowa, tohungia ahau, he ngoikore hoki ahau: rongoatia ahau, e Ihowa, e ohooho ana hoki oku wheua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:3">6:3</a> E ohooho noa iho ana hoki toku wairua: ko koe ia, e Ihowa, kia pehea atu te roa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:4">6:4</a> Hoki mai, e Ihowa, kia mawhiti atu toku wairua: kia mahara ki tou aroha, a whakaorangia ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:5">6:5</a> Kahore hoki he mahara ki a koe ina mate: ko wai hei whakawhetai ki a koe i roto i te reinga?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:6">6:6</a> Mauiui iho ahau i toku auetanga; e manu ana toku moenga i ahau a pau noa te po; e whakamakukuria ana e ahau toku takotoranga ki oku roimata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:7">6:7</a> Pakoko kau toku kanohi i te tangi; kua koroheke haere i oku hoariri katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:8">6:8</a> ¶ Mawehe atu i ahau, e nga kaimahi katoa i te kino; kua rongo nei hoki a Ihowa i te reo o taku tangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:9">6:9</a> Kua rongo a Ihowa ki taku inoi; ka manako a Ihowa ki taku karakia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:10">6:10</a> Ka whakama, ka pokaikaha noa iho oku hoariri katoa: ka hoki ratou, ka pa whakarere atu te whakama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:1">7:1</a> ¶ He Hikaiono na Rawiri, tana i waiata ai ki a Ihowa mo nga kupu a Kuhu Pineamine. E Ihowa, e toku Atua, kei a koe toku whakawhirinakitanga: kia ora ahau i te hunga katoa e aru ana i ahau, kia mawhiti atu hoki ahau:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:2">7:2</a> Kei haehae ia i toku wairua, ano he raiona, a titaritari noa, i te mea kahore he kaiarai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:3">7:3</a> E Ihowa, e toku Atua, ki te mea naku tena mahi, ki te mea he hara kei oku ringa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:4">7:4</a> Ki te mea i whakahokia e ahau he kino ki te tangata kua mau nei ta maua rongo; i whakaora nei hoki ahau i te tangata i kino noa mai ki ahau:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:5">7:5</a> Kia arumia toku wairua e te hoariri, a kia mau; kia takahia hoki toku ora e ia ki te whenua, kia whakatokotoria ano toku kororia ki te puehu. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:6">7:6</a> E Ihowa, whakatika, kia riri koe, ara ake, e nana nei hoki oku hoa whawhai: kia oho ake hoki koe moku; kua kiia e koe te whakawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:7">7:7</a> Tukua kia karapotia koe e te whakaminenga o nga iwi: ma runga atu i a ratou tou hokinga atu ki runga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:8">7:8</a> Ko Ihowa e whakarite whakawa ana mo nga iwi; kia rite, e Ihowa, tau whakawa moku ki taku mahi tika, ki te tapatahi hoki o oku whakaaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:9">7:9</a> Kia whakamutua te kino o te hunga kino: whakaukia hoki te tangata tika: e whakamatautau ana hoki te Atua tika i nga ngakau, i nga whatumanawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:10">7:10</a> ¶ Kei te Atua toku whakangungu rakau, mana e whakaora te hunga ngakau tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:11">7:11</a> He kaiwhakawa tika te Atua, ae ra, he Atua e riri ana i tenei ra, i tenei ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:12">7:12</a> Ki te kore tetahi e tahuri, ka whakakoia e ia tana hoari; kua whakapikoa e ia tana kopere, a oti rawa te whakapai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:13">7:13</a> Oti rawa ano ana mea whakamate te whakapai e ia; kua meinga e ia ana pere ano he ahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:14">7:14</a> Nana, he kino te mea e whakamamae nei ia; he whanoke te mea i hapu ki roto ki a ia, a whanau ake he teka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:15">7:15</a> I pokaia e ia he poka, he mea keri nana, taka iho ia ki roto ki te rua i mahia e ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:16">7:16</a> Ka hoki tona whanoke ki tona matenga, a ka tau iho tana tukino ki tona tumuaki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:17">7:17</a> Ka rite ki tona tika taku whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa: ka himene atu hoki ahau ki te ingoa o Ihowa, o te Runga Rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:1">8:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Kititi. He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, e to matou Ariki, ano te nui o tou ingoa i te whenua katoa! Paku ana i a koe tou kororia ki runga ake i nga rangi!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:2">8:2</a> U pu i a koe te kaha o te mangai o nga kohungahunga, o nga mea ngote u hei mea mo ou hoariri, hei pehi mo te hoariri, mo te kairapu utu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:3">8:3</a> ¶ Ka titiro ahau ki au rangi, ki te mahi a ou maihao, ki te marama, ki nga whetu, i hanga nei e koe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:4">8:4</a> He aha te tangata i maharatia ai e koe? te tama ranei a te tangata i tirohia ai ia e koe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:5">8:5</a> Nohinohi nei te wahi i whakaititia iho ai ia e koe i te Atua, karaunatia ana ia e koe ki te kororia, ki te honore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:6">8:6</a> Waiho iho e koe hei kingi mo nga mahi a ou ringa; kua waiho e koe nga mea katoa i raro i ona waewae;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:7">8:7</a> Nga hipi katoa, nga puru, me nga kirehe katoa o te parae;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:8">8:8</a> Te manu o te rangi, me te ika o te moana, e tere nei i nga ara o nga moana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:9">8:9</a> E Ihowa, e to matou Ariki, ano te nui o tou ingoa i te whenua katoa!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:1">9:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Muturapena. He himene na Rawiri. Ka whakapaua toku ngakau ki te whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa, ka korerotia e ahau au mahi whakamiharo katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:2">9:2</a> Ka koa ahau, ka whakamanamana ki a koe, ka himene atu ki tou ingoa, e te Runga Rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:3">9:3</a> I te hokinga whakamuri o oku hoariri, tutuki ana ratou, ngaro iho i tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:4">9:4</a> Nau hoki i whakatika aku korero me toku whakawa; i runga koe i te torona e noho ana, e whakarite tika ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:5">9:5</a> Kua whakatupehupehu koe ki nga tauiwi, huna ana e koe te tangata kino, horoia atu ana to ratou ingoa ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:6">9:6</a> Ko te hoariri, mutu pu ratou, he ngaromanga oti tonu iho: a ko nga pa i huna e koe, ngaro whakarere to ratou whakamaharatanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:7">9:7</a> Ko Ihowa ia noho tonu hei kingi ake, ake: kua whakapaia e ia tona torona mo te whakawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:8">9:8</a> A e whakarite ia mo te ao i runga i te tika, ka whakatakoto tikanga mo nga iwi i runga i te pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:9">9:9</a> Hei pa teko ano a Ihowa mo te tangata e tukinotia ana, hei pa teko i nga wa o te he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:10">9:10</a> A ka whakawhirinaki ki a koe te hunga e matau ana ki tou ingoa: no te mea e kore e whakarerea e koe, e Ihowa, te hunga e rapu ana i a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:11">9:11</a> ¶ Himene ki a Ihowa e noho nei i Hiona: whakapuakina i waenganui i nga iwi ana mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:12">9:12</a> Ka whakataki toto ia, ka mahara ia ki a ratou: kahore e wareware i a ia te karanga a te hunga iti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:13">9:13</a> Tohungia ahau, e Ihowa; titiro ki toku mate i te hunga e kino ana ki ahau, e te kaiwhakaara i ahau i nga tatau o te mate:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:14">9:14</a> Kia whakakitea katoatia ai e ahau ou whakamoemiti i nga tatau o te tamahine o Hiona: ka hari ahau ki tau whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:15">9:15</a> Kua tapoko nga tauiwi ki te rua i keria e ratou: kua mau to ratou waewae i roto i te kupenga i huna e ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:16">9:16</a> Kua matauria a Ihowa ki te whakawa e whakaritea ana e ia: he mahanga mo te tangata kino te mahi a ona ringa. (Hikaiono. Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:17">9:17</a> Ka hoki nga tangata kino ki te reinga, ara nga iwi katoa e wareware ana ki te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:18">9:18</a> E kore hoki e warewarea tonutia te tangata rawakore: e kore e taka tonu ta te hunga iti i tumanako atu ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:19">9:19</a> E ara, e Ihowa, kei riro i ta te tangata: kia whakawakia nga tauiwi i tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:20">9:20</a> E Ihowa, meinga ratou kia wehi: kia matau nga tauiwi he tangata nei ano ratou. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:1">10:1</a> ¶ He aha koe ka tu mai ai i tawhiti, e Ihowa? ka whakangarongaro ai i nga wa o te he?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:2">10:2</a> E whakakake ana te tangata kino, e tukino ana i te tangata iti: kia hopukina ratou ki nga whakaaro i whakaaro ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:3">10:3</a> E whakapehapeha ana hoki te tnngata kino ki te hiahia o tona ngakau, a ko te hunga apo taonga, e whakakahore ana, ae ra, e whakahawea ana ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:4">10:4</a> Ka mea te tangata kino, i te whakapehapeha o tona mata, E kore e hiahiatia e ia. Kei roto i ona whakaaro katoa e mea ana, Kahore he Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:5">10:5</a> Whanoke tonu ona ara i nga wa katoa; kei runga noa ake au whakaritenga te kitea e ia, he mea whakatupereru e ia ona hoariri katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:6">10:6</a> E mea ana i roto i tona ngakau, e kore ahau e whakakorikoria: kahore hoki he he moku a nga whakatupuranga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:7">10:7</a> Ki tonu tona mangai i te kanga, i te hianga, i te tukino: kei raro i tona arero te whanoke me te teka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:8">10:8</a> E noho ana ia, e whanga ana i nga pa koraha: e kohurutia ana e ia te hunga harakore i nga wahi ngaro; e matatau ana ona kanohi ki te hunga rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:9">10:9</a> E whanga puku ana ia me he raiona i tona kuhunga: e whanga ana kia hopukia te tangata iti: e hopukia ana e ia te tangata iti, ua kumea ki tana. kupenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:10">10:10</a> Kupapa ana ia, piko ana, hinga ana te hunga rawakore i ana mea kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:11">10:11</a> E mea ana i roto i tona ngakau, Ka wareware te Atua: e huna ana ia i tona mata, e kore ia e kite ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:12">10:12</a> ¶ Whakatika, e Ihowa, e te Atua, takiritia tou ringa: kaua e wareware ki te hunga iti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:13">10:13</a> He aha te tangata kino ka whakahawea ai ki te Atua? kua mea ia i roto i tona ngakau, E kore tenei e whakatakina e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:14">10:14</a> Kua kite koe; e tirohia nei hoki e koe te whanoke me te whakatoi, a ka utua e tou ringa: e tuku ana te rawakore i a ia ano ki a koe; ko koe hei tuara mo te pani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:15">10:15</a> Whatiia e koe te ringa o te tangata kino; tena ko te tangata nanakia, whakatakina tona kino, kia kahore ra ano e kitea e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:16">10:16</a> Ko Ihowa te Kingi ake ake: kua kahore ke nga tauiwi i tona whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:17">10:17</a> E Ihowa, kua whakarongo koe ki te hiahia o te hunga whakaiti: mau ano o ratou ngakau e whakapai, ka tahuri ano tou taringa ki te whakarongo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:18">10:18</a> Ki te whakawa mo te pani, mo te tangata e tukinotia ana, kei whakamataku a mua ake te tangata o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:1">11:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Na Rawiri. Ko Ihowa taku e whakawhirinaki ai: he aha koutou ka mea ai ki toku wairua, rere a manu atu ki to koutou maunga?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:2">11:2</a> Nana, kua whakapikoa te kopere e te hunga kino, e whakatikaia ana a ratou pere ki te aho, hei perenga pukutanga ma ratou ki te hunga ngakau tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:3">11:3</a> Ki te wawahia nga turanga ake, me pehea te tangata tika?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:4">11:4</a> ¶ Kei tona temepara tapu a Ihowa, kei te rangi te torona o Ihowa: e titiro ana ona kanohi, e whakamatautau ana ona kamo i nga tama a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:5">11:5</a> E whakamatautau ana a Ihowa i te tangata tika: a e kinogia ana e tona wairua te tangata kino me te tangata e aroha ana ki te tutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:6">11:6</a> Ka uaina e ia ki runga ki te hunga kino he mahanga, he ahi, he whanariki, he awha tuaikerekere: ko te wahi tena mo to ratou kapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:7">11:7</a> No te mea he tika a Ihowa, e aroha ana ki te tika; ka kite te hunga tika i tona kanohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:1">12:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Heminiti. He himene na Rawiri. Whakaorangia, e Ihowa; ka mutu hoki nga tangata tapu; ka taweke atu te hunga pono i roto i nga tama a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:2">12:2</a> E korero teka ana ratou tetahi ki tetahi; he ngutu patipati, he ngakau rua o ratou ina korero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:3">12:3</a> Ka hatepea e Ihowa nga ngutu patipati katoa, me te arero e korero whakapehapeha ana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:4">12:4</a> E mea nei, Ma o tatou arero tatou ka kake ai; no tatou ano o tatou ngutu, ko wai hei ariki mo tatou?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:5">12:5</a> Mo te tukinotanga i te hunga iti, mo te aue a te hunga rawakore, ka whakatika ahau aianei, e ai ta Ihowa, Ka whakanohoia ia e ahau ki te wahi e ora ai ia i nga tangata e whakatupereru ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:6">12:6</a> He kupu parakore nga kupu a Ihowa: he hiriwa i whakakorea nei te para i roto i te oumu whenua, he mea tuku whitu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:7">12:7</a> Ka tiakina ratou e koe, e Ihowa, ka whakaorangia ratou i tenei whakatupuranga ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:8">12:8</a> E haereere noa ana nga tangata kino i tetahi taha, i tetahi taha, i te mea e whakateiteitia ana te kino i roto i nga tama a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:1">13:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. Kia pehea te roa o tou wareware ki ahau, e Ihowa? mo ake tonu atu ranei? Kia pehea te roa o tau hunanga i tou mata ki ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:2">13:2</a> Kia pehea te roa o toku whakaaroaronga i roto i toku wairua, o te pouri i roto i toku ngakau i tenei ra, i tenei ra? Kia pehea te roa o te whakakake mai a toku hoariri ki ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:3">13:3</a> Titiro mai, whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau, e Ihowa, e toku Atua: whakamaramatia oku kanohi, kei moe ahau i te moe o te mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:4">13:4</a> Kei mea mai toku hoariri, Kua taea ia e ahau: kei whakamanamana oku hoariri, ina whakakorikoria ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:5">13:5</a> Ko ahau ia e whakawhirinaki ana ki tau mahi toku: ka whakamanamana toku ngakau ki tau whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:6">13:6</a> Ka waiata ahau ki a Ihowa, mona i atawhai mai ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:1">14:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Na Rawiri. Kua ki te wairangi i tona ngakau, Kahore he Atua. Kua pirau ratou, he whakahouhou a ratou mahi, kahore tetahi e mahi ana i te pai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:2">14:2</a> I titiro iho a Ihowa i te rangi ki nga tama a te tangata, kia kite me kahore tetahi e mahara ana, e rapu ana i te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:3">14:3</a> Kua peka ke ratou katoa kua pirau tahi: kahore tetahi e mahi ana i te pai, kohore kia kotahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:4">14:4</a> ¶ E kore ranei e mohio nga kaimahi katoa o te kino? e kai nei i toku iwi, me te mea e kai taro ana, a kahore e karanga ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:5">14:5</a> Na, i reira ratou e tuiri noa ana: kei roto hoki te Atua i te whakatupuranga o te hunga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:6">14:6</a> Meinga ana e koutou te whakaaro o te hunga iti hei whakama, no te mea ko Ihowa tona piringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:7">14:7</a> Aue, me i puta mai te whakaoranga o Iharaira i Hiona! Kia whakahokia e Ihowa tana iwi i te whakarau, ka whakamanamana a Hakopa, ka hari a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:1">15:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, ko wai e noho ki tou tapenakara? Ko wai e noho ki tou maunga tapu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:2">15:2</a> Ko ia he tapatahi nei te haere, he tika te mahi, he korero pono ano i roto i tona ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:3">15:3</a> Kahore nei e ngautuara tona arero, kahore e kino te mahi ki tona hoa, kahore ana ingoa kino mo tona hoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:4">15:4</a> E whakahengia ana te tangata kino e ona kanohi, e whakahonoretia ana ia e ia te hunga e wehi ana ki a Ihowa. Ahakoa mate i tana oati, kahore e whakapaheketia e ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:5">15:5</a> Kahore e tuku i tana moni hei moni whakatupu; kahore hoki e tango i te moni hei utu mate mo te tangata harakore. Ki te penei te mahi a tetahi, e kore ia e whakakorikoria ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:1">16:1</a> ¶ He Mikitama na Rawiri. Tiakina ahau, e te Atua: e whakawhirinaki nei hoki ahau ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:2">16:2</a> Kua mea ahau ki a Ihowa, Ko koe toku Ariki, kahore oku pai i tua atu i a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:3">16:3</a> Ko te hunga tapu i runga i te whenua, te hunga pai rawa, kua ahau katoa toku ahuareka ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:4">16:4</a> Ka whakanuia nga mamae o te hunga e whakawhiti ana i a Ihowa mo tetahi atua ke: e kore e ringihia e ahau a ratou ringihanga toto, e kore ano o ratou ingoa e whakahuatia e oku ngutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:5">16:5</a> Ko Ihowa te wahi i wehea mai moku, taku kapu hoki: ko koe te kaiwhakapumau i te wahanga maku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:6">16:6</a> Kua takoto oku aho ki nga wahi ahuareka, ina, he wahi pai toku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:7">16:7</a> Ka whakapaingia e ahau a Ihowa, i whakamahara nei i ahau: ka whakaako ano hoki oku whatumanawa i ahau i te po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:8">16:8</a> ¶ Kua waiho tonu e ahau a Ihowa ki toku aroaro: kei toku ringa matau nei ia, e kore ahau e whakakorikoria.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:9">16:9</a> Koia i koa ai toku ngakau, i whakamanamana ai toku kororia, i takoto tumanako ai ano oku kikokiko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:10">16:10</a> No te mea e kore e waiho e koe toku wairua i te reinga, e kore e tukua tau Mea Tapu kia kite i te pirau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:11">16:11</a> Ka whakakitea mai e koe ki ahau te huarahi o te ora; kei tou aroaro te hari nui, kei tou matau nga ahuareka e kore e mutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:1">17:1</a> ¶ He inoi na Rawiri. Whakarongo ki te tika, e Ihowa, tahuri mai ki taku karanga, kia titaha mai tou taringa ki taku inoi, ara ki ta te ngutu tinihangakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:2">17:2</a> Kia puta mai te whakaritenga o taku whakawa i tou aroaro; tirohia mai e ou kanohi te mea rite.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:3">17:3</a> Kua whakamatauria e koe toku ngakau; kua tirotirohia iho ahau e koe i te po; kua whakamatau koe i ahau, a kahore he mea i kitea e koe; e mea ana ahau kia kaua e hara toku mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:4">17:4</a> Ko nga mahi ia a te tangata, ko nga kupu a tou mangai taku mea hei pa mai i ahau i nga ara o te kaiwhakangaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:5">17:5</a> I whakaukia oku hikoinga ki au ara, kihai i paheke oku waewae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:6">17:6</a> Kua karanga nei ahau ki a koe, no te mea ka whakahoki kupu mai koe, e te Atua, ki ahau: whakatitahatia mai tou taringa ki ahau, whakarongo ki taku kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:7">17:7</a> Whakaaturia tou aroha whakamiharo, ko koe hoki, ko tou matau, te kaiwhakaora mo te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a koe, i te hunga e whakatika mai ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:8">17:8</a> ¶ Tiakina ahau, ano ko te whatu o te kanohi, huna ahau ki raro i te taumarumarutanga o ou pakau,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:9">17:9</a> I te hunga kino e tukino nei i ahau, i oku hoariri whakamate e karapoti nei i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:10">17:10</a> E kopakia ana ratou e o ratou ngako: e korero whakapehapeha ana o ratou mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:11">17:11</a> Tenei o matou hikoinga te karapotia nei e ratou: matatau tonu iho o ratou kanohi ki te tuku iho i a matou ki te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:12">17:12</a> Kei te raiona e hiahia ana ki te hopu kai te rite, kei te kuao raiona e piri ana i nga wahi ngaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:13">17:13</a> E ara, e Ihowa, haukotia tona aroaro, turakina ia ki raro; whakaorangia toku wairua ki tau hoari i te tangata kino;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:14">17:14</a> I nga tangata, ma tou ringa, e Ihowa, i nga tangata o te ao: kei tenei ora nei to ratou wahi, a e whakakiia ana o ratou kopu e koe ki tau taonga. E kiki ana ratou i te tamariki, whakarerea iho nga toenga o a ratou taonga ki a ratou kohungahunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:15">17:15</a> Ko ahau, e kite ahau i tou mata i runga i te tika, a ka tatu toku ngakau, ina oho ake ahau, kia kite i tou ahua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:1">18:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na te pononga a Ihowa, na Rawiri. Nana i whakahua nga kupu o tenei waiata ki a Ihowa i te ra i whakaorangia ai ia i te ringa o ona hoariri katoa, i te ringa ano o Haora. I mea ia, Ka aroha ahau ki a koe, e Ihow a, e toku kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:2">18:2</a> Ko Ihowa toku kamaka, toku pa, toku kaiwhakaora; toku Atua, toku tino kamaka, e whakawhirinaki ai ahau; toku whakangungu rakau, te haona o toku whakaoranga, toku pourewa tiketike.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:3">18:3</a> Ka karanga ahau ki a Ihowa, e tika nei kia whakamoemititia: a ka ora i oku hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:4">18:4</a> I karapotia ahau e nga whakawiringa a te mate, a whakawehia ana ahau e nga waipuke o te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:5">18:5</a> I karapotia ahau e nga whakawiringa a te reinga, i haukotia e nga mahanga a te mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:6">18:6</a> I karanga ahau ki a Ihowa i toku paweratanga, i hamama ki toku Atua: i whakarongo ia ki toku reo i roto i tona temepara, i tae ano taku hamama ki tona aroaro, ki ona taringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:7">18:7</a> Na ka ngaueue te whenua, ka ru, wiri ana nga putake o nga maunga, ngaueue ana i tona riri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:8">18:8</a> I kake he paowa i ona pongaponga, a kai ana te kapura a tona mangai, ngiha ana nga waro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:9">18:9</a> I whakapingoretia e ia nga rangi, a heke iho ana, a i raro te pouri matotoru i ona waewae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:10">18:10</a> I eke ia ki runga ki te kerupa, a rere ana: ae, i rere omaki ia i runga i nga parirau o te hau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:11">18:11</a> I meinga e ia te pouri hei wahi ngaro mona, hei teneti i tetahi taha ona, i tetahi taha; ko te pouritanga o nga wai, ko nga kapua matotoru o te rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:12">18:12</a> I rere atu ona kapua metotoru i te wherikotanga o tona aroaro: te whatu, me nga waro kapura.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:13">18:13</a> I papa ano te whatitiri a Ihowa i nga rangi, a puaki ana te reo o te Runga Rawa; he whatu, he waro kapura.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:14">18:14</a> I kokiritia e ia ana pere, a marara ana ratou: ae, i koperea hoki e ia te tini uira, a whati ana ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:15">18:15</a> Katahi ka kitea nga takere o nga wai, a ka takoto kau nga putake o te ao i tau whakatupehupehutanga, e Ihowa, i te whengunga o te manawa o ou pongaponga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:16">18:16</a> I tono karere mai ia i runga, ka mau ki ahau; toia ake ahau e ia i roto i nga wai maha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:17">18:17</a> Nana ahau i ora ai i toku hoariri kaha, i te hunga e kino ana ki ahau; he kaha rawa hoki ratou i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:18">18:18</a> I huakina tatatia ahau e ratou i te ra o toku matenga; ko Ihowa ia toku whakawhirinakitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:19">18:19</a> I whakaputaina ahau e ia ki te wahi nui, i whakaorangia ahau e ia; he ahuareka nona ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:20">18:20</a> ¶ Rite tonu ki taku mahi tika ta Ihowa utu ki ahau: rite tonu ki te ma o oku ringa tana i whakahoki ai ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:21">18:21</a> Moku i pupuri i nga ara o Ihowa, a kihai i he, i whakarere i toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:22">18:22</a> Kei mua tonu hoki i ahau ana whakaritenga katoa, kihai ano i whakamataratia atu i ahau ana tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:23">18:23</a> Tapatahi tonu hoki toku whakaaro ki tona aroaro, a i tiaki ahau i ahau kei kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:24">18:24</a> Na ka homai e Ihowa he utu ki ahau, rite tonu ki toku tika, ki te ma o oku ringa i tona aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:25">18:25</a> He tangata atawhai, ka atawhai hoki koe; he tangata tika, ka tika hoki koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:26">18:26</a> He tangata ma, ka ma hoki koe; he tangata whakakeke, ka whakakeke hoki koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:27">18:27</a> E whakaorangia hoki e koe te iwi ngakau mamae; ka whakahokia ano e koe ki raro nga kanohi whakakake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:28">18:28</a> Mau hoki e whakau taku rama: ma Ihowa, ma toku Atua, e whakamarama toku pouri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:29">18:29</a> ¶ Nau hoki ahau i rere ai na waenganui atu i te ropu: na toku Atua hoki i pekea ai e ahau te taiepa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:30">18:30</a> Tena ko te Atua, tika tonu tona ara: kua oti tana kupu te whakamatau; he whakangungu rakau ia ki te hunga katoa e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:31">18:31</a> Ko wai oti te Atua, ki te kahore a Ihowa? Ko wai hoki he kamaka, ki te kahore to tatou Atua?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:32">18:32</a> Ko te Atua, nana ahau i whitiki ki te kaha, i mea kia tino tika toku ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:33">18:33</a> Ko ia hei mea i oku waewae kia rite ki o te hata: mana hoki ahau e whakatu ki runga ki oku wahi tiketike.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:34">18:34</a> Ko ia hei whakaako i oku ringa ki te whawhai, a whati ana te kopere parahi i oku ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:35">18:35</a> Kua homai ano e koe ki ahau te whakangungu rakau o tau whakaoranga: puritia ana ahau e tou ringa matau whakanuia ana e tou whakaaro mahakai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:36">18:36</a> I whakanuia e koe oku takahanga i raro i ahau; te paheke oku waewae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:37">18:37</a> Ka arumia e ahau oku hoariri, mau iho i ahau; e kore ahau e tahuri mai, a ngaro noa ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:38">18:38</a> Maru ana ratou i ahau, te kaha te whakatika: hinga ana ki raro i oku waewae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:39">18:39</a> Nau hoki ahau i whitiki ki te kaha mo te whawhai: piko ana i a koe ki raro i ahau te hunga e whakatika mai ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:40">18:40</a> Kua meinga e koe kia tahuri mai nga tuara o oku hoariri ki ahau, kia hautopea ai e ahau te hunga e kino ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:41">18:41</a> I karanga ratou, heoi kahore he kaiwhakaora: ki a Ihowa, otira kihai i whakahoki kupu ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:42">18:42</a> Na ka tukia ratou e ahau a rite noa ratou ki te puehu e puhia ana e te hau: akiritia atu ana ratou ki waho, ano he paru no te huarahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:43">18:43</a> Kua whakaorangia ahau e koe i nga ngangautanga a te iwi; kua meinga e koe hei rangatira mo nga tauiwi: hei apa moku te iwi kahore i matauria e ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:44">18:44</a> Kia rongo kau te taringa ki ahau, ka kakama tonu mai ratou ki ahau; ko nga tangata iwi ke ngohe kau ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:45">18:45</a> Ka memeha haere nga tangata iwi ke: ka puta wehi mai hoki i roto i o ratou kuhunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:46">18:46</a> E ora ana a Ihowa; kia whakapaingia hoki toku kamaka, kia whakanuia te Atua o toku whakaoranga:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:47">18:47</a> Ko te Atua, mana nei e rapu he utu moku, mana e pehi nga iwi ki raro i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:48">18:48</a> Mana ahau e mawhiti ai i oku hoariri, ae ra, mau ahau e mea kia teitei ake i te hunga e whakatika mai ana ki ahau; ka whakaorangia ahau e koe i te tangata tutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:49">18:49</a> Mo konei ka whakawhetai ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa, i waenganui i nga tauiwi: ka himene ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:50">18:50</a> He nui nei tana whakaora i tana kingi; e whakaputa aroha ana ki tana tangata i whakawahi ai, ki a Rawiri ratou ko ona uri ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:1">19:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. E korerotia ana e nga rangi te kororia o te Atua; a e whakaaturia ana e te kikorangi te mahi a ona ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:2">19:2</a> E puaki ana te reo o tena rangi, o tena rangi, e whakaatu mohiotanga ana hoki tena po, tena po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:3">19:3</a> Kahore he hamumu, kahore he kupu, kahore e rangona to ratou reo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:4">19:4</a> Kua puta ta ratou aho ki te whenua katoa, a ratou kupu, a te pito ra ano o te ao. Whakaturia ana e ia ki reira te tapenakara mo te ra;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:5">19:5</a> A e puta ana ia me he tane marena hou i tona whare moenga, whakai ana ia, pera ana me te tangata kaha e mea ana ki te oma whakataetae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:6">19:6</a> Ko tona putanga kei tetahi pito o te rangi, a whawhe noa ke tetahi pito: kahore hoki tetahi mea e ngaro i tona mahana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:7">19:7</a> ¶ Tapatahi tonu te ture a Ihowa, he mea whakatahuri i te wairua: pono tonu nga whakaatu a Ihowa, e whakawhaiwhakaaro ana i te kuare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:8">19:8</a> He tika nga ako a Ihowa, e whakahari ana i te ngakau, he ma te whakahau a Ihowa, e whakamarama ana i nga kanohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:9">19:9</a> He ma te wehi ki a Ihowa, pumau tonu ake ake, he pono nga whakaritenga a Ihowa, tika kau ano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:10">19:10</a> Engari ena e hiahiatia ana i te koura, ae, i te tino koura ahakoa maha: reka atu i te honi, i te maturuturutanga iho o nga honikoma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:11">19:11</a> Na ena ano tau pononga i whakatupato; he nui te utu ki te puritia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:12">19:12</a> Ko wai e matau ana ki ona he? Whakamakia oku hara puku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:13">19:13</a> Puritia ano tau pononga kei riro i nga hara whakakake hei rangatira moku: ko reira ahau tu tika ai, a ka watea i te he nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:14">19:14</a> Kia manakohia nga kupu a toku mangai: me nga whakaaro o toku ngakau i tou aroaro, e Ihowa, e toku kamaka, e toku kaihoko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:1">20:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. Ma Ihowa e whakahoki he kupu ki a koe i te ra o te he; ma te ingoa o te Atua o Hakopa koe e tiaki;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:2">20:2</a> Mana e tono mai he awhina mou i te wahi tapu, e whakau hoki koe i Hiona;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:3">20:3</a> Mana e mahara ki au whakahere katoa, e manako ki au tahunga tinana. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:4">20:4</a> Mana e homai ki a koe ta tou ngakau e mea ai, e whakamana katoa hoki tau e wawata ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:5">20:5</a> Ka hari matou ki tau whakaoranga, ka whakatu hoki i o matou kara i runga i te ingoa o to matou Atua: ma Ihowa e whakarite au inoi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:6">20:6</a> ¶ Katahi ahau ka matau e whakaora ana a Ihowa i tana tangata i whakawahi ai, ka whakahoki kupu ia ki a ia i tona rangi tapu, me te kaha ano tona ringa matau ki te whakaora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:7">20:7</a> Ko ta etahi he hariata, ko ta etahi he hoiho: ko tatou ia ka whakahua i te ingoa o Ihowa, o to tatou Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:8">20:8</a> Kua piko ratou, kua hinga: ko tatou ia kua ara, kua tu ki runga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:9">20:9</a> Whakaorangia, e Ihowa: kia whakahoki kupu mai te Kingi ina karanga matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:1">21:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. Ka hari te kingi ki tou kaha, e Ihowa; ano te nui o tona whakamanamana ki tau whakaoranga!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:2">21:2</a> Kua homai e koe ki a ia ta tona ngakau i hiahia ai; kihai ano i kaiponuhia e koe ta ona ngutu i inoi ai. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:3">21:3</a> Kei mua nei hoki koe i a ia e homai ana i nga manaakitanga o te pai; karaunatia ana e koe tona matenga ki te tino koura.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:4">21:4</a> He ora tana i inoi ai i a koe, a kua homai e koe ki a ia, he roa noa atu nga ra ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:5">21:5</a> He nui tona kororia i tau whakaoranga: uhia ana ia e koe ki te honore, ki te kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:6">21:6</a> Nau hoki ia i mea kia manaakitia rawatia ake ake: whakaharitia ana ia e koe ki te koa o tou mata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:7">21:7</a> ¶ E whakawhirinaki ana hoki te kingi ki a Ihowa; e kore ano ia e whakangaueuetia, he atawhai hoki no te Runga Rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:8">21:8</a> Ka mau i tou ringa ou hoariri katoa: ka mau i tou ringa matau te hunga e kino ana ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:9">21:9</a> Ka meinga ratou e koe, kia rite ki te oumu kapura i te wa e riri ai koe: e horomia ratou e Ihowa ina weriweri ia, a ma te kapura ratou e kai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:10">21:10</a> Ka whakamotitia e koe o ratou hua i runga i te whenua, o ratou uri i waenganui o nga tama a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:11">21:11</a> He kino hoki ta ratou i whakatakoto ai mou, he mahi nanakia ta ratou i whakaaro ai, kihai nei i taea e ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:12">21:12</a> Mo reira ka meinga e koe kia tahuri o ratou tuara, ina whakatihaia e koe au pere i runga i au aho ki o ratou mata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:13">21:13</a> Kia whakanuia koe, e Ihowa, i runga i tou kaha: ka waiata matou, ka himene ki tou nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:1">22:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Airete Hahara. He himene na Rawiri. E toku Atua, e toku Atua, he aha koe i whakarere ai i ahau? he aha koe i matara atu ai ki te whakaora i ahau i nga kupu hoki o taku hamama?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:2">22:2</a> E toku Atua, e karanga nei ahau i te awatea, heoi kahore koe e rongo, i te po ano kahore ahau e wahangu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:3">22:3</a> Otiia he tapu koe, kei nga whakamoemiti a Iharaira tou nohoanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:4">22:4</a> I whakawhirinaki o matou matua ki a koe, i whakawhirinaki, a whakaorangia ana e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:5">22:5</a> I karanga ratou ki a koe, a kua ora; i whakawhirinaki ki a koe, a kihai i whakama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:6">22:6</a> Ko ahau ia he toke, ehara i te tangata: e tawaia ana e te tangata, e whakahaweatia ana e te iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:7">22:7</a> Kataina iho ahau e te hunga katoa e kite ana i ahau, ko ana o ratou ngutu, ruru ana o ratou matenga, e ki mai ana,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:8">22:8</a> Tukua atu koe ki a Ihowa, mana ia e whakaora: mana ia e whakaora, e pai ana hoki ia ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:9">22:9</a> Nau ia ahau i whakawhanau mai i roto i te kopu, i mea hoki kia tumanako, i ahau i nga u o toku whaea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:10">22:10</a> He mea whakarere atu ahau ki runga ki a koe no te kopu mai; ko koe toku Atua no te kopu mai ano o toku whaea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:11">22:11</a> ¶ Kei mamao atu i ahau, e tata ana hoki te he, kahore hoki he kaiawhina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:12">22:12</a> He tini nga puru e karapoti nei i ahau: e whakapaea ana ahau e nga mea kaha o Pahana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:13">22:13</a> E hamama ana o ratou mangai ki ahau, ano he raiona e haehae ana, e hamama ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:14">22:14</a> Kua ringihia ahau, ano he wai, kua takoki katoa oku iwi; me te ware pi toku ngakau, e rewa ana i waenganui i oku whekau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:15">22:15</a> Kua maroke toku kaha, ano he maramara rihi, piri tonu toku arero ki oku kauae; kua whakatakotoria ano ahau e koe ki te puehu o te mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:16">22:16</a> Kua karapotia nei hoki ahau e te kirehe, kua muia e te whakaminenga o nga tangata hara: kua pokaia e ratou oku ringa me oku waewae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:17">22:17</a> E taea e ahau te tatau oku iwi katoa: e titiro mai ana ratou, e matakitaki ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:18">22:18</a> E wehewehea ana oku kakahu mo ratou, e maka rota ana mo toku weruweru.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:19">22:19</a> Kaua ra ia koe e matara atu, e Ihowa; e toku kaha, hohoro mai hei awhina moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:20">22:20</a> Whakaorangia toku wairua i te hoari, taku hoki e matenui nei i te kuri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:21">22:21</a> Whakaorangia ahau i te mangai o te raiona: ae, i nga haona o nga kau maka kua whakahokia mai e koe he kupu ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:22">22:22</a> ¶ Ka korerotia e ahau tou ingoa ki oku teina, ka whakamoemititia koe e ahau i waenganui i te whakaminenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:23">22:23</a> E te hunga e wehi ana ki a Ihowa, whakamoemiti ki a ia; whakakororiatia ia, e te uri katoa o Hakopa, kia wehi hoki ki a ia, e te uri katoa o Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:24">22:24</a> Kihai hoki ia i whakahawea, kihai i whakarihariha ki te aue o te ngakau mamae; kihai ano i huna i tona mata ki a ia, engari i tana karangatanga ki a ia i whakarongo ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:25">22:25</a> Ko koe taku e whakamoemiti ai i waenganui o te whakaminenga nui, ka whakamana e ahau aku kupu taurangi ki te aroaro o te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:26">22:26</a> Ka kai te hunga mahaki, a ka makona: ka whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa te hunga e rapu ana ki a ia; kia ora tonu o koutou ngakau, ake, ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:27">22:27</a> E mahara nga pito katoa o te whenua, a ka tahuri ki a Ihowa: ka koropiko ano nga hapu katoa o nga iwi ki tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:28">22:28</a> No Ihowa hokite rangatiratanga, ko ia ano te kawana i waenganui o nga iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:29">22:29</a> Ka kai, a ka koropiko nga tangata tetere katoa o te whenua: ka tuohu ki tona aroaro te hunga katoa e heke ana ki te puehu; tae no ki te tangata kahore e ora i a ia tona wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:30">22:30</a> Tera e mahi tetahi uri ki a ia; ka waiho ki te Ariki hei whakatupuranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:31">22:31</a> E haere mai ratou, e kauwhau i tona tika ki te iwi e whanau a mua, he meatanga tenei nana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:1">23:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. Ko Ihowa toku hepara; e kore ahau e hapa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:2">23:2</a> Ko ia hei mea kia takoto ahau ki nga wahi tarutaru hou: e arahi ana ia i ahau ki te taha o nga wai ata rere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:3">23:3</a> Ko ia hei whakahoki ake i toku wairua: e arahi ana ia i ahau i nga ara o te tika, he whakaaro ki tona ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:4">23:4</a> Ae, ahakoa haere ahau i te awaawa o te atarangi o te mate, kahore he kino e wehi ai ahau: no te mea kei toku taha koe; ko tau rakau, ko tau tokotoko, ko ena hei oranga ngakau moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:5">23:5</a> E taka ana e koe he tepu ki toku aroaro i te tirohanga a oku hoariri, e whakawahia ana e koe toku matenga ki te hinu, purena tonu taku kapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:6">23:6</a> He pono e aru i ahau te pai me te atawhai i nga ra katoa e ora ai ahau, a ka noho ahau ki te whare o Ihowa ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:1">24:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. No Ihowa te whenua, me ona tini mea, te ao, me nga tangata e noho ana i runga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:2">24:2</a> He mea whakatu hoki nana ki runga ki nga moana, he mea whakau ki runga ki nga roma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:3">24:3</a> ¶ Ko wai e eke ki te maunga o Ihowa? Ko wai e tu ki tona wahi tapu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:4">24:4</a> Ko te tangata he ma nei nga ringa, he harakore tona ngakau, kahore nei i ara tona wairua ki te horihori, a kahore i oati teka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:5">24:5</a> Ka riro i a ia te manaaki a Ihowa, me te tika a te Atua o tona whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:6">24:6</a> Ko te whakatupuranga tenei o te hunga e rapu ana ki a ia, e rapu nei i tou mate, e Hakopa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:7">24:7</a> ¶ Kia ara o koutou matenga, e nga tatau, ara ake, e nga tatau onamata; a ka tomo te Kingi o te kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:8">24:8</a> Ko wai tenei Kingi kororia? Ko Ihowa, ko te kaha, ko te marohirohi, ko Ihowa, ko te marohirohi ki te whawhai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:9">24:9</a> Kia ara o koutou matenga, e nga tatau, kia ara ake, e nga tatau onamata, a ka tomo te Kingi o te kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:10">24:10</a> Ko wai tenei Kingi kororia? Ko Ihowa o nga mano, ko ia te Kingi kororia. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:1">25:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. Ka ara nei toku wairua ki a koe, e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:2">25:2</a> E toku Atua, ko koe toku whakawhirinakitanga: kei whakama ahau, aua oku hoariri e tukua kia whakaputa ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:3">25:3</a> Ae, aua tetahi o te hunga e tatari ana ki a koe e tukua kia whakama: kia whakama te hunga e tinihanga noa ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:4">25:4</a> Whakakitea ki ahau au ara, e Ihowa; whakaakona ahau ki au huarahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:5">25:5</a> Arahina ahau i tou pono, whakaakona hoki ahau: ko koe hoki te Atua o toku whakaoranga; pau noa te ra i ahau e tatari nei ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:6">25:6</a> E Ihowa, kia mahara ki au mahi tohu, ki au mahi aroha; nonamata riro hoki ena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:7">25:7</a> Kaua e maharatia nga hara o toku tamarikitanga, me oku kino: mahara mai koe ki ahau, e Ihowa, kia rite ki tau mahi tohu, kia whakaaro ki tou pai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:8">25:8</a> ¶ He pai, he tika a Ihowa, a ka whakaakona e ia te hunga hara ki te huarahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:9">25:9</a> Ka arahina e ia te hunga mahaki i runga i te whakawa: ka akona hoki e ia te hunga mahaki ki tana ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:10">25:10</a> He mahi tohu, he pono nga ara katoa o Ihowa ki te hunga e pupuri ana i tana kawenata, i ana whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:11">25:11</a> Kia mahara ki tou ingoa, e Ihowa, a murua toku kino, he nui nei hoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:12">25:12</a> Ko wai te tangata e wehi ana ki a Ihowa? Ka whakaako ia i a ia ki te ara e pai ai ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:13">25:13</a> Ka noho tona wairua i runga i te pai, a ka riro te whenua i tona uri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:14">25:14</a> Kei te hunga e wehi ana i a ia te mea ngaro a Ihowa; a mana e whakakite ki a ratou tana kawenata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:15">25:15</a> ¶ E tau tonu ana oku kanohi ki a Ihowa; mana hoki e unu ake oku waewae i te kupenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:16">25:16</a> Tahuri mai ki ahau, tohungia hoki ahau; he mokemoke hoki ahau, e mamae ana te ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:17">25:17</a> Kua whakanuia nga whakapawera o toku ngakau: whakaputaina ahau i roto i nga mea e pehi nei i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:18">25:18</a> Tirohia toku mate me toku mamae, a murua katoatia oku hara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:19">25:19</a> Tirohia mai oku hoariri, he tokomaha hoki ratou: a he nanakia te kino e kino nei ratou ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:20">25:20</a> Tiakina toku wairua, a whakaorangia ahau: kei whakama ahau; e whakawhirinaki ana hoki ahau ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:21">25:21</a> Tukua ma te ngakau tapatahi, ma te tika ahau e tiaki; e tumanako ana hoki ahau ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:22">25:22</a> Hokona, e te Atua, a Iharaira i roto i ona whakapawera katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:1">26:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. Whakawakia ahau, e Ihowa, kua haere nei hoki ahau i te tapatahitanga o toku ngakau: kua whakawhirinaki ano ki a Ihowa, na, e kore e paheke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:2">26:2</a> Tirohia iho ahau, e Ihowa, whakamatauria ahau, kia kitea oku whatumanawa me toku ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:3">26:3</a> Kei mua hoki tou atawhai i oku kanohi; kua haere nei ahau i tou pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:4">26:4</a> Kahore ahau i noho tahi ki nga tangata horihori; e kore ano ahau e tomo tahi me nga tangata tinihanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:5">26:5</a> Kino tonu ahau ki te whakaminenga o nga kaimahi i te he, e kore ano ahau e noho tahi ki te hunga kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:6">26:6</a> ¶ Ka horoia e ahau oku ringa ki te harakore, ka taiawhio ai i tau aata, e Ihowa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:7">26:7</a> A ka rangona toku reo e whakamoemiti ana, e whakapuaki ana i au mahi whakamiharo katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:8">26:8</a> E Ihowa, kua aroha nei ahau ki tou whare nohoanga, ki te wahi e nohoia ana e tou kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:9">26:9</a> Kei huia toku wairua ki roto ki te hunga hara, me toku ora ki roto ki te hunga toto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:10">26:10</a> He mahi nanakia hoki ta o ratou ringa; ki tonu o ratou matau i te utu whakapati.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:11">26:11</a> Ko ahau ia, ka haere i runga i toku tapatahi: hokona ahau, tohungia hoki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:12">26:12</a> E tu ana toku waewae i te wahi tika: ka whakapaingia a Ihowa e ahau i roto i nga whakaminenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:1">27:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. Ko Ihowa toku marama, toku whakaoranga; kia wehi ahau i a wai? Ko Ihowa te kaha o toku ora; ko wai e mataku ai ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:2">27:2</a> I te whakatatanga mai o te hunga kino, o oku hoariri, o oku hoa whainga, ki te kai i oku kikokiko, tutuki ana ratou, hinga ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:3">27:3</a> Ahakoa whakapae noa te ope i ahau e kore toku ngakau e wehi: ahakoa ara noa te pakanga ki ahau, ka au tonu ia ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:4">27:4</a> Kotahi taku mea i inoi ai i a Ihowa, ko taku tena e rapu ai: kia noho i te whare o Ihowa i nga ra katoa e ora ai ahau, kia kite ai i te ataahua o Ihowa, kia ui ai i roto i tona temepara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:5">27:5</a> Ka huna hoki ahau e ia ki tona teneti i te ra o te he, ka huna ki te wahi ngaro i tona tapenakara, ka hapainga ahau ki runga ki te kohatu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:6">27:6</a> Na, aianei ka teitei toku mahunga ki runga ake i oku hoariri, e karapoti nei i ahau; a ka patua e ahau i roto i tona tapenakara he whakahere hari; ka waiata ahau, ae ka himene ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:7">27:7</a> ¶ Whakarongo mai ki toku reo, e Ihowa, ua karanga ahau, tohungia ahau, whakahokia mai hoki he kupu ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:8">27:8</a> I a koe i mea, Rapua e koutou toku mata; ka mea toku ngakau ki a koe, ka rapu ahau i tou mata, e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:9">27:9</a> Kaua tou mata e huna ki ahau, kaua tau pononga e peia atu ua riri koe: ko koe toku kaiawhina, kei mahue ahau i a koe, kei whakarerea e koe e te Atua o toku whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:10">27:10</a> Ki te whakarerea ahau e toku papa, e toku whaea, ko Ihowa hei tukunga atu moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:11">27:11</a> E Ihowa, whakaakona ahau ki tau ara; arahina ahau i te ara tika, he hoariri hoki oku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:12">27:12</a> Kaua ahau e tukua ki te hiahia o oku hoariri; kua whakatika mai hoki ki ahau he kaiwhakapae teka, me te hunga manawa nanakia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:13">27:13</a> Kua ngohe ahau, me i kaua ahau i whakapono, tera ahau e kite i te pai o te Atua i te whenua o te ora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:14">27:14</a> Taria a Ihowa: kia maia, a kia kaha tou ngakau; ina, taria a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:1">28:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. Ka karanga ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa, e toku kohatu, kaua e wahangu ki ahau; ki te wahangu hoki koe ki ahau, ka rite ahau ki te hunga e heke atu ana ki te poka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:2">28:2</a> Whakarongo ki toku reo inoi, ua karanga ahau ki a koe, ina totoro oku ringa ki tou ahurewa tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:3">28:3</a> Kaua ahau e kumea tahitia me te hunga he; me nga kaimahi i te kino, he marie a ratou kupu ki o ratou hoa, he kino ia kei roto i o ratou ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:4">28:4</a> Kia rite ki a ratou mahi tau e hoatu ai ki a ratou, ki te kino ano o a ratou hanga: kia rite ki nga mahi a o ratou ringa tau e hoatu ai ki a ratou, whakahokia ta ratou utu ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:5">28:5</a> Na kahore nei ratou e whakaaro ki nga mahi a Ihowa, ki nga meatanga a ona ringa, mo reira ka whakahoroa iho ratou e ia, e kore ano e whakaturia ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:6">28:6</a> ¶ Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa mona i whakarongo mai ki toku reo inoi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:7">28:7</a> Ko Ihowa toku kaha, toku whakangungu rakau; i whakawhirinaki toku ngakau ki a ia, a awhinatia ana ahau; koia i hari ai toku ngakau, i whakamoemiti ai hoki taku waiata ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:8">28:8</a> Ko Ihowa to ratou kaha, ko ia ano te kaha whakaora o tana tangata i whakawahi ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:9">28:9</a> Whakaorangia tau iwi, manaakitia tou kainga tupu: whangainga ratou, whakaarahia ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:1">29:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. Hoatu ki a Ihowa, e nga tama a te hunga nunui, hoatu ki a Ihowa te kororia me te kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:2">29:2</a> Hoatu ki a Ihowa te kororia e rite ana mo tona ingoa, koropiko ki a Ihowa i roto i te ataahua o te tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:3">29:3</a> Kei runga te reo o Ihowa i nga wai: e papa ana te whatitiri a te Atua o te kororia: kei runga a Ihowa i nga wai maha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:4">29:4</a> Kaha tonu te reo o Ihowa; kororia tonu te reo o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:5">29:5</a> Mongamonga noa nga hita i te reo o Ihowa; ina, mongamonga noa i a Ihowa nga hita o Repanona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:6">29:6</a> Ko ia hei mea i a ratou kia mokowhiti, ano he kuao: a Repanona raua ko Hiriona, ano he kuao kau maka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:7">29:7</a> E wehewehe ana te reo o Ihowa i nga mura ahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:8">29:8</a> Wiri ana te koraha i te reo o Ihowa: wiri ana i a Ihowa te koraha o Karehe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:9">29:9</a> Whanau ana nga hata i te reo o Ihowa, tihorea ana nga ngahere kia tahanga: i tona temepara ko te kupu a te katoa, Kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:10">29:10</a> I noho a Ihowa hei kingi i runga i te Waipuke; ae, ka noho a Ihowa hei kingi, ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:11">29:11</a> Ka homai e Ihowa he kaha ki tana hunga; he rongo mau ta Ihowa manaaki mo tana hunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:1">30:1</a> ¶ He hemene, he waiata mo te tainga o te kawa o te whare. Na Rawiri. Ka whakanui ahau i a koe, e Ihowa; nau hoki ahau i hapai ake, a kihai i tukua oku hoariri kia hari ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:2">30:2</a> E Ihowa, e toku Atua, i karanga ahau ki a koe, a kore ake toku mate i a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:3">30:3</a> E Ihowa, nau i whakaputa ake toku wairua i te reinga; nau ahau i whakaora kei heke ki te poka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:4">30:4</a> Himene ki a Ihowa, e tana hunga tapu, whakawhetai hoki ki tona ingoa tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:5">30:5</a> He iti hoki te wahi e riri ai ia; he oranga ki te manakohia e ia: e tau iho te tangi i te ahiahi, a i te ata he hari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:6">30:6</a> ¶ I mea ahau i toku wa i kake ai, E kore ahau e whakangaueuetia a muri ake nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:7">30:7</a> He manakohanga nau, e Ihowa, i u ai i a koe te tu o toku maunga; i huna e koe tou mata a raru iho ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:8">30:8</a> E Ihowa, i karanga ahau ki a koe, i inoi hoki ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:9">30:9</a> He aha te pai o oku toto ina heke ahau ki te poka? Ma te puehu koia koe e whakamoemiti? mana oti e whakapuaki tou pono?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:10">30:10</a> Whakarongo, e Ihowa, tohungia hoki ahau: e Ihowa, ko koe hei awhina moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:11">30:11</a> Kua puta ke i a koe taku tangi hei kanikani: kua wewete i toku kakahu taratara, a whitikiria ana ahau e koe ki te koa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:12">30:12</a> Hei mea e himene ai toku kororia ki a koe, kore ake e wahangu. E Ihowa, e toku Atua, ka whakawhetai ahau ki a koe ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:1">31:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, ko koe taku e whakawhirinaki nei; kei whakama ahau ake ake: whakaorangia ahau, he tika nei hoki koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:2">31:2</a> Anga mai tou taringa ki ahau; hohoro te whakaora i ahau: kia ai koe hei kohatu kaha moku, hei whare tiaki moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:3">31:3</a> Ko koe hoki toku kohatu, toku pa: na kia mahara ki tou ingoa, a arahina ahau, tohutohungia hoki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:4">31:4</a> Kapohia ahau i roto i te kupenga i huna e ratou moku; ko koe hoki toku kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:5">31:5</a> Tenei toku wairua te tukua atu nei e ahau ki tou ringa; nau ahau i hoki e Ihowa, e te Atua o te pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:6">31:6</a> E kino ana ahau ki te hunga e whakaaro ana ki nga mea tekateka noa; e whakawhirinaki ana hoki ahau ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:7">31:7</a> Ka whakamanamana ahau, ka hari ki tou atawhai; mou i titiro ki taku tangi; i matau hoki ki toku wairua i nga wa o te he;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:8">31:8</a> Kahore ahau i kopia e koe ki roto ki te ringa o te hoariri: kua whakaturia e koe oku waewae ki te wahi nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:9">31:9</a> ¶ Tohungia ahau, e Ihowa, kei te he hoki ahau, pakoko kau toku mata i te pouri, toku wairua me toku kopu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:10">31:10</a> Ka hemo nei hoki toku ora i te tangi, me oku tau i te aue; poto iho toku kaha i toku he, kurupopo ana oku iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:11">31:11</a> He tawainga ahau na oku hoariri katoa; ko te tino mahi ia tena a oku hoa noho tata, he mea wehi ahau na nga tangata i mohio ki ahau: ko te hunga i kite i ahau i waho, rere ana i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:12">31:12</a> Kua warewaretia ahau me te tupapaku kua ngaro atu i te ngakau; kua rite ki te oko pakaru.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:13">31:13</a> I rongo hoki ahau i te ngautuara a te tini; i karapotia ahau e te wehi: i a ratou e runanga ana ki te he moku, i mea kia whakamatea ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:14">31:14</a> Ko ahau ia i whakawhirinaki ki a koe, e Ihowa: i mea, Ko koe toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:15">31:15</a> Kei tou ringa oku taima, whakaorangia ahau i nga ringa o oku hoariri, i te hunga e tukino ana i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:16">31:16</a> Kia whiti tou mata ki tau pononga; whakaorangia ahau, he mahi tohu hoki tau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:17">31:17</a> Kei whakama ahau, e Ihowa; kua karanga hoki ahau ki a koe: kia whakama te hunga kino, kia takoto puku i te reinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:18">31:18</a> Whakamutua te korero a nga ngutu teka, he kino nei a ratou korero mo te tangata tika, na to ratou whakapehapeha hoki, na to ratou whakahihi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:19">31:19</a> ¶ Ano te nui o tau pai kua rongoatia nei e koe mo te hunga e wehi ana ki a koe; i mahia nei e koe mo te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a koe i te aroaro o nga tama a te tangata!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:20">31:20</a> Ka huna ratou e koe ki te wahi ngaro i tou aroaro i nga rauhanga a te tangata; ka huna ratou e koe ki roto ki te teneti, kei taea e te ngangau a nga arero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:21">31:21</a> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, mona i mea kia miharotia tana mahi tohu ki ahau i te pa kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:22">31:22</a> I ki hoki ahau i toku potatutatunga, Kua motuhia mai ahau i mua i ou kanohi: ahakoa ra i rongo koe ki toku reo inoi i taku karangatanga ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:23">31:23</a> Arohaina a Ihowa, e tana hunga tapu katoa: e tiakina ana e Ihowa te hunga pono, a he nui tana utu ki te kaimahi whakapehapeha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:24">31:24</a> Kia maia, kia kaha o koutou ngakau, e te hunga katoa e tumanako ana ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:1">32:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri: he Makiri. Ka hari te tangata kua oti tana he te muru, tona hara te hipoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:2">32:2</a> Ka hari te tangata kahore nei e whakairia e Ihowa he hara ki a ia, a kahore he hianga i tona wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:3">32:3</a> I ahau kihai i kuihi, ngahengahe kau oku iwi i taku auetanga i te ra roa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:4">32:4</a> No tou ringa i taimaha ki ahau i te ao, i te po; kua whakaputaina ketia toku makukuranga, ano na te maroketanga o te raumati. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:5">32:5</a> I whakina e ahau toku hara ki a koe, kihai hoki i huna i toku kino: i mea ahau, Ka whakina aku mahi tutu ki a Ihowa; a murua ana e koe te kino o toku hara. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:6">32:6</a> Mo konei ka inoi ki a koe nga tangata tapu katoa i te wa e kitea ai koe: he pono ka ngawha nga wai nui, e kore e tata ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:7">32:7</a> ¶ Ko koe toku piringa; mau ahau e whakaora i te pouri, mau ahau e karapoti ki nga waiata whakaora. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:8">32:8</a> Ka tohutohungia koe e ahau, ka whakaakona koe ki te ara e haere ai koe; ma toku kanohi koe e arahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:9">32:9</a> Kei rite koutou ki te hoiho, ki te muera ranei, kahore nei he matauranga; he mea kuku nei o raua kauae ki te paraire, ki te moka hei pupuri mai; ki te kore hoki, e kore e tata ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:10">32:10</a> He tini nga mea whakapouri mo te tangata hara: ko te tangata ia e whakawhirinaki ana ki a Ihowa, ka karapotia e te atawhai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:11">32:11</a> Kia koa ki a Ihowa, whakamanamana, e te hunga tika: kia hari, hamama, e te hunga ngakau tika katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:1">33:1</a> ¶ Kia hari ki a Ihowa, e te hunga tika: he mea ataahua te whakamoemiti ma te hunga kore he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:2">33:2</a> Whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa i runga i te hapa; himene ki a ia i runga i te hatere kotahi tekau nei nga aho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:3">33:3</a> Waiatatia ki a ia he waiata hou: kia tika te whakatangi, kia nui te reo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:4">33:4</a> No te mea he tika te kupu a Ihowa, a kei runga i te pono ana mahi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:5">33:5</a> E paingia ana e ia te tika me te whakawa: ki tonu te whenua i te atawhai a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:6">33:6</a> Na te kupu a Ihowa nga rangi i hanga; ko nga mano katoa hoki o reira na te ha o tona mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:7">33:7</a> He mea huihui e ia nga wai o te moana, ano he puranga; he mea whawhao e ia te rire ki nga pakoro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:8">33:8</a> Kia wehi te whenua katoa ki a Ihowa; kia ohooho nga tangata katoa o te ao ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:9">33:9</a> I ki hoki ia, a kua oti: i whakahau, a tu tonu iho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:10">33:10</a> E whakataka ana e Ihowa te whakaaro o nga tauiwi: e whakakahoretia ana e ia nga meatanga a nga iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:11">33:11</a> Ko te whakaaro o Ihowa, tu tonu ake ake; ko nga meatanga a tona ngakau kei tena whakatupuranga, kei tena whakatupuranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:12">33:12</a> ¶ Ka hari te iwi no ratou nei Atua a Ihowa, te iwi kua whiriwhiria e ia hei taonga tupu mona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:13">33:13</a> E titiro iho ana a Ihowa i te rangi: e kite ana ia i nga tama katoa a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:14">33:14</a> Kei tona wahi nohoanga ia e matakitaki iho ana ki nga tangata katoa o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:15">33:15</a> Nana i hanga nga ngakau o ratou katoa, e mohiotia ana e ia a ratou mahi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:16">33:16</a> E kore tetahi kingi e ora i te nui o te ope, e kore e ora te marohirohi i te nui o te kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:17">33:17</a> He mea teka te hoiho hei whakaora; ehara ano tona kaha nui i te mea e mawhiti ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:18">33:18</a> Nana, kei runga i te hunga e wehi ana i a ia te kanohi o Ihowa, kei te hunga e tumanako ana ki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:19">33:19</a> Hei whakaora i o ratou wairua kei mate, hei mea i a ratou kia ora i te wa o te hemokai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:20">33:20</a> Kua tatari nei o tatou wairua ki a Ihowa; ko ia to tatou kaiawhina, to tatou whakangungu rakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:21">33:21</a> Hari tonu to tatou ngakau ki a ia; no tatou hoki i whakawhirinaki ki tona ingoa tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:22">33:22</a> E Ihowa, hei runga i a matou tau mahi tohu; kia rite hoki ki ta matou tumanako ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:1">34:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri, i tona ahua i rere ke ra i te aroaro o Apimereke; na pei ana ia, a haere ana. Ka whakapaingia e ahau a Ihowa i nga wa katoa; he whakamoemiti tonu ta toku mangai ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:2">34:2</a> Ka whakamanamana toku wairua ki a Ihowa: ka rongo te hunga mahaki, a ka hari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:3">34:3</a> Kia whakanui tahi tatou i a Ihowa, kia whakateitei tahi hoki i tona ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:4">34:4</a> I rapu ahau i a Ihowa, a rongo mai ana ia ki ahau, whakaorangia ana ahau e ia i oku wehi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:5">34:5</a> I titiro ratou ki a ia, a kua marama: a kahore rawa he whakama o o ratou mata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:6">34:6</a> I karanga tenei tangata iti, a whakarongo ana a Ihowa, whakaora ana i a ia i ona whakapawera katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:7">34:7</a> E noho ana te anahera a Ihowa i tetahi taha, i tetahi taha, o te hunga e wehi ana i a ia, a e whakaora ana i a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:8">34:8</a> Whakamatauria, kia kite ai koutou i te pai o Ihowa: ka hari te tangata e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:9">34:9</a> Kia wehi ki a Ihowa, e tona hunga tapu: e kore hoki e hapa nga tangata e wehi ana i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:10">34:10</a> E hapa ana nga kuao raiona, e mate ana i te kai: ko te hunga ia e rapu ana ki a Ihowa, e kore e hapa i tetahi mea pai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:11">34:11</a> ¶ Haere mai, e nga tamariki, whakarongo ki ahau: maku koutou e ako kia wehi ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:12">34:12</a> Ko wai te tangata e hiahia ana ki te ora, e whai ana kia maha nga ra, kia kite i te pai?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:13">34:13</a> Tiakina tou arero kei kino, ou ngutu kei korero hianga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:14">34:14</a> Mawehe atu i te kino, mahia te pai; rapua te ata noho, whaia hoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:15">34:15</a> E tau ana nga kanohi o Ihowa ki te hunga tika; me ona taringa ki ta ratou karanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:16">34:16</a> E he ana te mata o Ihowa ki nga kaimahi i te kino, hei hatepe i a ratou i te whenua kei maharatia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:17">34:17</a> I karanga te hunga tika, a i whakarongo a Ihowa, whakaorangia ana ratou e ia i o ratou whakapawera katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:18">34:18</a> E tata ana a Ihowa ki te hunga ngakau maru: ka whakaorangia ano e ia te hunga wairua iro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:19">34:19</a> He tini nga mate o te tangata tika: otiia e whakaorangia ana ia e Ihowa i roto i era katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:20">34:20</a> E tiakina ana e ia ona wheua katoa: e kore tetahi e whati.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:21">34:21</a> Ka mate i te kino te tangata hara; a ka he te hunga e kino ana ki te tangata tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:22">34:22</a> E hokona ana e Ihowa te wairua o ana pononga, e kore ano e he tetahi o te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:1">35:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. E ngana, e Ihowa, ki te hunga e tohe ana ki ahau: whawhaitia te hunga e whawhai nei ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:2">35:2</a> Kia mau ki te whakangungu rakau, ki te puapua; whakatika hei awhina moku</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:3">35:3</a> Unuhia te tao, araia te ara o te hunga e whai nei i ahau: ki mai ki toku wairua, Ko ahau tou whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:4">35:4</a> Kia whakama, kia numinumi te hunga e whai ana kia whakamatea ahau: kia whakahokia ki muri, kia whakapoauautia te hunga e whakatakoto ana i te kino moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:5">35:5</a> Kia rite ratou ki te papapa e puhia ana e te hau; kia aia haeretia e te anahera a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:6">35:6</a> Kia pouri to ratou ara, kia pahekeheke: kia whaia ratou e te anahera a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:7">35:7</a> Kahore hoki he rawa i huna ai e ratou te poka o ta ratou kupenga moku; he mea keri takekore kia mate ai ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:8">35:8</a> Kia rokohanga poauautia ia e te ngaromanga; kia mau ano ko ia i tana kupenga i huna ai: kia taka ia ki taua tino ngaromanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:9">35:9</a> A ka koa toku wairua ki a Ihowa, ka hari ki tana whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:10">35:10</a> Ka ki katoa oku wheua, E Ihowa, ko wai te rite mou, mo te kaiwhakaora o te iti i te tangata e kaha ake ana i a ia, ae o te iti, o te rawakore i tona kaipahua?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:11">35:11</a> ¶ Whakatika ana nga kaiwhakapae teka: whakawakia ana ahau mo nga mea kihai nei ahau i matau atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:12">35:12</a> Utua ana e ratou taku pai ki te kino, a whakatupu pani ana toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:13">35:13</a> Tena ko ahau, i a ratou e mate ana, he kahu taratara toku, waikauwere ana toku wairua, kihai i kai: a hoki mai ana taku inoi ki toku uma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:14">35:14</a> Ko toku ahua me te mea he hoa ia, he teina noku: kupapa noa iho ahau, ano he tangata e tangi ana ki tona whaea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:15">35:15</a> I toku paheketanga ia koa ana ratou, huihui ana; huihui ana nga tangata kino noa iho hei hoariri moku, kihai ano ahau i mohio; haehae ana ratou i ahau, kihai hoki i mutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:16">35:16</a> Rite tonu ki nga kaiwhakakata o nga hakari, tetea ana o ratou niho ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:17">35:17</a> ¶ E te Ariki, kia pehea te roa o tau titiro kau mai? Whakaorangia toku wairua i a ratou whakangaromanga, taku e aroha nei, i nga raiona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:18">35:18</a> Ka whakawhetai ahau ki a koe i roto i te whakaminenga nui, ka whakamoemiti ki a koe i roto i te iwi maha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:19">35:19</a> Kei hari pokanoa ki ahau oku hoariri; kei whakakini te kanohi o te hunga e kino noa ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:20">35:20</a> Ehara hoki ta ratou i te korero mo te rangimarie; heoi kei te whakatakoto kupu tinihanga ratou mo te hunga ata noho o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:21">35:21</a> Ina, hamama ana o ratou mangai ki ahau, e ki ana, Ha, ha, kua kite to matou kanohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:22">35:22</a> Kua kite koe, e Ihowa: kaua ra e wahangu; e te Ariki, kei matara i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:23">35:23</a> Oho ake, e ara ki te whakarite i toku whakawa, ki taku tautohe, e toku Atua, e toku Ariki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:24">35:24</a> Kia rite ki tou tika te whakarite moku, e Ihowa, e toku Atua: kei koa ano ratou ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:25">35:25</a> Kei mea ratou i roto i o ratou ngakau, Ha, ko ta matou tena i pai ai: kei mea ratou, Kua horomia ia e tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:26">35:26</a> Kia whakama, kia numinumi ngatahi, te hunga e koa ana ina he ahau: kia whakakakahuria ki te whakama, ki te numinumi, te hunga e whakakake ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:27">35:27</a> Kia hamama i te hari, kia koa te hunga e pai ana ki taku mahi tika: ae, kia mea tonu, kia whakanuia a Ihowa e whakapai nei ki te ora o tana pononga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:28">35:28</a> A ka korerotia e toku arero tau mahi tika, me te whakamoemiti ki a koe i te ra roa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:1">36:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Na te pononga a Ihowa, na Rawiri. E mea ana te mahi kino a te tangata hara i roto i toku ngakau, Kahore he wehi ki te Atua i mua i ona kanohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:2">36:2</a> E whakapai ana hoki ona kanohi ake ki a ia ano, e kore e kitea tona hara, e kore e kinongia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:3">36:3</a> He kino nga kupu a tona mangai he rauhanga hoki, kua mahue i a ia te mahara, te mahi i te pai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:4">36:4</a> He mahi nanakia tana e whakaaro ai i runga i tona moenga; ehara i te pai te ara e turia ana e ia, kahore ona whakarihariha ki te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:5">36:5</a> ¶ Kei nga rangi, e Ihowa, tau mahi tohu: tutuki noa atu tou pono ki nga kapua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:6">36:6</a> Rite tonu tou tika ki nga maunga o te Atua; he rire nui au whakaritenga: ko koe, e Ihowa, te kaiwhakaora i te tangata, i te kararehe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:7">36:7</a> Ano te pai o tou aroha, e te Atua: ka okioki nga tama a te tangata i raro i te taumarumarutanga iho o ou pakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:8">36:8</a> Ka makona ratou i nga mea momona o tou whare: ka whakainumia ano e koe ki te awa o au mea whakahari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:9">36:9</a> Kei a koe hoki te puna o te ora; ma tou marama ka kite ai matou i te marama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:10">36:10</a> Kia roa tou aroha ki te hunga e matau ana ki a koe, tou tika hoki ki te hunga ngakau tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:11">36:11</a> Kei puta mai ki ahau te waewae whakapakari; kei aia atu ahau e te ringa o te hunga hara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:12">36:12</a> Hinga iho i reira nga kaimahi i te kino: kua turakina iho, te ahei te ara ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:1">37:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. Kaua e mamae ki te hunga kino, kaua e hae ki nga kaimahi i te he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:2">37:2</a> No te mea ka hohoro ratou te kotia, te peratia me te tarutaru, a ka memenga me he otaota hou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:3">37:3</a> Whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa, mahia te pai; e noho ki te whenua, a e aru i muri i te pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:4">37:4</a> Whakaahuareka ki a Ihowa, a ka homai e ia ki a koe ta tou ngakau i hiahia ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:5">37:5</a> Tukua tou ara ki a Ihowa; whakawhirinaki hoki ki a ia, a mana e mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:6">37:6</a> Mana hoki e whakaputa tou tika, ano he marama, ou ritenga me te mea ko te ra e tu ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:7">37:7</a> ¶ Okioki ki a Ihowa, tatari marie ki a ia: kei mamae ki te tangata e tere ana i tona ara, ki te tangata e taea ana e ia nga whakaaro kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:8">37:8</a> Kati te riri, whakarerea hoki te arita; kei mamae koe, kei takina kia mahi i te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:9">37:9</a> No te mea ka hatepea atu te hunga kino: ko te hunga ia e tatari ana ki a Ihowa, ka riro i a ratou te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:10">37:10</a> Kia potopoto ake nei hoki, a ka kore noa iho te hunga kino: ae ra, ka ata tirohia e koe tona wahi, a kore kau noa iho ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:11">37:11</a> Na ka riro te whenua i te hunga mahaki; a ka hari ratou i te roa o te ata noho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:12">37:12</a> E whakangarahu ana te tangata kino mo te tangata tika: pakiri ana ona niho ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:13">37:13</a> Ka kata te Ariki ki a ia, no te mea ka kite ia e tata ana tona ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:14">37:14</a> Kua unuhia te hoari e te hunga kino, kua piko ta ratou kopere, hei turaki i te ware, i te rawakore, hei kohuru i te hunga e tika ana, i te ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:15">37:15</a> Ka tapoko ta ratou hoari ki o ratou ngakau: a ka whatiia a ratou kopere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:16">37:16</a> Engari te wahi iti a te tangata tika i nga taonga o nga tangata kino tokomaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:17">37:17</a> Ka whatiia hoki nga ringa o te hunga kino: u tonu ia i a Ihowa te hunga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:18">37:18</a> E matau ana a Ihowa ki nga ra o te hunga tika: a ka pumau to ratou kainga ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:19">37:19</a> E kore ratou e whakama i te wa o te he, ka makona ano ratou i nga ra o te hemokai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:20">37:20</a> Ka ngaro ia te hunga kino, a ka rite nga hoariri o Ihowa ki te momona o te tarutaru: ka mahea atu ratou; ka mahea atu me he paowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:21">37:21</a> ¶ E tango ana te tangata kino i te taonga tarewa, kahore hoki ana utu: ko te tangata tika ia he aroha tona, he homai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:22">37:22</a> Ka riro hoki te whenua i ana e manaaki ai; ka hatepea ano ana e kanga ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:23">37:23</a> Ka u i a Ihowa nga hikoinga o te tangata tika; e paingia ana hoki e ia tona ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:24">37:24</a> Ahakoa hinga, e kore e tino takoto rawa; ka u hoki ia i te ringa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:25">37:25</a> He tamariki ahau i mua, a kua koroheke nei, heoi, kahore ahau i kite i te tangata tika e whakarerea ana, i ona uri hoki e pinono taro ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:26">37:26</a> I te ra roa he atawhai tonu tana, he ohaoha: ka manaakitia hoki ona uri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:27">37:27</a> Whakarerea te kino, mahia te pai, ka noho tonu ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:28">37:28</a> E aroha ana hoki a Ihowa ki te ritenga pai: e kore ano e whakarere i tana hunga tapu; e tiakina tonutia ana ratou ake ake; ka hatepea atu ia nga uri o te hunga kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:29">37:29</a> Ka riro te whenua i te hunga tika, ka nohoia hoki a reira e ratou ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:30">37:30</a> He kupu mohio ta te mangai o te tangata tika; he ritenga pai ta tona arero e korero ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:31">37:31</a> Kei tona ngakau te ture a tona Atua; e kore e paheke tetahi o ona hikoinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:32">37:32</a> E tau ana te titiro a te tangata kino ki te tangata tika, a e whai ana kia whakamatea ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:33">37:33</a> E kore a Ihowa e whakarere i a ia ki tona ringa: e kore ano ia e whakatau he ki a ia ina whakawakia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:34">37:34</a> ¶ Taria a Ihowa, kia mau ki tana ara, a ka whakanuia koe e ia, ka whakawhiwhia hoki ki te whenua: e hatepea atu te hunga kino, ka kite koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:35">37:35</a> I kite ahau i te tangata kino e kake ana, e tautorotoro ana me te rakau matomato i tona oneone tupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:36">37:36</a> Heoi, pahure noa ake tetahi, a kore kau noa iho; ae, i rapua ia e ahau, a kihai i kitea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:37">37:37</a> Waitohutia te tangata tika, tirohia iho te tangata kore he: no te mea he marie te tukunga iho ki taua tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:38">37:38</a> Tena ko te hunga kino, ka ngaro ngatahi atu ratou: te tukunga iho ki te hunga kino, ka hatepea atu ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:39">37:39</a> Na Ihowa ia te whakaoranga o te hunga tika: ko ia to ratou pa kaha i te wa o te he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:40">37:40</a> Ma Ihowa ratou e awhina, ko ia hoki hei tauarai mo ratou: ko ia hei tauarai mo ratou i te hunga kino, ka whakaorangia ratou e ia, mo ratou ka whakawhirinaki ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:1">38:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri, hei whakamahara. E Ihowa, kaua e whakatupehupehu mai ki ahau ina riri koe, kaua ano ahau e pakia ina arita koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:2">38:2</a> Titi tonu hoki au pere ki ahau: kaha rawa te pehi a tou ringa i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:3">38:3</a> Kahore he wahi ora o oku kikokiko, na tou riri hoki: kahore ano e ata takoto oku wheua, noku i hara nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:4">38:4</a> Kua taupokina iho hoki toku matenga e oku kino: ano he pikaunga taimaha e pehi rawa ana i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:5">38:5</a> E piro ana oku whiunga, kua pirau i taku mahi poauau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:6">38:6</a> E whakawiria ana ahau, piko rawa; e tangi haere ana i te roa o te ra.</p>
