 <p><a name="an_38:7">38:7</a> Kei te tahuna hoki toku hope, kapi tonu: kahore hoki he wahi ora o oku kikokiko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:8">38:8</a> Kua kore oku kaha, maru rawa ahau: hamama ana taku aue i te mamae o toku ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:9">38:9</a> E te Ariki, kei tou aroaro oku hiahia katoa; kahore hoki e ngaro i a koe taku aue.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:10">38:10</a> Kihakiha kau toku ngakau, kua hemo toku kaha: me te marama o oku kanohi, kua kore hoki ena oku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:11">38:11</a> Matara noa atu i toku mate te turanga mai o nga tangata i aroha mai ki ahau, o oku hoa hoki; i tawhiti ano oku whanaunga e tu ke mai ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:12">38:12</a> ¶ E whakatakoto mahanga ana moku te hunga e whai ana i ahau kia whakamatea; he nanakia ano nga kupu a te hunga e rapu ana i te he moku; he whakaaro tinihanga ano a ratou a pau noa te ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:13">38:13</a> Ko ahau ia, i rite ki te turi, kihai i rongo, ki te tangata wahangu, kahore nei e hamamu tona mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:14">38:14</a> Na rite tonu ahau ki te tangata kahore nei e rongo, kahore nei he whakatupehupehu i tona mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:15">38:15</a> E tumanako nei hoki ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa: ka whakahoki kupu mai ano koe, e te Ariki, e toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:16">38:16</a> I mea hoki ahau, Kei koa mai ratou ki ahau: ka paheke toku waewae, ka whakahihi ratou ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:17">38:17</a> Ko ahau hoki, meake kopa, a kei inua tonu i ahau toku pouri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:18">38:18</a> Ka whaki hoki ahau i toku kino, ka pouri mo toku hara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:19">38:19</a> Ko oku hoariri ia hauhau tonu, kaha tonu; kua tokomaha ano te hunga e kino noa ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:20">38:20</a> He hoariri ano ki ahau te hunga e utu ana i te pai ki te kino: moku e whai ana i te pai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:21">38:21</a> Kaua ahau e whakarerea, e Ihowa, e toku Atua; kei mamao atu koe i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:22">38:22</a> Hohoro ki te awhina i ahau, e te Ariki, e toku whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:1">39:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ki a Ierutunu. He himene na Rawiri. I mea ahau, Ka ata whakaaro ahau ki oku ara, kei hara toku arero; ka tiakina toku mangai, paraire rawa, i te mea kei toku aroaro te tangata kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:2">39:2</a> I whakamoroki ahau, i wahangu, kihai i puaki taku kupu, ahakoa pai; a ka oho toku mamae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:3">39:3</a> Werawera ana toku ngakau i roto i ahau; i ahau e whakaaro ana ka ka te ahi, a ka korero toku arero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:4">39:4</a> E Ihowa, meinga ahau kia matau ki toku mutunga, ki te maha hoki o oku ra, e hia ranei: kia matau ai ahau he mea memeha noa ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:5">39:5</a> Nana, he whanuitanga ringa oku ra kua homai nei e koe; he kahore noa iho ano oku tau i tou aroaro: ahakoa u noa te tu o nga tangata katoa, he mea memeha kau. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:6">39:6</a> He pono kei roto i te atarangi te tangata e kopikopiko noa ana; he pono e ohorere noa ana ratou: e ami ana ia i te taonga, a kahore e matau ma wai ranei e kohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:7">39:7</a> ¶ Na he aha taku e tatari atu nei, e te Ariki? Ko koe taku e tumanako ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:8">39:8</a> Whakaorangia ahau i aku mahi tutu katoa: kaua ahau e waiho hei tawainga ma te wairangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:9">39:9</a> Wahangu ana ahau, kihai i kuihi toku mangai: he meatanga hoki tenei nau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:10">39:10</a> Nekehia atu i ahau tau whiu: ka ngaro ahau i te pakinga a tou ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:11">39:11</a> Ka pakia e koe te tangata, ka whakatupehupehutia mo te hara, ka meinga e koe tona ataahua kia memeha, kia pera me te purehurehu: he pono he mea teka noa nga tangata katoa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:12">39:12</a> Whakarongo ki taku inoi, e Ihowa, kia titaha mai tou taringa ki taku karanga; kei wahangu koe ki oku roimata: he heke hoki ahau nau, he manene, he pera me oku matua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:13">39:13</a> Kia ata hanga ki ahau, kia ta ai toku manawa, keiwha haere atu ahau i konei, a ka kahore noa iho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:1">40:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. I tatari marie ahau ki a Ihowa: a anga ana ia ki ahau, whakarongo ana ki taku karanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:2">40:2</a> Na kei te tango ake ia i ahau i te poka whakamataku, i te paru taoruoru; kei te whakatu i oku waewae ki runga ki te kohatu, kei te whakau i oku hikoinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:3">40:3</a> A homai ana e ia he waiata hou ki toku mangai, he whakamoemiti ki to tatou Atua: he tokomaha e kite, a ka wehi ka whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:4">40:4</a> Ka hari te tangata kua waiho nei e ia a Ihowa hei whakawhirinakitanga mona: a kahore e tahuri ki te hunga whakakake, ki te hunga hoki e peka ana ki te teka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:5">40:5</a> E Ihowa, e toku Atua, he tini au mahi whakamiharo i mahia e koe, me ou whakaaro ki a matou; e kore e taea te korero whakatepe atu ki a koe: me i mea ahau kia whakakitea, kia korerotia, e kore e taea te tatau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:6">40:6</a> ¶ Kihai i matenuitia e koe te patunga tapu, me te whakahere; pokaia ana e koe oku taringa: kihai koe i mea mai ki te tahunga tinana, ki te whakahere hara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:7">40:7</a> Na ko taku meatanga atu, Na kua tae mai ahau: kei roto i te pukapuka te tuhituhi moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:8">40:8</a> Ko taku pai ko te mea i tau e pai ai, e toku Atua: ae ra, kei toku ngakau tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:9">40:9</a> Kua kauwhautia e ahau te tika i roto i te whakaminenga nui: nana, kihai i kopia oku ngutu, tena koe te matau ana, e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:10">40:10</a> Kihai i huna e ahau tou tika i roto i toku ngakau; kua korerotia e ahau tou pono me tau whakaoranga: kihai i hunga e ahau tou aroha me tou pono i te whakaminenga nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:11">40:11</a> ¶ Kei kaiponuhia tou aroha ki ahau, e Ihowa: ma tou atawhai me tou pono ahau e tiaki i nga wa katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:12">40:12</a> Ta te mea kua karapotia ahau e nga kino e kore e taea te tatau: mau pu ahau i oku kino, te ahei te titiro ake; he tini ke i nga makawe o toku matenga: a hemo iho toku ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:13">40:13</a> Kia pai, e Ihowa, ki te whakaora i ahau; e Ihowa, hohoro ki te awhina i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:14">40:14</a> Kia whakama, kia pororaru ngatahi te hunga e rapu ana i toku wairua kia whakamatea: kia whakahokia ki muri, kia whakama te hunga e hiahia ana kia he ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:15">40:15</a> Kia huna, hei utu mo to ratou whakama te hunga e mea mai ana ki ahau, Ha, ha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:16">40:16</a> Kia hari, kia koa ki a koe te hunga katoa e rapu ana i a koe; kia mea tonu te hunga e pai ana ki tau whakaoranga, Kia whakanuia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:17">40:17</a> Ko ahau ia, he iti, he rawakore; heoi e whakaaro ana te Ariki ki ahau: ko koe toku awhina, toku kaiwhakaora; kaua ra e whakaroa, e toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:1">41:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. Ka hari te tangata e whakaaro ana ki te rawakore; e whakaorangia ia e Ihowa i te ra o te he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:2">41:2</a> Ma Ihowa ia e tiaki, e whakaora; ka whakaharitia ia i runga i te whenua: e kore ano e tukua e koe ki nga hiahia o ona hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:3">41:3</a> Ma Ihowa ia e whakakaha, i a ia e whakaruhi ana i runga i te moenga: mau ano e whakapai katoa tona moenga i a ia e mate ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:4">41:4</a> I mea ahau, E Ihowa, tohungia ahau; rongoatia toku wairua; kua hara hoki ahau ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:5">41:5</a> ¶ He kino te korero a oku hoariri moku, e mea ana, A hea ranei ia mate ai, pirau ai tona ingoa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:6">41:6</a> A ki te haere mai ia kia kite i ahau, ka korero horihori ia: e ami ana tona ngakau i te kino mana; i tona putanga ki waho, korerotia ana e ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:7">41:7</a> E komuhumuhu ana moku te hunga katoa e kino ana ki ahau; e whakatakoto ana i te kino moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:8">41:8</a> E ai ta ratou, E piri ana te mate kino ki a ia; a ka takoto nei ia, heoi ano tona aranga ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:9">41:9</a> Ae, ko toku hoa ake ano, i whakawhirinaki ai ahau, i kai nei i taku taro, kua hiki ake tona rekereke ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:10">41:10</a> Ko koe ia, e Ihowa, kia aroha ki ahau: a whakaarahia ahau, kia utua ai ratou e ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:11">41:11</a> Na konei ahau i matau ai e pai ana koe ki ahau, no te mea kahore toku hoariri e whakamanamana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:12">41:12</a> Ko ahau ia, ko koe e whakamau ake ana i ahau i runga i toku ngakau tapatahi: e whakatu ake ana hoki i ahau ki tou aroaro ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:13">41:13</a> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, te Atua o Iharaira inamata riro ano, ake tonu atu ano hoki. Amine, ae Amine.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:1">42:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He Makiri, ma nga tama a Koraha. Rite tonu ki te hata e kihakiha nei ki nga manga wai toku ngakau e kihakiha nei ki a koe, e te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:2">42:2</a> E hiainu ana toku wairua ki te Atua, ki te Atua ora: a hea ahau tae ai, puta ai ki te aroaro o te Atua?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:3">42:3</a> Ko oku roimata taku kai i te ao, i te po, i a ratou e mea tonu mai nei ki ahau, Kei hea tou Atua?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:4">42:4</a> Ka mahara ahau ki enei mea; me te wai toku ngakau e maringi ana i roto i ahau: i haere hoki ahau i roto i te huihui, i haere tahi matou ki te whare o te Atua, he hari te reo, he whakamoemiti, me te huihui e mea hakari ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:5">42:5</a> He aha koe i piko ai, e toku wairua? i ohorere ai i roto i ahau? Tumanako ki te Atua; tera ano ahau e whakawhetai ki a ia, mo te ora o tona mata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:6">42:6</a> ¶ E toku Atua, kua piko toku wairua i roto i ahau: koia ahau ka mahara ai ki a koe i te whenua o Horano, o nga Heremoni, i Maunga Mitara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:7">42:7</a> Rara ana tetahi rire ki tetahi rire i te haruru o au awhiowhio wai: tika ana au ngaru katoa me au tuatea i runga i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:8">42:8</a> Ahakoa ra e whakahaua mai ano e Ihowa tona atawhai i te awatea; a he waiata taku ki a ia i te po, he inoi ki te Atua o toku ora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:9">42:9</a> Ka mea ahau ki te Atua, E toku kohatu, he aha koe i wareware ai ki ahau? He aha ahau ka haere pouri ai i te tukino a te hoariri?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:10">42:10</a> Ano he hoari i roto i oku wheua te tawai a oku hoariri: i a ratou e mea mai nei ki ahau i nga ra katoa, Kei hea tou Atua?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:11">42:11</a> He aha koe i piko ai, e toku wairua? He aha koe i ohorere ai i roto i ahau? Tumanako ki te Atua: tera ano ahau e whakawhetai ki a ia, ko te ora nei ia o toku mata, ko toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:1">43:1</a> ¶ E te Atua, whakaritea taku whakawa, whakatikaia aku korero ki te iwi atuakore: whakaorangia ahau i te tangata tinihanga e mahi nei i te he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:2">43:2</a> Ko koe hoki te Atua o toku kaha: he aha ahau ka panga nei e koe? He aha ahau ka haere pouri ai i te tukino a te hoariri?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:3">43:3</a> Tukua mai tou marama me tou pono hei arahi i ahau: hei kawe i ahau ki tou maunga tapu, ki ou tapenakara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:4">43:4</a> A ka haere ahau ki te aata a te Atua, ki te Atua, ki toku hari nui: ae, ka whakamoemiti ki a koe, e te Atua, e toku Atua, i runga i te hapa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:5">43:5</a> He aha koe i piko ai, e toku wairua? He aha koe i ohorere ai i roto i ahau? Tumanako ki te Atua: tera ano ahau e whakawhetai ki a ia, ko te ora nei ia o toku mata, ko toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:1">44:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ma nga tama a Koraha. He Makiri. E te Atua, kua rongo o matou taringa, kua korerotia ki a matou e o matou matua, nga mahi i mahia e koe i o ratou ra, i nga ra o mua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:2">44:2</a> Nau nga tauiwi i pana ki tou ringa, nau ratou i whakato: nau nga iwi i whiu, a whakamararatia ana ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:3">44:3</a> Ehara hoki i te mea, na ta ratou hoari i whiwhi ai ratou ki te whenua, ehara to ratou takakau i te mea i ora ai ratou: engari na tou matau, na tou takakau hoki, na te marama ano o tou mata, he pai hoki nou ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:4">44:4</a> E te Atua, ko koe toku Kingi: whakahaua he whakaora mo Hakapa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:5">44:5</a> Mau ka turaki ai matou i o matou hoariri; ma tou ingoa ka takahia ai e matou te hunga e whakatika ana ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:6">44:6</a> E kore hoki ahau e whakawhirinaki ki taku kopere: e kore ano taku hoari e whakaora i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:7">44:7</a> Nau hoki matou i ora ai i o matou hoariri: nau ano i whakama ai te hunga i kino ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:8">44:8</a> Ko te Atua ta matou e whakamanamana ai i te roa o te ra: ka whakamoemiti ano matou ki tou ingoa ake ake. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:9">44:9</a> ¶ Otira kua panga nei matou e koe, kua meinga kia whakama: kahore hoki koe kia haere tahi me a matou taua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:10">44:10</a> Kua meinga matou kia hoki whakamuri mai i te hoariri; kei te pahua ano i etahi ma ratou te hunga e kino ana ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:11">44:11</a> Kua hoatu matou e koe, ano he hipi e kainga ana: kua marara ki roto ki nga tauiwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:12">44:12</a> E hokona ana e koe tau iwi, a hore he utu: kahore hoki koe e whiwhi rawa i te utu mo ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:13">44:13</a> E meinga ana matou e koe hei tawainga ma o matou hoa kainga; hei whakahaweatanga, hei whakakatanga mai ma te hunga i tetahi taha, i tetahi taha o matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:14">44:14</a> E meinga ana matou e koe hei whakatauki ma nga tauiwi; hei rurutanga matenga ma nga iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:15">44:15</a> Kei mua tonu i ahau toku whakama; kua taupokina ahau e te pawera o toku mata;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:16">44:16</a> I te reo o te kaitawai, o te kaikohukohu; i te hoariri, i te kairapu utu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:17">44:17</a> ¶ Kua pa katoa tenei ki a matou; heoi kahore matou i wareware ki a koe, kihai ano i teka ki tau kawenata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:18">44:18</a> Kahore to matou ngakau i tahuri whakamuri; kihai ano o matou hikoinga i peka ke i tau ara;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:19">44:19</a> I maru ai matou i a koe i te wahi o nga tarakona; a taupoki rawa ki te atarangi o te mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:20">44:20</a> Mehemea kua wareware matou ki te ingoa o to matou Atua, kua totoro ranei o matou ringa ki te atua ke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:21">44:21</a> E kore ranei tenei e ata tirohia e te Atua? E matau ana hoki ia ki nga mea ngaro o te ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:22">44:22</a> Mou nei hoki matou i patua ai i te ra roa nei: kiia iho matou he hipi e patua ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:23">44:23</a> E ara, he aha koe ka moe ai, e te Ariki? Whakatika, kaua matou e panga tonutia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:24">44:24</a> He aha koe ka huna ai i tou mata? ka wareware ai ki to matou mamae, ki to matou tukinotanga?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:25">44:25</a> Kua piko nei hoki to matou wairua ki raro ki te puehu; piri rawa to matou kopu ki te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:26">44:26</a> E ara, hei awhina i a matou; kia mahara ki tou aroha, a hokona matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:1">45:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He Homhanimi ma nga tama a Koraha. He Makiri, he waiata aroha. E pupuke ake ana te mea pai i roto i toku ngakau: ka korerotia e ahau aku i tito ai mo te kingi: he pene toku arero na te kaituhituhi hohoro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:2">45:2</a> Engari koe he ataahua i nga tama a te tangata: kua ringihia ou ngutu ki te ahuareka, na reira i manaakitia ai koe e te Atua ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:3">45:3</a> Whitikiria tau hoari ki tou huwha, e te Nui Rawa, tou kororia me tou honore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:4">45:4</a> Aratakina hoki tou hoiho i runga i tou honore, i te kaha, hei mea hoki mo te pono, mo te mahaki, mo te tika, a ma tou matau koe e whakaako ki nga mea whakamataku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:5">45:5</a> He koi au pere; ka hinga nga iwi ki raro i a koe; kei roto ratou i te ngakau o nga hoariri o te kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:6">45:6</a> ¶ He pumau, e te Atua, tou torona ake ake: he hepeta tika te hepeta o tou kingitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:7">45:7</a> Kua aroha koe ki te tika, kua kino ki te hara: na reira, nui atu i to ou hoa te whakawahinga a te Atua, a tou Atua i a koe ki te hinu o te hari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:8">45:8</a> Ko tou kakahu katoa he kakara maira, he aroe, he kahia; ko nga mea aho, whakatangitangi o nga whare rei nana koe i whakaahuareka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:9">45:9</a> Kei roto i au wahine honore nga tamahine kingi; kei tou matau te kuini e tu ana, no Opira te koura.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:10">45:10</a> ¶ Whakarongo, e ko, titiro, tahuri iho tou taringa: a kia wareware koe ki tou iwi, ki te whare ano o tou papa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:11">45:11</a> Penei ka matenuitia e te kingi tou ataahua: ko ia hoki tou Ariki; a me koropiko ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:12">45:12</a> Ko reira ano te tamahine o Taira me te ohaoha: ka whai ano nga tangata taonga o te iwi kia manakohia e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:13">45:13</a> Kei roto te tamahine a te kingi, he kororia kau, he mea whakairo ki te koura tona kakahu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:14">45:14</a> He mea whakapaipai ki te ngira tona kakahu e kawea ai ia ki te kingi: ka arahina ki a koe nga wahine, ona takahoa e whai ana i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:15">45:15</a> He hari, he koa ina kawea mai ratou; ka tomo ki te whare o te kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:16">45:16</a> Ko au tamariki hei whakakapi mo ou matua: ka meinga ano ratou e koe hei kawana mo te whenua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:17">45:17</a> Ka meinga e ahau tou ingoa kia maharatia e nga whakatupuranga katoa: e whakamoemititia ai koe e nga iwi a ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:1">46:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ma nga tama a Koraha. He waiata Aramoto. Ko te Atua to tatou piringa, to tatou kaha; he kaiawhina e tino tata ana i nga wa o te he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:2">46:2</a> Na reira kore ake to tatou wehi, ahakoa nekehia te whenua, ahakoa kahakina nga maunga ki waenga moana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:3">46:3</a> Ahakoa rara, taupatupatu noa ona wai, ahakoa wiri nga maunga i tona huamo. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:4">46:4</a> He awa tena ko ona manga hei whakahari i te pa o te Atua, i te wahi tapu o nga tapenakara o te Runga Rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:5">46:5</a> Kei waenganui ona te Atua, e kore ia e whakakorikoria: ma te Atua ia e awhina i te putanga ano o te ata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:6">46:6</a> ¶ I nana nga tauiwi, i whakakorikoria nga rangatiratanga; puaki ana tona reo, rewa ana te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:7">46:7</a> Kei a tatou a Ihowa o nga mano, ko te Atua o Hakopa to tatou piringa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:8">46:8</a> Haere mai, tirohia nga mahi a Ihowa, nga whakangaromanga i whakaputaina e ia ki te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:9">46:9</a> E whakamutua ana e ia nga whainga a te pito ra ano o te whenua: whati ana i a ia te kopere, poro pu te tao, tahuna ake e ia te hariata ki te kapura.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:10">46:10</a> Kia ata noho, a kia matau ko ahau te Atua; e whakanuia ahau i waenganui i nga tauiwi, e whakanuia ahau i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:11">46:11</a> Kei a tatou a Ihowa o nga mano: ko te Atua o Hakopa to tatou piringa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:1">47:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene ma nga tama a Koraha. Pakia o koutou ringa, e nga iwi katoa: hamama ki te Atua, kia hari te reo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:2">47:2</a> No te mea he wehi a Ihowa, te Runga Rawa, he kingi nui ia no te whenua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:3">47:3</a> Mana e riro ai nga iwi ki raro i a tatou, me nga tautangata ki raro ki o tatou waewae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:4">47:4</a> Mana e whiriwhiri to tatou nohoanga mo tatou, te mea pai rawa o Hakopa, o tana i aroha ai. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:5">47:5</a> ¶ Kua kake atu te Atua i roto i te hamama, a Ihowa i roto i te tangi o te tetere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:6">47:6</a> Himene ki te Atua, himene atu; himene ki to tatou Kingi, himene atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:7">47:7</a> Ko te Atua hoki te Kingi o te whenua katoa: himene atu i runga i te mohio.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:8">47:8</a> Ko te Atua te Kingi o nga tauiwi: e noho ana te Atua i runga i te torona o tona tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:9">47:9</a> Kua huihui nga rangatira o nga iwi, hei iwi mo te Atua o Aperahama: na te Atua hoki nga whakangungu rakau o te whenua; kua whakanuia rawatia ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:1">48:1</a> ¶ He waiata, he himene ma nga tama a Koraha. He nui a Ihowa, kia nui hoki te whakamoemiti ki a ia i te pa o to tatou Atua, i te maunga o tona tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:2">48:2</a> Ataahua ana te tairanga o Maunga Hiona, ko ta te ao katoa e koa ai: kei te taha ki te raki te pa o te Kingi nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:3">48:3</a> E matauria ana te Atua i roto i ona whare papai hei piringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:4">48:4</a> Na, huihui tahi mai ana nga kingi haere tahi atu ana ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:5">48:5</a> I kite ratou, miharo iho: raruraru ana, hohoro tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:6">48:6</a> Pa ana te wehi ki a ratou i reira, te mamae, ano he wahine e whanau ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:7">48:7</a> E wahia ana e koe nga kaipuke o Tarahihi ki te marangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:8">48:8</a> ¶ Rite tonu ki ta matou i rongo ai, ta matou i kite ai i roto i te pa o Ihowa o nga mano, i te pa o to tatou Atua: ma te Atua e whakapumau ake ake. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:9">48:9</a> I whakaaroaro matou ki tou atawhai, e te Atua, i waenganui o tou temepara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:10">48:10</a> E te Atua, rite tahi ki tou ingoa te whakamoemiti mou, tae noa atu ki nga pito o te whenua: ki tonu tou matau i te tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:11">48:11</a> Kia hari a Maunga Hiona, kia koa nga tamahine a Hura i au whakaritenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:12">48:12</a> Taiawhiotia a Hiona, haere, a kopiko noa mai: taua ona pourewa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:13">48:13</a> Maharatia ona pekerangi, tirohia ona whare papai; hei korerotanga ma koutou ki enei ake whakatupuranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:14">48:14</a> Ko tenei Atua hoki te Atua mo tatou ake ake: ko ia hei kaiarahi i a tatou a mate noa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:1">49:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene ma nga tama a Koraha. Whakarongo ki tenei, e nga iwi katoa: tahuri mai o koutou taringa, e nga tangata katoa o te ao.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:2">49:2</a> E nga tangata iti, koutou ko nga tangata rahi, e te tangata taonga korua ko te rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:3">49:3</a> Ka whakapuakina he matauranga e toku mangai: a he ata ngarahu te whakaaro o toku ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:4">49:4</a> Ka titaha toku taringa ki te kupu whakarite; ka puaki taku pepeha i runga i te hapa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:5">49:5</a> Kia wehi ahau ki te aha i nga ra o te kino, ina karapotia ahau e te kino kei oku rekereke?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:6">49:6</a> ¶ Ko te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki o ratou taonga, e whakamanamana ana ki te nui o o ratou rawa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:7">49:7</a> E kore tetahi o ratou e ahei te hoko i tona teina, te hoatu ranei i tetahi utu mona ki te Atua;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:8">49:8</a> He nui hoki te utu mo to ratou wairua, a me whakarere atu ake ake;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:9">49:9</a> Kia ora tonu ai ia ake ake: kia kaua e kite i te pirau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:10">49:10</a> E kite ana hoki ia e matemate ana nga tangata whakaaro nui, e ngaro ngatahi ana te poauau me te whakaarokore, a mahue iho o ratou taonga ki etahi atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:11">49:11</a> Ki to ratou whakaaro puku, tera e pumau tonu o ratou whare me o ratou nohoanga, ki nga whakatupuranga katoa: huaina iho o ratou whenua ki o ratou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:12">49:12</a> Heoi kahore te tangata e noho tonu i roto i te honore: ko tona rite kei nga kararehe ka moti nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:13">49:13</a> Ko to ratou ara tenei, ara ko to ratou poauau: heoi e whakapai ana to ratou uri ki a ratou korero. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:14">49:14</a> Kei te hipi te rite: ko te wahi mo ratou ko te reinga; ko te mate hei hepara mo ratou, hei rangatira ano te hunga tika mo ratou i te ata; ko to ratou ataahua ma te reinga e whakamoti, kia kore ai he whare mona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:15">49:15</a> ¶ Ma te Atua ia toku wairua e hoko mai i te reinga: ko ia hoki hei tukunga atu moku. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:16">49:16</a> Kaua e wehi ua whai taonga te tangata, ina nui haere te kororia o tona whare;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:17">49:17</a> Kahore hoki ana mea e mau atu ai ia ina mate; e kore tona kororia e tuku iho i muri i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:18">49:18</a> Whakapai noa ia i tona wairua i a ia e ora ana; a ka whakamoemititia koe ua pai au mahi ki a koe ano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:19">49:19</a> Ka haere ia ki te whakatupuranga o ona tupuna: e kore rawa ratou e kite i te marama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:20">49:20</a> Ko te tangata e whakahonoretia ana, a kahore e whai whakaaro, kei nga kararehe ka moti nei tona rite.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:1">50:1</a> ¶ He himene na Ahapa. Kua puaki te kupu a te Atua, a te Atua tonu, a Ihowa, a karangatia ana e ia te whenua i te putanga mai o te ra, tae noa ki tona torengitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:2">50:2</a> Kua tiaho mai te Atua i roto i Hiona, i te tino o te ataahua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:3">50:3</a> Ka haere mai to tatou Atua, e kore ano e wahangu: ka kai te kapura i tona aroaro, a ka hukerikeri te awha ki tetahi taha ona, ki tetahi taha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:4">50:4</a> Ka karangatia e ia nga rangi i runga, me te whenua hoki, ki te whakaritenga mo tona iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:5">50:5</a> Huihuia mai ki ahau taku hunga tapu, te hunga i whakarite kawenata ki ahau i runga i te patunga tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:6">50:6</a> A ma nga rangi e whakakite tona tika: ko te Atua ake nei hoki te kaiwhakawa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:7">50:7</a> ¶ Whakarongo, e toku iwi, a ka korero ahau; e Iharaira, ka whakaatu ahau ki a koe; ko ahau te Atua, ko tou Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:8">50:8</a> E kore ahau e riri ki a koe mo au patunga tapu; a kei toku aroaro tonu au tahunga tinana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:9">50:9</a> E kore ahau e tango i tetahi puru i roto i tou whare, i etahi koati toa ranei i roto i au taiepa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:10">50:10</a> Naku nei hoki nga kirehe katoa o te ngahere, nga kararehe i runga i te mano o nga pukepuke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:11">50:11</a> E matau ana ahau ki nga manu katoa o nga maunga; naku ano nga kirehe o te parae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:12">50:12</a> Me he matekai toku, e kore ahau e korero ki a koe: naku nei hoki te ao, me ona tini mea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:13">50:13</a> E kai koia ahau i te kikokiko o nga puru, e inu ranei i te toto o nga koati?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:14">50:14</a> Ko te whakawhetai hei patunga tapu mau ki te Atua; whakamana hoki au kupu taurangi ki te Runga Rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:15">50:15</a> A karanga ki ahau i te ra o te he: maku koe e whakaora, a ka whakakororiatia ahau e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:16">50:16</a> ¶ Ki te tangata hara ia ka mea te Atua, He aha mau te whakapuaki i aku tikanga, te whakahua ranei i taku kawenata e tou mangai?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:17">50:17</a> Kua kino nei hoki koe ki te ako, a e akiri ana i aku kupu ki muri i a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:18">50:18</a> I tou kitenga i te tahae, na whakaae ana koe ki a ia; a whai tahi ana me te hunga puremu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:19">50:19</a> Kua tukua e koe tou mangai ki te kino; a e tito hianga ana tou arero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:20">50:20</a> Noho ana koe, ka korero kino ki tou teina: ngautuara tonu iho koe ki te tama a tou whaea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:21">50:21</a> Ko au mahi enei, a wahangu tonu ahau; i mea koe he pena pu ahau me koe: otira ka riria koe e ahau, ka whakararangitia ano aua mea ki tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:22">50:22</a> Na whakaaroa tenei, e te hunga kua wareware ki te Atua; kei haehaea koutou e ahau, a kahore he kaiwhakaora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:23">50:23</a> Ko te whakamoemiti te patunga tapu e whai kororia ai ahau: ko te tangata hoki he tika nei tona ara ka whakakitea e ahau ki a ia te whakaoranga a te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:1">51:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri, i te taenga o Natana poropiti ki a ia, mo tona haerenga ki a Patehepa. Tohungia ahau, e te Atua, kia rite ki tou atawhai: kia rite ki tou aroha nui te murunga o oku he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:2">51:2</a> Horoia rawatia toku kino: kia ma hoki toku hara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:3">51:3</a> E whaki ana hoki ahau i aku mahi tutu: kei toku aroaro tonu toku hara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:4">51:4</a> He hara ki a koe, ki a koe anake, toku; i meatia ano tenei he ki tou aroaro; kia tika ai koe i tau korerotanga, kia ma ai hoki ina whakawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:5">51:5</a> Na i whakaahuatia ahau i roto i te kino, i runga ano i te hara toku whakahaputanga ki roto ki toku whaea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:6">51:6</a> Na ko tau e matenui ai ko te pono i nga wahi o roto, a ka whakaakona oku wahi ngaro e koe ki te whakaaro nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:7">51:7</a> ¶ Purea ahau ki te hihopa, a ka ma ahau; horoia ahau, a ka ma ke atu i te hukarere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:8">51:8</a> Meinga kia rongo ahau i te hari, i te koa, a ka whakamanamana nga iwi i whatiia nei e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:9">51:9</a> Huna tou mata ki oku hara; a murua katoatia oku kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:10">51:10</a> Hanga, e te Atua, he ngakau ma ki roto ki ahau: whakahoutia hoki ki roto ki ahau he wairua tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:11">51:11</a> Kaua ahau e maka i tou aroaro; kaua hoki tou wairua tapu e tangohia i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:12">51:12</a> Whakahokia mai ki ahau te hari o tau whakaoranga: tautokona hoki ahau ki te wairua kakama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:13">51:13</a> Ko reira ahau whakaako ai i au ara ki te hunga tutu; a ka tahuri te hunga hara ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:14">51:14</a> ¶ Whakaorangia ahau i te hara toto, e te Atua, e te Atua o toku whakaoranga, a ka waiatatia au mahi tika e toku arero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:15">51:15</a> Whakatuwheratia oku ngutu, e te Ariki; a ka puaki i toku mangai te whakamoemiti ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:16">51:16</a> Kahore nei hoki koe e aro ki te patunga tapu; penei kua hoatu e ahau: kahore koe e ahuareka ki te tahunga tinana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:17">51:17</a> Ko nga patunga tapu ma te Atua he wairua maru: e kore koe e whakahawea e te Atua, ki te ngakau maru, ki te ngakau iro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:18">51:18</a> Kia pai koe ki te atawhai i Hiona: hanga nga taiepa o Hiruharama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:19">51:19</a> Ko reira koe pai ai ki nga patunga tapu o te tika, ki nga tahunga tinana, he mea whakaeke katoa: ko reira ratou whakaeke ai i nga puru ki runga ki tou aata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:1">52:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He Makiri; na Rawiri, i a Roeke Eromi i haere, i whakaatu ki a Haora, i mea ki a ia, Kua tae a Rawiri ki te whare o Ahimereke. He aha koe ka whakapakari ai ki te kino, e te tangata nui? He pumau tonu te atawhai o te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:2">52:2</a> E whakatakoto ana tou arero i nga mea nanakia, e mahi hianga ana, ano he heu koi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:3">52:3</a> E arohaina rawatia ana e koe te kino i te pai, te teka i te korero tika. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:4">52:4</a> E te arero hianga, e arohaina ana e koe nga kupu horomiti katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:5">52:5</a> Ka whakangaro hoki te Atua i a koe ake tonu atu; ka tangohia atu koe e ia, ka takiritia atu i tou nohoanga, ka hutia atu hoki koe i te whenua o te ora. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:6">52:6</a> ¶ E kite hoki te hunga tika, a ka wehi; ka kata hoki ki a ia, ka mea,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:7">52:7</a> Inana, ko te tangata tenei kihai nei i waiho e ia te Atua hei kaha mona; otiia, whakawhirinaki ana ki te tini o ana taonga, whakapakari ana i runga i tana mahi kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:8">52:8</a> Ko ahau ia, e rite ana ki te oriwa matomato i roto i te whare o te Atua: ka whakawhirinaki ahau ki te mahi tohu a te Atua ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:9">52:9</a> Ka whakamoemiti tonu ahau ki a koe, nau hoki tenei i mea: ka tumanako ano ki tou ingoa; he mea pai hoki, ki te aroaro o tau hunga tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:1">53:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Maharata. He Makiri, na Rawiri. Kua ki te wairangi i roto i tona ngakau, Kahore he Atua. Kua pirau ratou, he kino whakahouhou ta ratou mahi; kahore tetahi e mahi ana i te pai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:2">53:2</a> I titiro iho te Atua i te rangi ki nga tama a te tangata, kia kite me kahore tetahi e mahara ana, e rapu ana i te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:3">53:3</a> Kua hoki ki muri ratou katoa, kua pirau tahi: kahore tetahi e mahi ana i te pai, kahore kia kotahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:4">53:4</a> E kore ranei e mohio nga kaimahi i te kino? e kai nei i toku iwi, me te mea e kai taro ana; a kahore e karanga ki te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:5">53:5</a> Wehi noa iho ratou i reira, i te wahi kahore he wehi, no te mea kua titaria e te Atua nga wheua o te tangata i whakapaea ai koe: kua whakama ratou i a koe; no te mea kua whakahaweatia ratou e te Atua</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:6">53:6</a> Aue, me i puta mai te whakaoranga o Iharaira i Hiona! Kia whakahokia mai e te Atua tana iwi i te whakarau, ka whakamanamana a Hakopa, ka hari a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:1">54:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nekinoto. He Makiri, na Rawiri i te haerenga o nga Tiwhi ki a Haora, ki ai, He teka ianei kei a matou a Rawiri e piri ana? E te Atua, kia whakaorangia ahau e tou ingoa; kia whakawakia hoki ahau e tou kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:2">54:2</a> E te Atua, whakarongo ki taku inoi, tahuri mai tou taringa ki nga kupu a toku mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:3">54:3</a> No te mea kua whakatika mai nga tangata iwi ki ki ahau, a e whaia ana toku wairua e te hunga tukino: kahore i waiho e ratou te Atua ki to ratou aroaro. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:4">54:4</a> ¶ Tenei te Atua hei kaiawhina moku; kei roto te Ariki i te hunga e tautoko ake ana i toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:5">54:5</a> Mana e utu te kino o oku hoariri: huna ratou, he pono nei hoki koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:6">54:6</a> Ka kakama ahau ki te mea patunga tapu ki a koe, ka whakamoemiti ki tou ingoa, e Ihowa: he mea pai hoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:7">54:7</a> Kua whakaorangia hoki ahau e ia i roto i nga he katoa: a kua titiro toku kanohi ki te mea e hiahia ana ahau ki oku hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:1">55:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nekinoto. He Makiri, na Rawiri. E te Atua, tahuri mai tou taringa ki taku inoi: kei whakangaro atu koe, ina tangi ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:2">55:2</a> Anga mai ki ahau, whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau: pokaikaha noa iho ahau i ahau e tangi nei, e hamama nei;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:3">55:3</a> I te reo hoki o te hoariri, i te tukino a te tangata kino: no te mea e utaina ana e ratou he hara ki runga ki ahau, a e kino ana ki ahau, e riri ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:4">55:4</a> Mamae pu toku ngakau i roto i ahau: kua taka ki runga ki ahau nga wehi whakamate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:5">55:5</a> Kua pa ki ahau te wehi me te wiri: a pokia iho ahau e te whakamataku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:6">55:6</a> Na ko taku meatanga, Aue, te whai pakau ahau me he kukupa; penei ka rere atu ahau, a ka whai okiokinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:7">55:7</a> Katahi ahau ka rere ki tawhiti; a noho rawa atu i te koraha. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:8">55:8</a> Ka hohoro toku rere atu i te hau, i te awha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:9">55:9</a> ¶ Whakangaromia, e te Ariki, wehia o ratou arero; kua kitea hoki e ahau te tukino me te tutu o roto o te pa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:10">55:10</a> Haereere ana ratou i te ao, i te po, i runga i ona taiepa, a tawhio noa: he kino kei roto, he hianga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:11">55:11</a> He hara kei waenganui ona: kahore ona ara e mahue i te tinihanga, i te hianga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:12">55:12</a> Ehara hoki i te hoariri nana ahau i tawai; penei e taea e ahau te whakaririka: ehara hoki i te hoa whawhai noku i whakakake ki ahau; penei kua piri ahau, kei kitea e ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:13">55:13</a> Nau ia, na te tangata i rite ki ahau, na toku takahoa, na taku i mohio ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:14">55:14</a> Ahuareka tonu ta taua korerorero; haere tahi ana hoki taua i roto i te ropu ki te whare o te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:15">55:15</a> Kia mau ohorere ratou i te mate, kia heke ora ki te reinga: he hara hoki kei o ratou nohoanga, kei waenganui i a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:16">55:16</a> ¶ Ko ahau, ka karanga ahau ki te Atua: a ma Ihowa ahau e whakaora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:17">55:17</a> I te ahiahi, i te ata, i te poutumarotanga, ka inoi ahau, ka tangi: a ka whakarongo ia ki toku reo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:18">55:18</a> Whakaorangia ana e ia toku wairua i runga i te rangimarie i ahau e whakaekea ana: he tokomaha hoki oku hoa whawhai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:19">55:19</a> Ka whakarongo te Atua, no tua iho nei tona nohoanga, a ka whakahoki i ta ratou. (Hera.) Ko te hunga kahore o ratou whakawhitiwhitinga, a kahore o ratou wehi ki te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:20">55:20</a> Kua totoro ona ringa ki te hunga kua mau nei ta ratou rongo ki a ia; kua whakataka e ia tana kawenata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:21">55:21</a> Maeneene atu tona mangai i te pata, he whawhai ia kei roto i tona ngakau: ngawari atu ana kupu i te hinu, kahore, he hoari kua oti te unu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:22">55:22</a> Maka ki runga ki a Ihowa tau pikaunga, a mana koe e whakau ake: e kore e tukua e ia te hunga tika kia whakangaueuetia ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:23">55:23</a> Mau ia ratou e mea, e te Atua, kia heke ki te poka o te pirau: e kore nga tangata toto, nga tangata hianga e tutuki ki te hawhe o o ratou ra; ko ahau ia, ka whakawhirinaki ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:1">56:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Ionata ereme rehokime. Na Rawiri. He Mikitama, i a ia ka mau i nga Pirihitini ki Kata. Tohungia ahau e te Atua, ka horomia hoki ahau e te tangata: e tukino ana ia ki ahau i te ra roa nei, i a ia e ngangare tonu nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:2">56:2</a> E whai ana oku hoariri i te ra roa nei, kia horomia ahau; he tokomaha nei hoki e whakahi ana, e whawhai mai ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:3">56:3</a> Ka whakawhirinaki ahau ki a koe i te wa e mataku ai ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:4">56:4</a> Ma te Atua ahau ka whakamoemiti ki tana kupu: e whakawhirinaki ana ahau ki te Atua, e kore ahau e wehi. He aha ta te kikokiko e mea ai ki ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:5">56:5</a> E whakariroia ketia ana e ratou aku kupu i nga ra katoa; heoi ano ta ratou e whakaaro ai ko te kino moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:6">56:6</a> E huihui ana ratou, e piri ana: e titiro matatau ana ki oku hikoinga, i a ratou e whanga nei ki toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:7">56:7</a> Ma te he koia ratou ka mawhiti ai? kia riri koe, e te Atua, whakataka iho hoki nga iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:8">56:8</a> ¶ E taua ana e koe oku kopikopikotanga: rongoatia oku roimata ki roto ki tau ipu: kahore ianei i tau pukapuka?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:9">56:9</a> I te ra e karanga ai ahau ka hoki whakamuri oku hoariri: e matau ana ahau ki tenei, kei ahau hoki te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:10">56:10</a> Ma te Atua ahau ka whakamoemiti ai ki tana kupu; ma Ihowa ahau ka whakamoemiti ai ki tana kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:11">56:11</a> E whakawhirinaki ana ahau ki te Atua: e kore ahau e wehi. He aha ta te tangata e mea ai ki ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:12">56:12</a> Kei ahau nga kupu taurangi ki a koe, e te Atua: me tuku e ahau nga whakamoemiti ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:13">56:13</a> Nau hoki toku wairua i whakaora kei mata: e kore ianei koe e whakau i oku waewae kei paheke, kia haere ai ahau i te aroaro o te Atua i roto i te marama o te hunga ora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:1">57:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Aratakiti. He Mikitama. Na Rawiri, i tona rerenga i a Haora i a ia nei i roto i te ana. Tohungia ahau, e te Atua, tohungia ahau, e whakawhirinaki ana hoki toku wairua ki a koe: ae, ka piri ahau ki raro ki te taumarumarut anga o ou pakau, kia pahemo ra ano enei mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:2">57:2</a> Ka karanga ahau ki te Atua, ki te Runga Rawa, ki te Atua e oti ai aku mea katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:3">57:3</a> Ka unga mai e ia he kaiwhakaora moku i te rangi, ina tawai te tangata e mea ana kia horomia ahau; (Hera.) ka unga mai e te Atua tana mahi tohu me tona pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:4">57:4</a> Kei waenganui toku wairua i nga raiona: e takoto ana ahau i waenganui i te hunga e kaia ana e te ahi; i nga tama hoki a te tangata, he tao nei o ratou niho, he pere, he hoari koi ano o ratou arero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:5">57:5</a> Kia whakanuia koe, e te Atua, ki runga ake i nga rangi: hei runga atu i te whenua katoa tou kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:6">57:6</a> Kua whakatakotoria e ratou he kupenga mo oku takahanga, kua piko toku wairua: kua keria e ratou he poka ki toku aroaro, a taka iho ko ratou ano ki roto. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:7">57:7</a> ¶ Pamau tonu toku ngakau, e te Atua, pumau tonu toku ngakau: ka waiata ahau, ae, ka himene ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:8">57:8</a> E ara, e toku kororia; e ara, e te hatere, e te hapa: ka ara wawe ano ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:9">57:9</a> Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe, e te Ariki, i waenganui i nga iwi; ka himene ki a koe i waenganui i nga tauiwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:10">57:10</a> He nui hoki tau mahi tohu, a tutuki noa ki nga rangi, me tou pono a tutuki noa ki nga kapua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:11">57:11</a> Kia whakanuia koe, e te Atua, ki runga i nga rangi: hei runga i te whenua katoa tou kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:1">58:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Aratakiti. He Mikitama. Na Rawiri. He korero puku ranei ta koutou i te pono? he tika ranei ta koutou whakarite, e nga tama a te tangata?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:2">58:2</a> He pono, e mahia ana e koutou te he i roto i te ngakau, e paunatia ana e koutou te tutu a o koutou ringa i runga i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:3">58:3</a> He tangata ke te hunga hara no te kopu mai ano; whanau kau kua kotiti ke, kua korero teka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:4">58:4</a> Ko to ratou paihana he rite ki to te nakahi, kei te neke turi e puru nei i tona taringa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:5">58:5</a> E kore nei e whakarongo ki te reo o te kaiwhakawai, ahakoa tino matau ia ki te whakawai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:6">58:6</a> ¶ Whatiia, e te Atua, o ratou niho i roto i o ratou mangai: kowhakia, e Ihowa, nga niho nunui o nga kuao raiona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:7">58:7</a> Kia mimiti ratou, ano he wai e heke atu ana: ka whakatikaia ana pere, kia rite ki te mea kua poutoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:8">58:8</a> Kia memeha haere, a kia pahure, ano he ngata: kia rite ki te mea mate roto a te wahine, kahore nei i kite i te ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:9">58:9</a> E kore e tukua kia rongo a koutou kohua i nga tataramoa, ka kahakina ratou e ia i roto i te awhiowhio, te mea kaiota, te mea e wera ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:10">58:10</a> Ka hari te tangata tika ua kite i te utu: ka horoia e ia ona waewae ki nga toto o te tangata hara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:11">58:11</a> A ka mea te tangata, Koia, ka whai utu te tangata tika: ina, he Atua ano tenei e whakawa ana i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:1">59:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Aratakiti. He Mikitama na Rawiri, i a Haora i tono tangata hei tiaki mo te whare, hei whakamate mona. Whakaorangia ahau, e toku Atua, i oku hoariri: whakateiteitia ake ahau i te hunga e whakatika ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:2">59:2</a> Whakaorangia ahau i nga kaimahi i te kino: kia ora ahau i te hunga toto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:3">59:3</a> Kei te whanga nei hoki ratou mo toku wairua: e whakamine ana te hunga kaha ki te whawhai ki ahau; kahore nei oku tutu, kahore oku hara, e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:4">59:4</a> Hore oku kino, oma ana ratou, kei te takatu: e ara hei awhina moku, titiro mai hoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:5">59:5</a> Ae ra, maranga, e Ihowa, e te Atua o nga mano, e te Atua o Iharaira, tirohia iho nga tauiwi katoa: kaua e tohungia tetahi o te hunga kino, e poka ke nei. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:6">59:6</a> Ka hoki mai ratou i te ahiahi, kei te tau, ano he kuri, taiawhiotia ana e ratou te pa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:7">59:7</a> Nana, kei te kupa o ratou mangai, he hoari kei o ratou ngutu: ki ta ratou, ko wai e rongo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:8">59:8</a> ¶ Ko tau ia, e Ihowa, he kata ki a ratou: hei tawainga mau nga tauiwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:9">59:9</a> E toku kaha, ka tatari ahau ki a koe: ko te Atua hoki toku pa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:10">59:10</a> Kei mua i ahau toku Atua aroha: ma te Atua ahau ka kite i taku i hiahia ai ki oku hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:11">59:11</a> Kaua ratou e whakamatea, kei wareware toku iwi: kia whakamararatia ratou e tou kaha; whakataka iho ratou, e te Ariki, e to matou whakangungu rakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:12">59:12</a> Mo te hara o to ratou mangai, mo nga kupu a o ratou ngutu, hopukia ratou i runga i to ratou whakakake, mo ta ratou korero, he kanga, he teka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:13">59:13</a> Whakamotitia i runga i te riri, kia kahore ai ratou: a kia matau ratou ko te Atua te Kawana o Hakopa puta noa ki nga pito o te whenua. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:14">59:14</a> I te ahiahi tukua ratou kia hoki, tukua ratou kia tau, ano he kuri, kia taiawhio ratou i te pa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:15">59:15</a> Ka kopikopiko noa ratou ki te rapu kai, a ka tauwhanga i te po roa ina kore ratou e makona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:16">59:16</a> Ko ahau ia, ka waiatatia e ahau tou kaha; ae, i te ata ka hamamatia e ahau tau mahi toku: ko koe hoki toku pa, toku piringa i te ra o toku pouri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:17">59:17</a> Ka himene ahau ki a koe, e toku kaha: ko te Atua nei hoki toku pa, toku Atua aroha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:1">60:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Huhana Erutu. He Mikitama, na Rawiri, hei whakaako. No tana whawhaitanga ki a Aramanaharaima raua ko Aramatopa. Na hoki ana a Ioapa, a patua ana e ia a Eroma ki te Raorao Tote, kotahi tekau ma rua mano. E te Atua, kua pa nga matou e koe, kua oti matou te whakamarara e koe, kua riri koe; tahuri mai ano ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:2">60:2</a> Wiri ana te whenua i a koe: kua ngatata i a koe: whakakapia ona wahi pakaru; e ru ana hoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:3">60:3</a> He mea pakeke kua whakakitea e koe ki tau iwi, kua oti matou te whakainu e koe ki te waina e wiri ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:4">60:4</a> Kua homai e koe he kara ki te hunga e wehi ana i a koe: kia whakakitea hei mea mo te pono. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:5">60:5</a> Hei mea e mawhiti ai au e aroha ai: ma tou matau e whakaora, whakahokia mai hoki he kupu ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:6">60:6</a> ¶ Kua korero te Atua i runga i tona tapu; ka hari ahau, ka kotikoti i Hekeme, ka roherohe hoki i te raorao o Hukota.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:7">60:7</a> Noku Kireara, noku ano a Manahi, ko Eparaima ano hoki te kaha o toku matenga; ko Hura taku kaiwhakatakoto ture;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:8">60:8</a> Ko Moapa taku oko horoi; ka maka e ahau toku hu ki runga ki Eroma: e Pirihitia, ko ahau hei whakamanamana mau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:9">60:9</a> Ma wai ahau e kawe ki te pa kaha? Na wai ahau i arahi ki Eroma?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:10">60:10</a> He teka ranei, e te Atua, kua panga matou e koe? kahore hoki koe, e te Atua, e haere tahi me a matou taua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:11">60:11</a> Homai he awhina mo matou ki o matou hoariri: he teka noa hoki te awhina a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:12">60:12</a> Ma te Atua tatou ka toa ai: mana hoki e takahi ki raro o tatou hoa whawhai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:1">61:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Nekina. Na Rawiri. Whakarongo, e te Atua, ki taku karanga: tahuri mai ki taku inoi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:2">61:2</a> Ka karanga ahau ki a koe i te pito o te whenua, ina pehia toku ngakau: arahina ahau ki te kohatu e tiketike ake ana i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:3">61:3</a> He piringa hoki koe moku: he pa kaha i te hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:4">61:4</a> Ka noho ahau ki tou tapenakara ake ake, ka okioki ki ou pakau hei piringa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:5">61:5</a> ¶ Kua rongo nei hoki koe, e te Atua, i aku kupu tauranga kua homai e koe te wahi o te hunga e wehi ana ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:6">61:6</a> Ka whakaraneatia e koe nga ra o te kingi; ona tau ki nga whakatupuranga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:7">61:7</a> E noho ia i te aroaro o te Atua ake ake: whakaritea mai he aroha, he pono, hei tiaki i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:8">61:8</a> Penei ka himene ahau ki tou ingoa ake ake: ka whakamana e ahau aku kupu taurangi i tenei ra, i tenei ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:1">62:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ki a Ierutonu. He himene na Rawiri. Ko te Atua anake taku e tatari nei: kei a ia te whakaoranga moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:2">62:2</a> Ko ia anake toku kohatu, toku whakaoranga, toku pa hoki, e kore e nui toku ngaueuetanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:3">62:3</a> Kia pehea te roa o ta koutou tatau ki te tangata, kia whakamatea ai e koutou, e koutou katoa, ka rite ki te taiepa e tungou ana, ki te wawa ka tata te hinga?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:4">62:4</a> Heoi ano ta ratou e runanga ai ko te turaki i a ia i tona wahi teitei: e ahuareka ana ki te teka; e manaaki ana o ratou mangai, a e kanga ana a roto i a ratou. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:5">62:5</a> Tatari, e toku wairua, ki te Atua anaki; ko ia taku e tumanako nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:6">62:6</a> Ko ia anake toku kohatu, toku whakaoranga, toku pa hoki; e kore ahau e whakangaueuetia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:7">62:7</a> Kei te Atua te whakaoranga moku, te kororia ano moku; kei te Atua te kohatu o toku kaha, toku piringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:8">62:8</a> ¶ Whakawhirinaki ki a ia i nga wa katoa, e te iwi, ringihia to koutou ngakau ki tona aroaro: hei piringa mo tatou te Atua (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:9">62:9</a> He pono he mea memeha noa nga ware, he teka noa nga rangatira; ki te paunatia ratou, mama noa ake ratou tahi i te horihori.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:10">62:10</a> Kaua e whakawhirinaki ki te tukino, kei wairangi hoki ki te pahua: ki te tini haere nga taonga, kei whakamanawa to koutou ngakau ki reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:11">62:11</a> Kotahi korerotanga a te Atua, ka rua oku rongonga i tenei, no te Atua te kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:12">62:12</a> Nau ano, e te Ariki, te mahi tohu: rite tonu hoki ki tana mahi tau utu ki te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:1">63:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri, i a ia i te koraha o Hura. E te Atua, noku koe Atua; ka moata taku rapu i a koe. E hiainu ana toku wairua ki a koe, e hiahia ana oku kikokiko ki a koe, i te whenua maroke, ruha noa, kahore nei he wai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:2">63:2</a> Koia i titiro atu ai ahau ki a koe i te wahi tapu, kia kite ai i tou kaha, i tou kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:3">63:3</a> ¶ Pai atu tou aroha i te ora: mo reira ka whakamoemiti oku ngutu ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:4">63:4</a> Ina, ka whakapai ahau ki a koe i ahau ano e ora nei; ka totoro atu oku ringa i runga i tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:5">63:5</a> Ka makona toku wairua, ano i te hinu wheua, i te ngako, a ka hari oku ngutu ina whakamoemiti toku mangai ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:6">63:6</a> Ina mahara ahau ki a koe i runga i toku moenga, ina whakaaro ki a koe i nga mataaratanga o te po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:7">63:7</a> ¶ Ko koe hoki toku kaiawhina: na ka hari ahau ki te taumarumarutanga iho o ou pakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:8">63:8</a> Piri tonu toku wairua ki a koe: e tautoko ake ana tou matau i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:9">63:9</a> Ko te hunga e whai ana i toku wairua kia whakangaromia, ka riro ratou ki nga wahi o raro rawa o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:10">63:10</a> Ka tukua atu ratou ki te kaha o te hoari: hei wahi ratou ma nga pokiha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:11">63:11</a> Tena ko te kingi, ka hari ia ki te Atua; ka whakamanamana nga tangata katoa ko ia nei ta ratou oati: a ka purua te mangai o te hunga katoa e korero teka ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:1">64:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. Whakarongo ki toku reo, e te Atua, ina inoi atu ahau: tiakina toku ora i te wehi o te hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:2">64:2</a> Huna ahau i te whakaaro ngaro o te hunga kino, i te ngangau a nga kaimahi i te he;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:3">64:3</a> Kua whakakoi nei i o ratou arero, ano he hoari, kua whakatika nei i a ratou pere, ara i nga kupu kikino,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:4">64:4</a> Hei koperenga pukutanga ma ratou ki te tangata tika; kitea rawatia ake kua kopere ki a ia, kahore hoki he wehi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:5">64:5</a> E whakamaia ana ratou i a ratou ano ki te mea kino; e runanga ana kia whakatakotoria pukutia he rore, e mea ana, Ko wai e kite i a ratou?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:6">64:6</a> E rapu hara ana ratou; e mea ana, Kua ata rapu marie tatou: taea noatia te hohonutanga o te whakaaro o ia tangata, a ko te ngakau he hohonu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:7">64:7</a> ¶ Ma te Atua ia e kopere he pere ki a ratou kitea rawatia ake kua tu ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:8">64:8</a> Heoi ka meinga ratou kia tapatu, ko to ratou arero ake ano ka tu atu ki a ratou; a ka ruru i to ratou matenga te hunga katoa e kite i a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:9">64:9</a> Ka wehi ano hoki nga tangata katoa, ka whakapuaki i te mahi a te Atua: ka ata maharatia hoki e ratou tana mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:10">64:10</a> Ka koa te tangata tika ki a Ihowa, ka whakawhirinaki hoki ki a ia: ka whakamanamana ano te hunga ngakau tika katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:1">65:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene, he waiata na Rawiri. E taria ana koe, e te Atua, e te whakamoemiti i Hiona: a ka whakamana te kupu taurangi ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:2">65:2</a> E te kaiwhakarongo inoi, e haere nga kikokiko katoa ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:3">65:3</a> E kaha ake ana i ahau nga kino: a matou mahi tutu, mau ena e hipoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:4">65:4</a> Ka hari te tangata e whiriwhiria e koe, e meatia e koe kia tata atu ki a koe, kia noho i roto i ou marae: ka makona matou i te pai o tou whare, o tou temepara tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:5">65:5</a> He mea whakawehi, he tapu, tau utu kupu ki a matou, e te Atua o to matou whakaoranga, e te okiokinga o nga pito katoa o te whenua, o te hunga hoki i tawhiti i runga o te moana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:6">65:6</a> ¶ E whakau nei i nga maunga, he kaha hoki nona; tona whitiki nei he kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:7">65:7</a> E whakamarie nei i te haruru o nga moana, i te haruru o o ratou ngaru, i te ngangau hoki o nga iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:8">65:8</a> Ka wehi ano ki au tohu te hunga e noho ana i nga pito rawa: hari ana i a koe nga putake o te ata, o te ahiahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:9">65:9</a> E tirotirohia ana e koe te whenua, e whakamakukuria ana, e whakamomonatia nuitia ana e koe; ki tonu te awa o te Atua i te wai: oti rawa ake te whakapai e koe, kua rite mai i a koe he witi mo aua wahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:10">65:10</a> Makuku rawa i a koe ona moa, pe ana i a koe ona tupuke: e whakangawaritia ana e koe ki nga ua: e manaakitia ana e koe tona pihinga ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:11">65:11</a> E karaunatia ana e koe te tau ki tou pai; e maturuturu ana hoki te momonatanga o ou ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:12">65:12</a> E maturuturu ana ki nga wahi kai o te koraha: a whitikiria ana nga pukepuke ki te koa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:13">65:13</a> He hipi te kakahu o nga wahi kai; ngaro ana nga raorao i te witi; hamama ana ratou i te hari, waiata ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:1">66:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene, he waiata. Hamama, e te whenua katoa, ki te Atua:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:2">66:2</a> Himenetia te kororia o tona ingoa, kia whai kororia te whakamoemiti ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:3">66:3</a> Mea atu ki te Atua, Ano te wehi o au mahi! Ma te nui o tou kaha e ngohengohe ai ou hoariri ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:4">66:4</a> E koropiko katoa te whenua ki a koe; ka himene ki a koe; ka himene ratou ki tou ingoa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:5">66:5</a> Haere mai kia kite i nga mahi a te Atua: mataku rawa tana mahi ki nga tama a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:6">66:6</a> Nana i mea te moana hei tuawhenua: haere a waewae ana ratou ra roto i te awa; hari ana matou ki a ia i reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:7">66:7</a> Ko tona kawanatanga tuturu tonu i runga i tona kaha; e titiro ana ona kanohi ki nga tauiwi; kei whakakake te hunga tutu. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:8">66:8</a> ¶ Whakapaingia to tatou Atua, e nga iwi; kia rangona te reo whakamoemiti ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:9">66:9</a> Nana nei hoki i mau ai to tatou wairua ki te ora, kahore hoki e tukua e ia o tatou waewae kia nekehia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:10">66:10</a> Kua whakamatauria hoki matou e koe, e te Atua: whakarewaia ana matou e koe, ano he hiriwa e whakarewaia ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:11">66:11</a> Kua kawea nei matou e koe ki roto ki te kupenga: whakapikaua ana e koe te mea whakamamae ki o matou hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:12">66:12</a> I meinga ano e koe o matou upoko kia ekengia hoihotia e te tangata; i ra roto matou i te kapura, i te wai: heoi whakaputaina mai ana matou e koe ki te wahi momona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:13">66:13</a> ¶ Ka tomo ahau me nga tahunga tinana ki tou whare; ka whakamana ahau i aku kupu taurangi ki a koe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:14">66:14</a> Era i puaki i oku ngutu, i korerotia e toku mangai i ahau e pouri ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:15">66:15</a> Ka whakaekea e ahau mau nga mea momona hei tahunga tinana, ngatahi ano me te mea kakara o nga hipi toa; ka tukua e ahau he puru, he koati. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:16">66:16</a> Haere mai, whakarongo, e koutou katoa e wehi ana ki te Atua, a maku e whakapuaki tana i mea ai ki toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:17">66:17</a> I tangi toku mangai ki a ia: i whakanuia ano ia e toku arero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:18">66:18</a> Ki te whakaaroa e toku ngakau te he, e kore te Ariki e whakarongo mai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:19">66:19</a> Nei ra he pono kua whakarongo te Atua, kua tahuri ia ki toku reo inoi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:20">66:20</a> Kia whakapaingia te Atua, kihai nei i whakapeau ke i taku inoi, i tana atawhai hoki ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:1">67:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Nekinoto. He himene, he waiata. Ma te Atua tatou e atawhai, mana tatou e manaaki; mana e mea kia tiaho tona mata ki a tatou; (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:2">67:2</a> Kia matauria ai tau ara ki runga ki te whenua, tau whakaoranga i roto i nga tauiwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:3">67:3</a> Kia whakamoemiti nga iwi ki a koe, e te Atua, kia whakamoemiti nga iwi katoa ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:4">67:4</a> Kia koa nga tauiwi, kia waiata i te hari: no te mea ka tika tau whakawa mo nga iwi, a ka kawana koe i nga tauiwi o te whenua. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:5">67:5</a> Kia whakamoemiti nga iwi ki a koe, e te Atua, kia whakamoemiti nga iwi katoa ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:6">67:6</a> Kua tuku mai nei te whenua i ona hua; a ka manaaki te Atua, to tatou Atua, i a tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:7">67:7</a> Ka manaaki te Atua i a tatou; a ka wehi nga pito katoa o te whenua i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:1">68:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene, he waiata na Rawiri. Kia ara te Atua, kia marara ona hoariri: kia whati hoki i tona aroaro te hunga e kino ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:2">68:2</a> Aia atu ratou, peratia me te paowa e aia ana: kia rite ki te ware pi e rewa ana i te kapura te ngaromanga o te hunga kino i te aroaro o te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:3">68:3</a> Kia koa ia te hunga tika; kia hari i te aroaro o te Atua: ae ra, kia tino hari pu ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:4">68:4</a> Waiata ki te Atua, himenetia tona ingoa; opehia ake he huanui mo tana hariata i nga koraha; tona ingoa ko IHA; kia hari hoki ki tona aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:5">68:5</a> Hei matua mo nga pani, hei kaiwhakarite mo nga pouaru, te Atua i tona nohoanga tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:6">68:6</a> E whakanohoia ana e te Atua te mokemoke ki te whare; e whakaputaina ana e ia nga herehere ki te ora: ko te hunga tutu ia e noho i te wahi waikore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:7">68:7</a> ¶ E te Atua, i tou haerenga atu i mua i tau iwi: i tou haerenga i te koraha; (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:8">68:8</a> I wiri te whenua, i tuturu iho ano nga rangi i te aroaro o te Atua; me taua Hinai ano i te aroaro o te Atua, o te Atua o Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:9">68:9</a> I taia mai, e koe, e te Atua, he ua nui; a i tou kainga e ruwha ana ka whakaukia e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:10">68:10</a> I noho tau whakaminenga ki reira: na tou pai, e te Atua, i mea kai ai koe ma nga rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:11">68:11</a> Ka homai e Ihowa te kupu: he ope nui nga wahine whakapuaki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:12">68:12</a> Whati rawa nga kingi o nga taua: a ko te wahine i noho i te whare, kei te tuwha i nga parakete.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:13">68:13</a> I a koutou ka takoto noa i nga takotoranga hipi, he rite ki nga pakau o te kukupa kua paparuatia nei ki te hiriwa, ona hou ki te koura whero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:14">68:14</a> I te whakamararatanga a te Kaha Rawa i nga kingi i reira, koia ano kei te hukarere o Taramono te ma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:15">68:15</a> ¶ He maunga Atua a Maunga Pahana; he maunga tiketike a Maunga Pahana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:16">68:16</a> He aha koutou ka titiro titaha ai, e nga maunga tiketike, ki te maunga i hiahiatia nei e te Atua kia nohoia e ia? ae, ka nohoia e Ihowa ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:17">68:17</a> Ko nga hariata a te Atua, e rua tekau mano, mano mano iho; kei roto i a ratou te Ariki, me te mea ko Hinai, ko te wahi tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:18">68:18</a> Kua kake koe ki runga, kua whakaraua e koe te whakarau: kua riro i a koe he ohaoha mo te tangata; ae, mo te hunga tutu ano, kia noho ai a Ihowa, te Atua ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:19">68:19</a> Kia whakapaingia te Ariki, e whakawaha nei i ta tatou pikaunga i tenei ra, i tenei ra, te Atua o to tatou whakaoranga. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:20">68:20</a> Ko to tatou Atua te Atua o te whakaoranga: na Ihowa ano, na te Ariki, nga putanga ake i te mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:21">68:21</a> Ka maru ia i te Atua te matenga o ona hoariri: me te tumuaki huruhuru o te tangata e haere tonu ana i ana kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:22">68:22</a> ¶ I mea te Ariki, Ka whakahokia mai e ahau i Pahana, ka whakahokia mai e ahau taku iwi i nga rire o te moana:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:23">68:23</a> Kia toua ai tou waewae ki te toto, kia whiwhi ai te arero o au kuri ki tana wahi o ou hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:24">68:24</a> I kite ratou, e te Atua, i ou haerenga, i nga haerenga o toku Atua, o toku Kingi, i te wahi tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:25">68:25</a> Ko nga kaiwaiata i haere i mua, i muri ko nga kaiwhakatangi, i waenganui o nga kotiro e patupatu ana i nga timipera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:26">68:26</a> Whakapaingia te Atua i roto i nga whakaminenga, te Ariki hoki, e nga mea i puta mai i te matapuna o Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:27">68:27</a> Kei reira a Pineamine, te whakaotinga, to ratou ariki, nga rangatira o Hura, me to ratou ropu, nga rangatira o Hepurona, me nga rangatira o Napatari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:28">68:28</a> Kua oti he kaha mou te whakahau iho e tou Atua: whakaukia, e te Atua, tau i mea ai mo matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:29">68:29</a> Ka maua mai e nga kingi he hakari ki a koe, mo tou temepara i Hiruharama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:30">68:30</a> Riria te kirehe o nga kakaho, te huinga puru, me nga kuao kau a nga iwi, me te takahi i nga pihi hiriwa ki raro: whakamararatia nga iwi e ahuareka ana ki te whainga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:31">68:31</a> E puta mai nga rangatira i Ihipa: meake hohoro te totoro o nga ringa o Etiopia ki te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:32">68:32</a> ¶ Waiata ki te Atua, e nga rangatiratanga o te whenua: himene ki te Ariki: (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:33">68:33</a> Ki a ia, ko tona hariata nei ko nga rangi o nga rangi, nonamata: na, ka puaki tona reo, he reo kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:34">68:34</a> Waiho te kaha i te Atua, kei runga nei i a Iharaira tana mahi rangatira: kei nga kapua hoki tona kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:35">68:35</a> Ka wehingia koe, e te Atua, i roto i ou wahi tapu: ko te Atua o Iharaira te kaihomai i te kaha, i te mana, ki tona iwi. Whakapaingia te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:1">69:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Hohanimi. Na Rawiri. Whakaorangia ahau e te Atua, ka tae mai hoki nga wai ki roto ki toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:2">69:2</a> Ka tapoko ahau ki te oru hohonu, ki te wahi kahore nei he tunga: kua tae ahau ki nga wai hohonu, ngaro iho ahau i nga waipuke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:3">69:3</a> Kua ruwha ahau i taku tangi; kua maroke toku korokoro: pakoko kau oku kanohi i ahau e tatari nei ki toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:4">69:4</a> Tini ke i nga makawe o toku matenga te hunga e kino noa ana ki ahau: he kaha rawa te hunga e mauahara noa ana ki ahau, e mea nei kia whakamatea ahau; utua ana e ahau i reira nga mea kihai i tangohia e ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:5">69:5</a> E te Atua, e matau ana koe ki toku kuware; kahore hoki oku he e ngaro i a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:6">69:6</a> E te Ariki, e Ihowa o nga mano kaua te hunga e tatari ana ki a koe e whakama i ahau: e te Atua o Iharaira, kei numinumi kau i ahau te hunga e rapu ana i a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:7">69:7</a> Mou hoki ahau i waiho ai hei tawainga: ngaro iho toku mata i te whakama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:8">69:8</a> He tangata ke ahau ki oku hoa ake: hei tautangata ki nga tama a toku whaea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:9">69:9</a> Ka pau hoki ahau i te aroha ki tou whare: kua tau ano ki ahau nga tawai a te hunga e tawai ana ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:10">69:10</a> I ahau i tangi, i whakatiki hei whiu i toku wairua, ka waiho tena hei tawainga moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:11">69:11</a> I kakahu hoki ahau i te kakahu taratara moku, a i waiho hei whakatauki ma ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:12">69:12</a> Kei te korero kino moku te hunga e noho ana i te kuwaha: waiatatia ana ahau e te hunga haurangi waina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:13">69:13</a> ¶ Ko ahau ia, ki a koe taku inoi, e Ihowa, i te wa e manakohia ai: whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau, e te Atua, i runga i te nui o tou aroha, o te pono o tau whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:14">69:14</a> Whakaorangia ahau i roto i te oru, kei toremi: kia ora ahau i te hunga e kino ana ki ahau, i nga wai hohonu ano hoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:15">69:15</a> Kei ngaro ahau i te waipuke, kei horomia e te rire; kei kopia ano te waha o te poka ki runga ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:16">69:16</a> E Ihowa whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau; he pai hoki tou atawhai: tahuri mai ki ahau, kia rite ki te nui o au arohatanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:17">69:17</a> A kaua e huna tou mata ki tau pononga; e pouri ana hoki ahau: hohoro te whakahoki kupu mai ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:18">69:18</a> Whakatata mai ki toku wairua, hokona: whakaorangia ahau, e mahi nei oku hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:19">69:19</a> E matau ana koe ki toku tawainga, ki toku whakama, ki toku numinumi: kei tou aroaro oku hoariri katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:20">69:20</a> Maru noa toku ngakau i te tawai; a ki tonu ahau i te pouri: i titiro ahau ki tetahi hei aroha mai, a kore ake; ki etahi hei whakamarie, a kihai i kitea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:21">69:21</a> I homai he au hei kai maku: i toku matewaitanga ano i whakainumia ahau ki te winika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:22">69:22</a> ¶ Kia meinga ta ratou tepu i to ratou aroaro hei mahanga; hei rore hoki i to ratou wa rangimarie.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:23">69:23</a> Kia whakapouritia o ratou kanohi, kei kite ratou: kia wiri tonu hoki o ratou hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:24">69:24</a> Ringihia atu tou riri ki runga ki a ratou, kia mau hoki ratou i tou arita, i tou weriweri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:25">69:25</a> Kia ururuatia to ratou nohoanga: kaua tetahi e noho ki o ratou teneti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:26">69:26</a> Mo ratou i tukino i te tangata i whiua nei e koe; a korerotia ana e ratou te pouri o te hunga i werohia e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:27">69:27</a> Tapiritia he kino ki runga ki to ratou kino; kaua hoki ratou e tukua kia tomo ki tou tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:28">69:28</a> Kia murua atu ratou i te pukapuka o te ora, kaua ano e tuhituhia ki roto ki te hunga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:29">69:29</a> Ko ahau ia, he rawakore, he pouri; kia whakateiteitia ake ahau, e te Atua, e tau whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:30">69:30</a> ¶ Ka whakamoemiti taku waiata ki te ingoa o te Atua, ka whakanui ano taku whakawhetai i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:31">69:31</a> Pai rawa tenei ki a Ihowa i te puru i te kau, i te mea whai haona, whai maikuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:32">69:32</a> Kua kite te hunga mahaki, kua hari: ka ora ano o koutou ngakau, e te hunga e rapu nei i te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:33">69:33</a> No te mea ka rongo a Ihowa ki nga rawakore, e kore ano e whakahawea ki ana herehere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:34">69:34</a> Kia whakamoemiti te rangi me te whenua ki a ia, nga moana, me nga mea katoa e tere ana i roto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:35">69:35</a> No te mea tera e whakaorangia e te Atua a Hiona, ka hanga ano e ia nga pa o Hura; a ka noho ratou ki reira, ka riro hoki a reira i a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:36">69:36</a> A ka nohoia a reira e nga uri o ana pononga: hei kainga tupu ano a reira mo te hunga e aroha ana ki tona ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:1">70:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Na Rawiri, hei whakamahara. Kia hohoro, e te Atua, ki te whakaora i ahau: e Ihowa, hohoro ki te awhina i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:2">70:2</a> Kia whakama, kia pororaru ngatahi te hunga e rapu ana i toku wairua: kia whakahokia ki muri, kia whakama te hunga e hiahia ana kia he ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:3">70:3</a> Kia whakahokia ki muri mo to ratou whakama, te hunga e mea ana ki ahau, Ha, ha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:4">70:4</a> Kia hari, kia koa, ki a koe te hunga katoa e rapu ana i a koe; kia mea tonu te hunga e pai ana ki tau whakaoranga, Kia whakanuia te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:5">70:5</a> Ko ahau ia, he iti, he rawakore; hohoro mai, e te Atua, ki ahau: ko koe toku awhina, toku kaiwhakaora; kaua ra e whakaroa, e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:1">71:1</a> ¶ Ko koe taku e whakawhirinaki ai, e Ihowa: kei whakama ahau ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:2">71:2</a> Whakaorangia ahau, i runga i tou tika, kia mawhiti ano ahau: tahuri mai tou taringa ki ahau, whakaorangia hoki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:3">71:3</a> Kia ai koe hei teko e noho ai ahau, hei hokihokinga tonutanga atu moku: kua kiia iho ahau e koe kia whakaorangia: ko koe nei hoki toku kohatu, toku pourewa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:4">71:4</a> Whakaorangia ahau, e toku Atua, i te ringa o te tangata kino, i te ringa o te whanoke, o te nanakia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:5">71:5</a> Ko koe nei hoki, e te Ariki, e Ihowa, taku e tumanako atu nei, taku e whakawhirinaki nei no toku tamarikitanga ake ano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:6">71:6</a> Nau ahau i tautoko ake no te kopu mai ano; nau ahau i tango mai i roto i nga whekau o toku whaea; ko koe taku e whakamoemiti tonu ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:7">71:7</a> He miharotanga ahau na te tini; ko koe ia toku piringa kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:8">71:8</a> Kia ki toku mangai i te whakamoemiti ki a koe, i tou honore i te roa o te ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:9">71:9</a> Kaua ahau e panga a te wa o te koroheketanga, kaua ahau e whakarerea ina hemo toku kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:10">71:10</a> E korerotia ana hoki ahau e oku hoariri, a e runanga tahi ana te hunga e whanga ana ki toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:11">71:11</a> E mea ana, Kua whakarerea ia e te Atua: whaia, hopukia; kahore hoki tetahi hei whakaora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:12">71:12</a> E te Atua, kei matara atu koe i ahau: e toku Atua, hohoro ki te awhina i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:13">71:13</a> Kia whakama, kia pau nga hoariri o toku wairua: kia hipokina ki te tawai, ki te whakama, te hunga e rapu ana i te he moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:14">71:14</a> ¶ Ko ahau ia, ka tumanako tonu: ka hono tonu ano te whakamoemiti ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:15">71:15</a> Ma toku mangai e whakakite tou tika, tau whakaoranga i te roa o te ra; kahore hoki ahau e mohio e hia ranei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:16">71:16</a> Ka haere ahau i runga i te kaha o te Ariki, o Ihowa, ka whakahuatia e ahau tou tika, tou anake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:17">71:17</a> E te Atua, he mea whakaako ahau nau, no toku tamarikitanga ake; a he whakapuaki taku i au mahi whakamiharo a mohoa noa nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:18">71:18</a> Na kaua ahau e whakarerea, e te Atua, a koroheke noa, hina noa ahau, kia whakakitea ra ano e ahau tou kaha ki tenei whakatupuranga, tou nui ki nga tangata katoa e puta mai a mua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:19">71:19</a> Kei runga rawa ano tou tika, e te Atua, he nui nei hoki au mahi: e te Atua, ko wai te rite ki a koe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:20">71:20</a> He nui, he kino nga pouritanga ngakau i whakakitea mai e koe ki a matou; tera ano koe ka whakahauora i a matou, ka whakahoki ake ano i a matou i nga wahi hohonu o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:21">71:21</a> Whakaraneatia e koe toku nui, a tahuri mai ano ka whakamarie i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:22">71:22</a> Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe i runga i te hatere, ara ki tou pono, e toku Atua: ka himene ahau ki a koe i runga i te hapa, e te Mea Tapu o Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:23">71:23</a> Ka tino hari oku ngutu ua himene ahau ki a koe: me toku wairua ano i hokona nei e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:24">71:24</a> Ka korerotia hoki e toku arero tou tika i te roa o te ra: kua whakama nei hoki, kua numinumi kau te hunga i rapu i te he moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:1">72:1</a> ¶ Na Horomona. Homai, e te Atua, au whakaritenga ki te kingi, me tou tika ki te tama a te kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:2">72:2</a> ¶ Mana e whakawa tou iwi i runga i te tika, au rawakore i runga i te whakawa tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:3">72:3</a> Ka kawea mai e nga maunga te rongo mau ki te iwi, e nga pukepuke i runga i te tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:4">72:4</a> Ka whakawa ia mo nga ware o te iwi: ka whakaorangia e ia nga tamariki a te rawakore; mongamonga noa i a ia te kaitukino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:5">72:5</a> I te ra e mau ana, i te marama hoki, ka pera te mau o to ratou wehi ki a koe i nga whakatupuranga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:6">72:6</a> E heke iho ia ano he ua ki runga ki te kotinga tarutaru, me nga ua e whakamakuku nei i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:7">72:7</a> Ka tupu te tangata tika i ona ra: tona roa ano o te ata noho, a kore noa te marama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:8">72:8</a> Ka kingi ia i tenei moana, a tae noa ki tetahi moana, i te awa, a nga pito atu ano o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:9">72:9</a> Ka piko ki tona aroaro te hunga o te koraha: a ka mitimiti ona hoariri i te puehu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:10">72:10</a> Ka maua mai he hakari e nga kingi o Tarahihi, o nga motu: ka kawea mai he tahua e nga kingi o Hepa, o Tepa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:11">72:11</a> Ae, ka koropiko nga kingi katoa ki a ia: ka mahi nga iwi katoa ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:12">72:12</a> Ka ora hoki i a ia te rawakore ua tangi atu, te ware hoki me te tangata kahore nei ona kaiawhina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:13">72:13</a> E tohu ia i te tangata iti, i te rawakore; ka ora ano i a ia nga wairua o nga rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:14">72:14</a> Ka hokona e ia to ratou wairua i roto i te tukino, i te tutu, he mea utu nui hoki o ratou toto ki tana titiro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:15">72:15</a> A e ora ratou; ka hoatu ano ki a ia he koura no Hepa: ka tukua tonutia hoki te inoi mona; ka whakapaingia ia i tenei ra, i tenei ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:16">72:16</a> He kutanga witi tera i runga i te whenua, i te tihi o nga maunga; ngarue ana ona hua, ano ko Repanona, a ka rite te tupu o nga tangata o te pa ki to te tarutaru o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:17">72:17</a> Ka mau tonu tona ingoa ake ake; ka rite tona ingoa ki te ra te pumau: kei roto i a ia te manaaki mo te tangata; ka korerotia tona koa e nga iwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:18">72:18</a> ¶ Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, te Atua, te Atua o Iharaira: ko ia nei anake hei mahi i nga mahi whakamiharo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:19">72:19</a> Kia whakapaingia ano tona ingoa kororia mo ake tonu atu; kia ki katoa hoki te whenua i tona kororia. Amine, ae Amine.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:20">72:20</a> Ko te mutunga tenei o nga inoi a Rawiri, a te tama a Hehe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:1">73:1</a> ¶ He himene na Ahapa. He pono, he pai te Atua ki a Iharaira; ki te hunga ngakau ma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:2">73:2</a> Ko ahau ia, wahi iti kua tapepa oku waewae: me i kotahi kua paheke oku takahanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:3">73:3</a> I hae hoki ahau ki te hunga whakahi, i toku kitenga i te tangata hara e kake ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:4">73:4</a> Kahore hoki he whakawiringa a te mate i a ratou: he maro ano o ratou uaua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:5">73:5</a> Kahore nga mea whakapouri tangata e pa ki a ratou; kahore ano ratou e whiua tahitia me te mano tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:6">73:6</a> Na reira, ano he hei te whakakake e awhi nei i a ratou, ano he kakahu te tutu e hipokina nei ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:7">73:7</a> Pupuhi ana o ratou kanohi i te ngako: nui ake nga mea i a ratou i a o ratou ngakau i hiahia ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:8">73:8</a> E whakahi ana ratou, e korero kino ana mo te whakatoi: kei runga noa ake a ratou korero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:9">73:9</a> Tutuki tonu to ratou mangai ki nga rangi: e kopikopiko ana hoki to ratou arero i runga i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:10">73:10</a> Koia tona iwi i hoki mai ai ki konei: a e whakawiria ana he wai mo ratou, ki tonu te kapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:11">73:11</a> E mea ana ratou, Ma te aha e matau ai te Atua? He matauranga koia to te Runga Rawa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:12">73:12</a> Nana, ko te hunga kino tenei, kei runga tonu i te whenua rangatira, e hua ana o ratou taonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:13">73:13</a> He pono he maumau taku mea i toku ngakau kia ma, taku horoi hoki i oku ringa ki te harakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:14">73:14</a> E whiua ana hoki ahau i te roa o te ra, e pakia ana i nga ata katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:15">73:15</a> ¶ Me i ki ahau, Ka penei taku korero; na e tinihanga ana ahau ki te whakatupuranga o au tamariki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:16">73:16</a> I taku meatanga kia matauria tenei, ka kite ahau he mahi whakauaua rawa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:17">73:17</a> Tae noa ahau ki te wahi tapu o te Atua, katahi ahau ka mohio ki to ratou mutunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:18">73:18</a> He pono i whakaturia ratou e koe ki nga wahi pahekeheke; a whakataka ana e koe ki te ngaromanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:19">73:19</a> Ano te panga whakareretanga o to ratou hunanga! kua pau rawa i nga wehi.</p>
