 <p><a name="an_73:20">73:20</a> Ka rite ki te rekanga kanohi, ina ara ake te tangata, tau whakahawea ki to ratou ahua, e te Ariki, ina ara ake koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:21">73:21</a> ¶ Na mamae noa iho toku ngakau, a hukihuki ana oku whatumanawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:22">73:22</a> He whakaarokore hoki ahau, he kuware: me te mea he kirehe ahau i tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:23">73:23</a> Ahakoa ra kei a koe tonu ahau; e puritia ana e koe toku ringa matau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:24">73:24</a> Ma tou whakaaro ahau e arahi; muri iho ka riro ahau i a koe ki te kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:25">73:25</a> Ko wai hoki toku i te rangi ko koe anake? Kahore atu hoki oku i te whenua e hiahia ai, ko koe anake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:26">73:26</a> Hemo iho oku kikokiko me toku ngakau: ko te Atua ia te kaha o toku ngakau, toku wahi ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:27">73:27</a> Na, ko te hunga e mamao atu ana i a koe ka mate: ka ngaro i a koe te hunga puremu katoa e whakarere nei i a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:28">73:28</a> Ko ahau ia, he pai ki ahau te whakatata ki te Atua: kua waiho e ahau te Ariki, a Ihowa, hei whakawhirinakitanga moku, kia whakapuakina ai e ahau au mahi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:1">74:1</a> ¶ He Makiri na Ahapa. E te Atua, he aha i panga ai matou e koe ake ake? He aha i pongere ai tou riri ki nga hipi o tau mara?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:2">74:2</a> Mahara ki tau whakaminenga i hokona e koe i mua, i utua e koe hei iwi mo tou kainga tupu; a ki tenei Maunga Hiona i nohoia nei e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:3">74:3</a> Hiki ake ou waewae ki nga whakangaromanga e mau tonu nei, ki nga mahi kino katoa a te hoariri ki te wahi tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:4">74:4</a> Kua hamama nei ou hoariri i waenganui i au whakaminenga, kua whakaturia e ratou a ratou kara hei tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:5">74:5</a> E rite ana ratou ki nga tangata e hapai ana i te titaha ki te puia rakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:6">74:6</a> Inaianei ia e tukitukia ana e ratou ona mea whakairo, pakaruhia iho ana ki te titaha, ki te hama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:7">74:7</a> Kua toua tou wahi tapu ki te kapura, kua noa i a ratou te nohoanga o tou ingoa, kei te whenua e takoto ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:8">74:8</a> I mea to ratou ngakau, Me whakangaro ratou a poto ake: kua tahuna e ratou nga whare huihui katoa o te Atua i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:9">74:9</a> Kahore matou e kite i o matou tohu, kahore atu he poropiti, kahore hoki tetahi o matou e matau ana kia pehea ake te roa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:10">74:10</a> E te Atua, kia pehea ake te roa o te tawai a te hoariri? Ka kohukohu tonu ranei te hoariri ki tou ingoa ake ake?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:11">74:11</a> He aha i pepeke ai tou ringa, tou matau? Unuhia i roto i tou uma, whakamotitia ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:12">74:12</a> ¶ Ko te Atua ia toku Kingi o tua iho, e mahi whakaora ana i waenganui i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:13">74:13</a> Nau, na tou kaha i wawae te moana: pakaru ana i a koe nga matenga o nga tarakona i nga wai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:14">74:14</a> Mongamonga noa i a koe nga matenga o rewiatana: a hoatu ana ia e koe hei kai ma te iwi o te koraha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:15">74:15</a> I wahia e koe te puna me te roma; mimiti ake i a koe nga awa nunui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:16">74:16</a> Nau te ao, nau hoki te po; nau i whakarite te marama me te ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:17">74:17</a> Nau i whakatu nga rohe katoa o te whenua: te raumati me te hotoke, he mea whakarite ena nau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:18">74:18</a> ¶ Kia mahara ki tenei, kua tawai te hoariri, e Ihowa: kua kohukohu te hunga poauau ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:19">74:19</a> Kaua e tukua te wairua o tau kukupa ki te kirehe: kei wareware ake ake ki te whakaminenga o au rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:20">74:20</a> Whakaaroa te kawenata; kua kiki hoki nga wahi pouri o te whenua i nga nohoanga nanakia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:21">74:21</a> Kei hoki whakama mai te tangata e tukinotia ana: kia whakamoemititia tou ingoa e te ware, e te rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:22">74:22</a> E ara, e te Atua, tohea tau tohe: mahara ki ta te tangata poauau tawai ki a koe a pau noa te ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:23">74:23</a> Kei wareware ki te reo o ou hoariri: e kake tonu ana te ngangau a te hunga e whakatika ana ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:1">75:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Aratakiti. He himene, he waiata na Ahapa. Ka whakawhetai tonu matou ki a koe, e te Atua; ka whakawhetai tonu matou, kei te tata mai hoki tou ingoa: e korerotia ana e te tangata au mahi whakamiharo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:2">75:2</a> Ka kitea e ahau te wa e rite ana, ka tika taku whakawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:3">75:3</a> Kuteretere noa iho te whenua me ona tangata katoa; naku i whakatu ona pou. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:4">75:4</a> I mea ahau ki te hunga whakakake, Kati ra te whakakake; ki te hunga hara ano, Kaua e whakaarahia te haona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:5">75:5</a> Kaua to koutou haona e whakaarahia ki runga: kati te whakamaro i te kaki ina korero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:6">75:6</a> ¶ No te mea kahore he aranga i te rawhiti, kahore i te hauauru, kahore hoki i te tonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:7">75:7</a> Ko te Atua ia te kaiwhakawa; ko tenei e whakaititia iho ana e ia, ko tera e whakaarahia ake ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:8">75:8</a> Kei te ringa hoki o Ihowa he kapu, pahuka tonu te waina; ki tonu, whakananu rawa, hei ringihanga mana: ko nga nganga ia, ma te hunga kino katoa o te whenua e tatau, e inu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:9">75:9</a> Ko ahau ia, ka kauwhau tonu: ka himene ki te Atua o Hakopa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:10">75:10</a> A ka kotia e ahau nga haona katoa o te hunga kino: ka whakaarahia ake ia nga haona o te tangata tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:1">76:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Nekinoto. He himene, he waiata na Ahapa. E matauria ana te Atua i roto i a Hura, he nui tona ingoa i roto i a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:2">76:2</a> Kei Harema hoki tona tapenakara; kei Hiona tona nohoanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:3">76:3</a> I whati i a ia i reira nga pere o te kopere, te whakangungu rakau, te hoari, me nga mea mo te whawhai. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:4">76:4</a> Tera atu tou kororia, tou nui, i to nga maunga kirehe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:5">76:5</a> Kua pahuatia te hunga ngakau toa, moe ana ratou i ta ratou moe; kihai ano i whai ringa tetahi o nga marohirohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:6">76:6</a> Na tau whakatupehupehu, e te Atua o Hakopa, i parangia ai te hariata me te hoiho e te moe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:7">76:7</a> ¶ Ko koe, ina, ko koe e wehingia; ko wai hoki e tu ki tou aroaro ina riri koe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:8">76:8</a> Nau i rangona iho ai te whakawa i te rangi: wehi ana te whenua, whakaririka kau ana,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:9">76:9</a> I te aranga ake o te Atua ki te whakawa, ki te whakaora i te hunga mahaki katoa o te whenua. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:10">76:10</a> He pono ka whai kororia koe i te riri o te tangata: mau ano e whitiki te toenga o te riri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:11">76:11</a> Whakapuakina te kupu taurangi ki a Ihowa, ki to koutou Atua, whakamana hoki; e te hunga katoa i tetahi taha ona, i tetahi taha, mauria he hakari ki a ia, ka tika hoki te wehi ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:12">76:12</a> Mana e poro atu te wairua o nga rangatira: e matakuria ana ia e nga kingi o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:1">77:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ki a Ierutunu. He himene na Ahapa. Ki te Atua toku reo, e karanga nei ahau, ki te Atua toku reo, a tera e tahuri mai tona taringa ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:2">77:2</a> I rapu ahau ki te Ariki i te ra o toku pouri: maro tonu toku ringa i te po, kihai ano i pepeke; kihai toku wairua i pai kia whakamarietia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:3">77:3</a> E mahara ana ahau ki te Atua, a e pouri ana: kei te whakaaroaro, a ngaro iho toku wairua. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:4">77:4</a> E puritia ana e koe oku kanohi kia mataara tonu; he pouri ahau, te ahei te korero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:5">77:5</a> Ka hoki oku whakaaro ki nga ra onamata, ki nga tau o tua iho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:6">77:6</a> E whakamahara ana ahau ki taku waiata i te po, e korerorero ana ki toku ngakau e rapurapu ana toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:7">77:7</a> Tera ranei te Ariki e panga tonu ake ake? A heoi ano ranei ana manakohanga mai?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:8">77:8</a> Kua kahore ranei tana mahi tohu mo ake tonu atu? Kua whati ranei tana kupu a ake ake?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:9">77:9</a> Kua wareware ranei te Atua ki te atawhai? Kua riri ranei ia, a tutakina atu ana e ia tona aroha? (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:10">77:10</a> Na ka mea ahau, Ko toku ngoikore tenei: otira ka mahara ahau ki nga tau o te ringa matau o te Runga Rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:11">77:11</a> ¶ Ka mahara ahau ki nga mahi a Ihowa; ae ra, ka mahara ahau ki au mea whakamiharo o tua iho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:12">77:12</a> Ka whakaaro hoki ahau ki au meatanga katoa, ka purakau ki au mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:13">77:13</a> E te Atua, kei te wahi tapu tou ara: ko wai te atua nui hei rite ki te Atua?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:14">77:14</a> Ko koe te Atua e mahi nei i nga mea whakamiharo: kua whakapuakina e koe tou kaha i waenganui o nga iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:15">77:15</a> Hokona ana e tou ringa tau iwi, nga tama a Hakopa raua ko Hohepa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:16">77:16</a> I kite nga wai i a koe, e te Atua i kite nga wai i a koe, mataku ana: i oho ano nga rire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:17">77:17</a> Ringihia ana he wai e nga kapua, puaki ana te haruru o nga rangi: rererere ana au pere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:18">77:18</a> I roto i te awhiowhio te haruru o tau whatitiri: marama noa te ao i nga uira; wiri ana te whenua, oioi ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:19">77:19</a> I te moana tou ara, i nga wai nui tou huarahi, e kore ano e kitea ou takahanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:20">77:20</a> He mea arahi e koe tau iwi ano he kahui, ara e te ringa o Mohi raua ko Arona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:1">78:1</a> ¶ He Makiri na Ahapa. Kia anga mai te taringa, e toku iwi, ki taku ture: tahuri mai o koutou taringa ki nga kupu a toku mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:2">78:2</a> Ka puaki te kupu whakarite i toku mangai, ka korerotia e ahau nga mea ngaro onamata:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:3">78:3</a> I rongo nei, i matau nei tatou, i korero ai hoki o tatou matua ki a tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:4">78:4</a> E kore e huna e matou i a ratou tamariki: me whakaatu ki to muri whakatupuranga nga whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa, me tona kaha, me ana mahi whakamiharo i mea ai ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:5">78:5</a> Kua pumau hoki i a ia he whakaaturanga i roto i a Hakopa, kua takoto he ture i roto i a Iharaira: a whakahaua mai ana e ia o tatou tupuna, kia whakaakona ki a ratou tamariki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:6">78:6</a> Kia matauria ai e to muri whakatupuranga, e nga tamariki e whanau, e ara ake a mua: mo ta ratou whakaatu ki a ratou tamariki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:7">78:7</a> Kia u ai ta ratou tumanako ki te Atua, kei wareware hoki ki nga mahi a te Atua: engari kia mau ki ana whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:8">78:8</a> Kei rite hoki ki o ratou tupuna, ki te whakatupuranga whakakeke, tutu, ki te whakatupuranga kihai nei i whakatikatika i to ratou ngakau, kihai hoki i u to ratou wairua ki te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:9">78:9</a> ¶ He hunga mau patu nga tama a Eparaima, he hunga hapai kopere, heoi tahuri ana ratou i te ra o te tatauranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:10">78:10</a> Kihai i puritia e ratou te kawenata a te Atua; kihai ano i pai ki te haere i tana ture;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:11">78:11</a> Heoi, kua wareware ki ana mahi, me ana mea whakamiharo i whakakitea e ia ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:12">78:12</a> He mea whakamiharo ana mahi i te aroaro o o ratou tupuna, i te whenua o Ihipa, i te parae o Toana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:13">78:13</a> Tapahia ana e ia te moana, a meinga ana ratou kia whiti: tu ake i a ia nga wai ano he puranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:14">78:14</a> He mea arahi ratou e ia i te awatea ki te kapua: i te roa hoki o te po ki te marama o te ahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:15">78:15</a> I wahia e ia nga kohatu i te koraha; a me te mea no nga rire nui tana wai hei inu ma ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:16">78:16</a> Puta mai ana i a ia he awa i roto i te kamaka: meinga ana nga wai kia heke, ano he waipuke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:17">78:17</a> Heoi ka hara ano ratou ki a ia: whakatoi ana ki te Runga Rawa i te koraha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:18">78:18</a> Na kei te whakamatautau to ratou ngakau i te Atua, kei te inoi kai ma to ratou hiahia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:19">78:19</a> I korero kino ano ratou ki te Atua, i mea; E ahei ranei i te Atua te taka he tepu ki te koraha?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:20">78:20</a> Nana, ko tana patunga i te kohatu, ka pakaru mai te wai, a puke ana nga awa: e taea ano ranei e ia te homai taro, e pae ranei i a ia he kikokiko ma tana iwi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:21">78:21</a> Na ko te rongonga o Ihowa, na ka riri: a toro ana te kapura ki a Hakopa, puta ake ana te riri ki a Iharaira;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:22">78:22</a> Mo ratou kihai i whakapono ki te Atua, kihai ano i whakawhirinaki ki tana whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:23">78:23</a> Nana nei hoki i whakahau nga kapua i runga, i whakatuwhera nga tatau o te rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:24">78:24</a> A whakauaina iho te mana ki runga ki a ratou hei kai; homai ana hoki e ia te witi o te rangi ma ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:25">78:25</a> Kai ana te tangata i ta te anahera kai: i tukua e ia he kai ma ratou, a makona noa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:26">78:26</a> I whakaohokia e ia te marangai i te rangi: i takina ano te tonga e tona kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:27">78:27</a> A whakauaina iho e ia te kikokiko ki a ratou ano he puehu; he manu whai pakau ano he one no te moana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:28">78:28</a> A whakangahorotia iho e ia ki waenganui i to ratou puni: ki o ratou nohoanga a tawhio noa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:29">78:29</a> Na kai ana ratou, tino makona; i tukua hoki e ia ki a ratou ta ratou i hiahia ai:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:30">78:30</a> Kihai ratou i ngaruru ki ta ratou i hiahia ai; a i roto tonu ta ratou kai i o ratou mangai,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:31">78:31</a> Na ka pa te riri o te Atua ki a ratou, a patua iho e ia te hunga tetere o ratou; piko ana i a ia nga taitamariki o Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:32">78:32</a> Ahakoa pa katoa tenei, i hara ano ratou, kihai ano i whakapono ki ana mahi whakamiharo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:33">78:33</a> I whakapaua ai e ia o ratou ra ki te horihori, o ratou tau ki te potatutatu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:34">78:34</a> Ka patua ratou e ia, na, ka rapu ratou i a ia, a ka hoki, ka ui wawe ki te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:35">78:35</a> Ka mahara hoki ko te Atua to ratou kohatu, ko te Atua, ko te Runga Rawa, to ratou kaihoko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:36">78:36</a> Otiia kei te patipati o ratou mangai ki a ia, a teka ana o ratou arero ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:37">78:37</a> Kihai hoki to ratou ngakau i tika ki a ia; kihai ano ratou i u ki tana kawenata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:38">78:38</a> Ko tana ia, he aroha; hipokina ana e ia te he, kihai ano i whakangaro: ae ra, he maha ana whakahokinga iho i tona riri, a kihai i oho katoa tona riri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:39">78:39</a> I mahara hoki ia he kikokiko nei ratou: he hau e pahure atu ana, a e kore e hoki mai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:40">78:40</a> ¶ Ano te tini o a ratou whakatoinga i a ia i te koraha, o a ratou whakapouritanga i a ia i te tahora!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:41">78:41</a> Hoki whakamuri ana ratou, whakamatautau ana i te Atua: whakatoia ana e ratou te Mea Tapu o Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:42">78:42</a> Kihai ratou i mahara ki tona ringa, ki te ra i whakaorangia ai ratou e ia i te hoariri;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:43">78:43</a> Ki tana meatanga i ana tohu ki Ihipa, i ana merekara ki te parae o Toana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:44">78:44</a> I puta ke ai i a ia o ratou awa hei toto, me o ratou manga wai, te inu ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:45">78:45</a> I tonoa ai e ia he huihuinga namu ki a ratou, a pau iho ratou; he poroka, i huna ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:46">78:46</a> A hoatu ana e ia o ratou hua ki te moka; me to ratou mauiui ki te mawhitiwhiti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:47">78:47</a> Whakamatea ana e ia a ratou waina ki te whatu, a ratou rakau hikamora ki te haupapa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:48">78:48</a> Tukua ana e ia a ratou kararehe ma te whatu, a ratou kahui ma nga uira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:49">78:49</a> I tukua whakareretia e ia ki a ratou tona riri, aritarita, weriweri, me te raruraru; he whakaeke na nga anahera kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:50">78:50</a> A whakatikaia ana e ia he ara mo tona riri; kihai i tohungia to ratou wairua kei mate: otiia tukua ana e ia to ratou ora ki te mate uruta.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:51">78:51</a> Na patua iho e ia nga matamua i Ihipa, te muanga o to ratou kaha i nga teneti o Hama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:52">78:52</a> Otira arahina ana e ia ana ake tangata ano he hipi; whakahaerea ana ratou e ia i te koraha ano he kahui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:53">78:53</a> Na ka arahina marietia ratou e ia, te wehi ratou: ko o ratou hoariri ia taupokina iho e te moana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:54">78:54</a> Na ka kawea ratou e ia ki te rohe o tona wahi tapu, ki tenei maunga, i hokona nei e tona matau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:55">78:55</a> Peia ana e ia nga tauiwi i to ratou aroaro: a wehea ana e ia he kainga mo ratou ki te aho, whakanohoia iho nga hapu o Iharaira ki o ratou teneti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:56">78:56</a> Heoi ka whakamatauria, ka whakatoia e ratou te Atua, te Runga Rawa; kihai hoki i mau ki ana whakaaturanga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:57">78:57</a> A hoki whakamuri ana, mahi hianga ana, pera ana me o ratou matua: parori ke ana ratou, he pera me te kopere tinihanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:58">78:58</a> Na ko o ratou wahi tiketike hei whakapataritari i a ia; ko o ratou whakapakoko hei mea i a ia kia hae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:59">78:59</a> I te rongonga o te Atua, ka riri, ka tino whakarihariha hoki ki a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:60">78:60</a> A mahue ake i a ia te tapenakara a Hiro, te teneti i whakaturia e ia ki waenganui i nga tangata;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:61">78:61</a> A tukua ana e ia tona kaha hei whakarau, tona kororia ki te ringa o te hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:62">78:62</a> I tukua atu ano e ia tana iwi ma te hoari; a i riri ki tona kainga tupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:63">78:63</a> Pau ake a ratou taitama i te ahi; kihai ano a ratou kotiro i marenatia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:64">78:64</a> I hinga o ratou tohunga i te hoari; kihai hoki i tangi a ratou pouaru.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:65">78:65</a> Na ka maranga te Ariki ano ko tetahi i te moe, me te tangata kaha e hamama ana i te waina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:66">78:66</a> A patua iho e ia a muri o ona hoariri, meinga ana ratou e ia hei taunutanga mo ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:67">78:67</a> I whakakahore ano ia ki te teneti a Hohepa: a kihai i whiriwhiri i te hapu o Eparaima;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:68">78:68</a> Heoi ko te hapu o Hura tana i whiriwhiri ai, ko Maunga Hiona tana i aroha ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:69">78:69</a> A whakaturia ana e ia tona wahi tapu kia pera me nga wahi teitei; me te whenua i whakapumautia e ia mo ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:70">78:70</a> I whiriwhiria ano e ia a Rawiri, tana pononga: he mea tango nana i nga kainga hipi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:71">78:71</a> Mauria ana mai e ia i te whai i nga hipi whaereere, hei whangai i a Hakopa, i tana iwi, i a Iharaira hoki, i tona kainga tupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:72">78:72</a> A rite tonu ki te tapatahi o tona ngakau tana whangai i a ratou: he arahi mohio hoki ta tona ringa i a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:1">79:1</a> ¶ He himene na Ahapa. E te Atua, kua tae mai nga tauiwi ki tou kainga tupu, kua noa i a ratou tou temepara tapu, kua waiho a Hiruharama kia puranga kau ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:2">79:2</a> Ko nga tinana mate o au pononga kua hoatu e ratou hei kai ma nga manu o te rangi, ko te kikokiko o tau hunga tapu ma nga kirehe o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:3">79:3</a> Ko o ratou toto, ringihia ake e ratou ano he wai, ki nga taha o Hiruharama; kahore hoki he tangata hei tanu i a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:4">79:4</a> Kua waiho matou hei tawainga ma o matou hoa, hei katanga ma te hunga i tetahi taha, i tetahi taha o matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:5">79:5</a> Kia pehea te roa, e Ihowa? E riri tonu ranei koe ake ake? E ngiha tonu ranei tou hae me he kapura?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:6">79:6</a> ¶ Ringihia tou riri ki nga tauiwi kahore nei e matau ki a koe, ki nga rangatiratanga kahore nei e karanga ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:7">79:7</a> Kua pau hoki a Hakopa i a ratou, kua ururua i a ratou tona nohoanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:8">79:8</a> Kaua ra e maharatia nga kino o o matou tupuna; kia hohoro tou aroha ki mua i a matou; kua whakaititia rawatia hoki matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:9">79:9</a> Awhinatia matou, e te Atua o to matou whakaoranga, kia whakakororiatia ai tou ingoa: whakaorangia matou, hipokina hoki o matou hara, he mahara ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:10">79:10</a> Kia mea koia nga tauiwi, Kei hea to ratou Atua? Kia kite atu matou e matau ana nga tauiwi ki te whakatakinga i te toto o au pononga i whakahekea nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:11">79:11</a> Kia tae atu ki tou aroaro te aue a te herehere: kia rite ki te nui o tou kaha tau whakaora i te hunga e meatia ana kia mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:12">79:12</a> Takiwhitutia atu te utu e hoatu e koe ki nga uma o o matou hoa mo ta ratou tawai, e tawai nei ratou ki a koe, e te Ariki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:13">79:13</a> Penei ka whakawhetai matou, tau iwi, nga hipi hoki e hepara nei koe, ki a koe ake ake: ka whakaitea e matou te whakamoemiti ki a koe, ki nga whakatupuranga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:1">80:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Hohanimi Erutu. He himene na Ahapa. Tahuri mai tou taringa, e te Hepara o Iharaira, e arahi nei i a Hohepa ano he kahui hipi; whiti mai koe e noho mai na i waenganui i nga kerupima;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:2">80:2</a> Whakaohoohokia tou kaha i te aroaro o Eparaima, o Pineamine, o Manahi: a haere mai ki te whakaora i a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:3">80:3</a> Whakahokia ake matou, e te Atua: kia marama mai tou mata, a ka ora matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:4">80:4</a> E Ihowa, e te Atua o nga mano, kia pehea ake te roa o tou riri ki te inoi a tau iwi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:5">80:5</a> Kua whangaia mai e koe he roimata hei taro ma ratou, he nui hoki te mehua roimata kua homai nei e koe kia inumia e ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:6">80:6</a> Kua meinga matou e koe hei totohetanga ma o matou hoa, a e kataina ana matou e o matou hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:7">80:7</a> Whakahokia ake matou, e te Atua o nga mano; kia marama mai tou mata, a ka ora matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:8">80:8</a> ¶ I maua mai e koe he waina i Ihipa: ka oti i a koe nga tauiwi te panga, na whakatokia iho e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:9">80:9</a> I whakapaia e koe he tunga mona, na, ka hou ona pakiaka, a ka kapi te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:10">80:10</a> Taumarumaru ana tona ata ki runga ki nga pukepuke; ko ona manga rite tonu ki nga hita a te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:11">80:11</a> I tautotoro atu ona manga ki te moana, ona rara ki te awa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:12">80:12</a> He aha i pakaruhia ai e koe ona taiepa ki raro, kia kowhakiwhakia ai ia e nga tangata katoa e tika ana i te ara?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:13">80:13</a> Mongamonga noa i te poaka toa o te ngahere, e kainga ana e te kirehe mohoao o te parae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:14">80:14</a> Tahuri mai ano, e te Atua o nga mano, e inoi atu nei matou: titiro iho i te rangi, kia kite mai koe, ka toro mai i tenei waina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:15">80:15</a> I te rakau i whakatokia e tou matau, i te manga hoki i meinga e koe kia pakari mau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:16">80:16</a> Kua pau i te ahi, kua tuaina ki raro: ngaro iho ratou i te riri o tou mata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:17">80:17</a> Waiho tou ringa i runga i te tangata o tou matau, i te tama a te tangata i whakakahangia e koe mau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:18">80:18</a> Penei e kore matou e hoki atu i a koe: whakahauorangia matou, a ka karanga matou ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:19">80:19</a> Whakahokia ake matou, e Ihowa, e te Atua o nga mano; kia marama mai tou mata, a ka ora matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:1">81:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Kititi. Na Ahapa. Kia kaha te waiata ki te Atua, ki to tatou kaha: kia hari te hamama ki te Atua o Hakopa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:2">81:2</a> Whakahuatia te himene, maua mai ki konei te timipera, te hapa reka me te hatere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:3">81:3</a> Whakatangihia te tetere i te kowhititanga marama, i te kinga o te marama, i to tatou ra hakari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:4">81:4</a> Ko te tikanga hoki tenei ma Iharaira, he mea whakarite na te Atua o Hakopa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:5">81:5</a> I whakatakotoria tenei e ia ma Hohepa hei whakaaturanga, i tona haerenga puta noa i te whenua o Ihipa: i rongo ai ahau ki reira i tetahi reo, kahore ahau i matau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:6">81:6</a> I tangohia mai e ahau tona pokohiwi i te pikaunga: whakarerea ake e ona ringa te kete.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:7">81:7</a> I karanga koe ki ahau i te pouritanga, a kua ora koe i ahau; i whakahoki kupu ahau ki a koe i te wahi ngaro o te whatitiri; i whakamatau i a koe ki nga wai o Meripa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:8">81:8</a> ¶ Whakarongo, e taku iwi, a ka whakaatu ahau ki a koe: e Iharaira, ki te whakarongo koe ki ahau;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:9">81:9</a> Aua tetahi atua ke i roto i a koe; kaua ano e koropiko ki te atua ke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:10">81:10</a> Ko Ihowa ahau, ko tou Atua, i arahina mai ai koe i te whenua o Ihipa: kia nui te kowhera o tou mangai, a maku e whakaki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:11">81:11</a> Otiia kihai taku iwi i pai ki te whakarongo ki toku reo: kihai ano a Iharaira i aro ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:12">81:12</a> Na tukua atu ana ratou e ahau ki te maro o o ratou ngakau: a haere ana ratou i runga i o ratou whakaaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:13">81:13</a> Aue, te whakarongo taku iwi ki ahau! Te haere a Iharaira i aku ara!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:14">81:14</a> Penei e kore e aha kua whati i ahau te tara o o ratou hoariri: kua tahuri ano toku ringa ki o ratou hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:15">81:15</a> Ko te hunga e kino ana ki a Ihowa kua ngohengohe ki a ia: ko to ratou taima ia kua mau tonu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:16">81:16</a> Kua whangainga hoki ratou e ia ki te witi pai rawa, kua whakamakonatia ano koe e ahau ki te honi i roto i te kohatu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:1">82:1</a> ¶ He himene na Ahapa. E tu ana te Atua i roto i te whakaminenga o te Atua, e whakawa ana i waenganui i nga atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:2">82:2</a> Kia pehea ake te roa o ta koutou whakawa he, o ta koutou whakapai ki nga kanohi o te hunga kino. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:3">82:3</a> Whakatikaia ta te ware, ta te pani: kia tika te whakawa mo te ngakau mamae, mo te rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:4">82:4</a> Whakaorangia te ware me te rawakore; tangohia mai ratou i te ringa o te tangata kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:5">82:5</a> Kahore o ratou matauranga, kakore hoki e mahara; e kopikopiko noa ana ratou i te pouri; e oioi ana nga turanga katoa o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:6">82:6</a> ¶ I mea ahau, He atua koutou, he tama katoa na te Runga Rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:7">82:7</a> Heoi ka pera koutou me te tangata, ka mate; ka hinga, ka pera me tetahi o nga piriniha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:8">82:8</a> E ara, e te Atua, whakawakia te whenua: mou hoki nga tauiwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:1">83:1</a> ¶ He waiata, he himene, na Ahapa. E te Atua, kei wahangu koe, kei whakarongo puku, kei ata noho, e te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:2">83:2</a> He mea hoki, tenei ou hoariri te ngangau nei, a kua ara nga matenga o te hunga e kino ana ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:3">83:3</a> Kua ata ngarahu ratou ki tau iwi, e whakatakoto korero ana hoki ratou mo au mea huna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:4">83:4</a> Kua mea nei ratou, Tena, tatou ka huna i a ratou, kia kore ai tena iwi; kia kaua ai hoki e maharatia te ingoa o Iharaira a muri ake nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:5">83:5</a> Kua kotahi to ratou ngakau i a ratou e runanga ana: kua whakatakoto ratou he tikanga kino ki a koe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:6">83:6</a> Ko nga teneti o Eroma, o nga Ihimaeri, o Moapa, o nga Hakarini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:7">83:7</a> A Kepara, a Amona, a Amareke, nga Pirihitini, me nga tangata o Taira:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:8">83:8</a> Kua uru hoki a Ahiria ki roto ki a ratou; kua awhinatia e ratou nga tamariki a Rota. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:9">83:9</a> ¶ Peratia ratou me Miriana: me Hihera, me Iapini, i te awa i Kihona:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:10">83:10</a> I mate nei ki Eneroro, i waiho nei hei whakawairakau mo te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:11">83:11</a> Kia rite o ratou rangatira ki a Orepe raua ko Teepe, ae, o ratou ariki katoa hoki ki a Tepa raua ko Taramuna;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:12">83:12</a> Mo ratou i mea, Tatou ka tango i nga kainga o te Atua mo tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:13">83:13</a> E toku Atua, meinga ratou kia rite ki te awhiowhio puehu, ki te papapa e puhia ana e te hau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:14">83:14</a> Kia rite ki te ahi e kai ana i te ngahere, ki te mura hoki e toro ai nga maunga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:15">83:15</a> Kia pera te whai o tau awha i a ratou, tau whakaohorere hoki i a ratou ki tau paroro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:16">83:16</a> Whakakiia o ratou kanohi ki te whakama: kia rapu ai ratou ki tou ingoa, e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:17">83:17</a> Kia whakama, kia ohorere ratou ake ake; ae, kia numinumi ratou, kia ngaro hoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:18">83:18</a> Kia matau ai ratou, ko koe anake, ko Ihowa nei tou ingoa, te Runga Rawa i te whenua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:1">84:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Kititi. He himene ma nga tama a Koraha. Ano te ataahua o ou tapenakara, e Ihowa o nga mano!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:2">84:2</a> E hiahia ana toku wairua, ae, e hemo ana ki nga marae o Ihowa: e tangi ana toku ngakau me oku kikokiko ki te Atua ora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:3">84:3</a> Me te pihoihoi hoki kua kite i tetahi whare, me te warou ano hoki i tetahi ohanga mona, hei takotoranga mo ana pi, ara i au aata, e Ihowa o nga mano, e toku Kingi, e toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:4">84:4</a> Ka hari te hunga e noho ana i tou whare: he whakamoemiti tonu ta ratou ki a koe. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:5">84:5</a> Ka hari te tangata ko tona kaha nei kei a koe: kei roto i o ratou ngakau nga huarahi ki reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:6">84:6</a> Ka haere ratou ra te raorao o Paka, ka meinga e ratou hei puna: ngaro iho ano hoki nga poka i te ua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:7">84:7</a> Ka haere atu ratou i te kaha ki te kaha; ka kitea ratou ki te aroaro o te Atua i Hiona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:8">84:8</a> ¶ E Ihowa, e te Atua o nga mano, whakarongo ki taku inoi: tahuri mai tou taringa, e te Atua o Hakopa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:9">84:9</a> Titiro mai, e te Atua, e to matou whakangungu rakau: tirohia iho hoki te mata o tau tangata i whakawahi ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:10">84:10</a> No te mea, he ra kotahi i ou whare, pai atu i nga ra kotahi mano: te tiaki tatau i te whare o toku Atua, pai atu ki ahau i te noho ki nga teneti o te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:11">84:11</a> He ra hoki a Ihowa te Atua, he whakangungu rakau: ka homai e Ihowa te atawhai me te kororia; e kore e kaiponuhia e ia tetahi mea pai ki te hunga e tapatahi ana te haere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:12">84:12</a> E Ihowa o nga mano, ka hari te tangata e whakawhirinaki ana ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:1">85:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene ma nga tama a Koraha. E Ihowa, kua aro mai koe ki tou whenua, kua whakahokia mai e koe a Hakopa i te whakarau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:2">85:2</a> Kua murua e koe te kino o tau iwi, kua hipokina e koe o ratou hara katoa (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:3">85:3</a> Kua mutu katoa tou weriweri; kua tahuri ke koe i te aritarita o tou riri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:4">85:4</a> Whakahokia ake matou, e te Atua o to matou whakaoranga: meinga hoki kia mutu tou riri ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:5">85:5</a> E riri ranei koe ki a matou ake ake? E mauahara tonu ranei, ki nga whakatupuranga katoa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:6">85:6</a> E kore ianei koe e whakahoki ake i a matou ki te ora: kia hari ai tau iwi ki a koe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:7">85:7</a> E Ihowa, whakakitea mai tau mahi tohu ki a matou: tukua mai ki a matou tau whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:8">85:8</a> ¶ Ka whakarongo ahau ki ta te Atua, ki ta Ihowa, e korero ai: no te mea mo te rongo mau ana korero ki tana iwi, ki tana hunga tapu hoki; kaua ia ratou e hoki ki te wairangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:9">85:9</a> Ina, he tata tonu tana whakaoranga ki te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia, kia noho ai te kororia ki to tatou whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:10">85:10</a> Kua tutaki te mahi tohu raua ko te pono: kua kihi ki a raua te tika me te rongo mau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:11">85:11</a> Ka tupu ake te pono i te whenua, a ka titiro iho te tika i te rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:12">85:12</a> Ae, ka homai e Ihowa te pai: a ka tukua mai ona hua e to tatou whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:13">85:13</a> Ka haere te tika i mua i a ia, hei whakatu i a tatou ki te ara o ona hikoinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:1">86:1</a> ¶ He inoi na Rawiri. Whakatitahatia iho tou taringa, e Ihowa whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau; he ware hoki ahau, he rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:2">86:2</a> Tiakina toku wairua: he tapu hoki ahau; mau, e toku Atua, e whakaora tau pononga e whakawhirinaki atu nei ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:3">86:3</a> Tohungia ahau, e te Ariki: e karanga nei hoki ahau ki a koe i te ra roa nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:4">86:4</a> Whakaharitia te wairua o tau pononga; ka ara atu nei hoki toku wairua, e te Ariki, ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:5">86:5</a> He pai hoki koe, e te Ariki, he ngawari: e ranea ana hoki tau mahi tohu ki te hunga katoa e karanga ana ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:6">86:6</a> Tahuri mai tou taringa, e Ihowa, ki taku inoi: whakarongo kitoku reo unene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:7">86:7</a> Ka karanga ahau ki a koe i te ra o toku pouri: e whakahoki kupu mai hoki koe ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:8">86:8</a> ¶ Kahore he rite mou, e te Ariki, i roto i nga atua: kahore hoki he rite mo au mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:9">86:9</a> Ka haere mai nga iwi katoa i hanga e koe, a ka koropiko ki tou aroaro, e te Ariki; ka whakakororia hoki i tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:10">86:10</a> He nui hoki koe, e mahi ana i nga mea whakamiharo: ko koe anake te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:11">86:11</a> Whakaakona ahau ki tau ara, e Ihowa; ka haere ahau i runga i tou pono: whakatapatahitia toku ngakau ki te wehi i tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:12">86:12</a> Ka whakamoemiti katoa toku ngakau ki a koe, e te Ariki, e toku Atua: ka whakakororia ano i tou ingoa ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:13">86:13</a> He nui hoki tau mahi tohu ki ahau: a kua whakaorangia e koe toku wairua i te reinga i raro riro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:14">86:14</a> E te Atua, kua whakatika ki ahau te hunga whakakake: kua whaia ano toku wairua e te huihuinga o te hunga tutu; kahore hoki koe e waiho i to ratou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:15">86:15</a> Ko koe ia, e te Ariki, he Atua atawhai, he tohu tangata: he puhoi ki te riri, e hua ana te mahi tohu me te pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:16">86:16</a> Tahuri mai ki ahau, tohungia hoki ahau: homai tou kaha ki tau pononga, whakaorangia te tama a tau pononga wahine.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:17">86:17</a> Whakakitea mai ki ahau he tohu mo te pai: kia kite ai te hunga e kino ana ki ahau, kia whakama ai: nou e Ihowa i awhina i ahau, i whakamarie i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:1">87:1</a> ¶ He himene, he waiata ma nga tama a Koraha. Kei nga maunga tapu tona turanga:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:2">87:2</a> E arohaina rawatia ana e Ihowa nga kuwaha o Hiona i nga nohoanga katoa o Hakopa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:3">87:3</a> He mea kororia nga mea e korerotia ana mou, e te pa o te Atua. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:4">87:4</a> ¶ Ka korerotia e ahau a Rahapa raua ko Papurona ki roto i te hunga e matau ana ki ahau: tirohia atu a Pirihitia, a Taira, a Etiopia; i whanau tenei ki reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:5">87:5</a> Ae ra ko te kupu tenei mo Hiona, I whanau tenei me tera ki reira: ma te Runga Rawa pu ano ia e whakapumau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:6">87:6</a> Ka korerotia e Ihowa, ina tuhituhia nga iwi, I whanau tenei ki reira. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:7">87:7</a> Na ka mea te hunga waiata, me te hunga kanikani, Kei a koe oku puna katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:1">88:1</a> ¶ He waiata, he himene ma nga tama a Koraha. Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Maharata Reanoto. He Makiri na Hemana Eterahi. E Ihowa, e te Atua o toku whakaoranga, he tangi taku ki tou aroaro i te ao, i te po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:2">88:2</a> Kia tae atu taku inoi ki tou aroaro: whakatitahatia mai tou taringa ki taku tangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:3">88:3</a> Kua ki hoki toku wairua i te pouri, a e whakatata ana toku ora ki te reinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:4">88:4</a> Kua taua tahitia ahau me te hunga e heke ana ki te rua; e rite ana ahau ki te tangata kahore ona awhina!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:5">88:5</a> I maka ki waenga i nga tupapaku, me he tangata i patua e takoto ana i te urupa, kahore nei e maharatia e koe i muri; he mea momotu ke ratou na tou ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:6">88:6</a> Kua whakatakotoria ahau e koe ki te rua i raro riro, ki te pouri, ki nga rire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:7">88:7</a> E pehia ana ahau e tou riri, e pakia ana hoki e koe ki au ngaru katoa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:8">88:8</a> Kua whakamataratia atu e koe oku hoa kia tawhiti i ahau: kua meinga ahau e koe hei mea whakarihariha ki a ratou: kua uakina mai ahau, a kahore e puta ki waho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:9">88:9</a> Kua he toku kanohi i te tangihanga: e karanga ana ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa, i nga ra katoa, kua totoro hoki oku ringa ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:10">88:10</a> ¶ Tera ranei koe e mahi merekara ki nga tupapaku? E ara koia te hunga kua mate ki te whakamoemiti ki a koe? (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:11">88:11</a> Ka kauwhautia ranei tou aroha i roto i te urupa? tou pono i roto i te ngaromanga?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:12">88:12</a> E matauria koia au mea whakamiharo i roto i te pouri? tou tika i te whenua o te warewaretanga?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:13">88:13</a> Ko ahau ia kua karanga ki a koe, e Ihowa: a i te ata ka tae atu taku inoi ki tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:14">88:14</a> He aha, e Ihowa, i panga ai toku wairua e koe? He aha i huna ai tou mata ki ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:15">88:15</a> No toku tamarikitanga ake ano i pakia ai ahau, i whakahemohemo ai: i ahau e pehia ana e au whakawehi, ka pororaru noa iho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:16">88:16</a> I tika tou riri nui ma runga i ahau; kua haukotia ahau e au mea whakawehi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:17">88:17</a> Ano he wai ratou ki te karapoti i ahau i te ra roa nei; hui tahi ratou ki te taiawhio i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:18">88:18</a> Kua wehea e koe kia tawhiti atu i ahau te hoa hei aroha mai, me oku hoa ki roto ki te pouri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:1">89:1</a> ¶ He Makiri na Etana Eterahi. Ka waiatatia e ahau nga mahi tohu a Ihowa ake ake: ka whakapuakina e toku mangai tou pono ki nga whakatupuranga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:2">89:2</a> I mea hoki ahau, Ka hanga ake te mahi tohu mo ake tonu atu: ka whakapumautia e koe tou pono ki nga tino rangi ra ano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:3">89:3</a> Kua whakarite kawenata ahau ki taku i whiriwhiri ai: kua oati ki taku pononga ki a Rawiri;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:4">89:4</a> Ka pumau i ahau ou uri ake ake: ka hanga tou torona ki nga whakatupuranga katoa. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:5">89:5</a> ¶ Ka whakamoemiti ano nga rangi, e Ihowa, ki au mahi whakamiharo; ki tou pono hoki i roto i te whakaminenga o te hunga tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:6">89:6</a> Ko wai oti i nga rangi hei rite mo Ihowa? Ko wai i roto i nga tama a te hunga nunui e rite ana ki a Ihowa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:7">89:7</a> He Atua whakamataku rawa i roto i te whakaminenga o te hunga tapu, e wehingia ana i runga ake i a ratou katoa i tetahi taha, i tetahi taha ona?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:8">89:8</a> E Ihowa, e te Atua o nga mano, ko wai te mea kaha hei rite mou, e IHA? Hei rite ranei mo tou pono i tetahi taha ou, i tetahi taha?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:9">89:9</a> Ko koe te kingi o te huamo o te moana: ka oho ona ngaru, ko koe hei whakamarino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:10">89:10</a> Mongamonga noa i a koe a Rahapa ano he tangata i patua: marara ana i a koe, i tou ringa kaha ou hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:11">89:11</a> Nau nga rangi, nau te whenua: te ao me ona mea e hua ana i runga, nau ena i pumau ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:12">89:12</a> Ko te raki me te tonga nau ena i hanga: ka hari a Taporo raua ko Heremona ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:13">89:13</a> He takakau marohirohi tou: he pakari tou ringa, rewa tonu tou matau ki runga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:14">89:14</a> Ko te tika me te whakawa te turanga o tou torona: e haere ana te mahi tohu me te pono i mua i tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:15">89:15</a> ¶ Ka hari te iwi e mohio ana ki te tangi whakahari: e haere ana ratou, e Ihowa, i te marama o tou mata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:16">89:16</a> E hari ana ratou ki tou ingoa i te roa o te ra: a ma tou tika ka kake ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:17">89:17</a> Ko koe hoki te kororia o to ratou kaha: ma tau manako ano ka ara ai to matou haona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:18">89:18</a> Na Ihowa hoki to matou whakangungu rakau: a na te Mea Tapu o Iharaira to tatou kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:19">89:19</a> ¶ I korero moemoea koe i reira ki tau Mea Tapu, i mea, Kua hoatu e ahau he kaha ki runga ki tetahi marohirohi; kua whakanuia e ahau tetahi i whiriwhiria i roto i te iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:20">89:20</a> Kua kitea e ahau taku pononga, a Rawiri: kua whakawahia ia e ahau ki taku hinu tapu:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:21">89:21</a> Ka u atu toku ringa hei awhina mona: ma toku takakau ano ia e whakakaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:22">89:22</a> E kore te hoariri e whai wahi ki a ia: e kore ano hoki te tama a te kino e tukino i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:23">89:23</a> Maku e tukituki ona hoariri ki tona aroaro: ka whiua e ahau te hunga e kino ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:24">89:24</a> Otira ka mau ki a ia toku pono me taku mahi tohu: a ma toku ingoa ka ara ai tona haona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:25">89:25</a> Maku ano tona ringa ka pa ai ki te moana: tona matau ki nga awa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:26">89:26</a> Ka karanga ia ki ahau, Ko koe toku Papa, toku Atua, te kohatu o toku whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:27">89:27</a> Ka waiho ano ia hei matamua maku ki runga ake i nga kingi o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:28">89:28</a> Ka rongoatia e ahau taku mahi tohu mona ake tonu atu: ka mau tonu taku kawenata ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:29">89:29</a> Ka meinga hoki e ahau ona uri kia mau tonu ake ake, tona torona ano ko nga ra o te rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:30">89:30</a> Ki te whakarerea e ana tamariki taku ture, a kahore e haere i aku whakaritenga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:31">89:31</a> Ki te takahi ratou i aku tikanga; a kahore e pupuri i aku whakahau;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:32">89:32</a> Katahi ka whaia ta ratou mahi tutu e taku rakau, o ratou kino e te whiu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:33">89:33</a> Otira e kore e tangohia rawatia e ahau taku mahi tohu i a ia, e tuku ranei i toku pono kia he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:34">89:34</a> E kore taku kawenata e takahia e ahau, e kore ano e whakarereketia te mea i puta i oku ngutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:35">89:35</a> Kotahi aku oatitanga i toku tapu; e kore ahau e teka ki a Rawiri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:36">89:36</a> Ka mau tonu tona uri ake ake; a ka rite tona torona ki te ra i toku aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:37">89:37</a> Ka rite tona pumau ki to te marama ake ake: hei kaiwhakaatu pono ano i runga i te rangi. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:38">89:38</a> ¶ Na kua panga nei koe, kua whakarihariha, kua riri ki tau i whakawahi ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:39">89:39</a> Kua weriweri koe ki te kawenata ki tau pononga: kua whakanoaia e koe tona karauna, taka noa ki te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:40">89:40</a> Kua pakaruhia e koe ona taiepa katoa; whakamotitia iho e koe ona pa kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:41">89:41</a> E pahua ana i a ia nga tangata katoa e tika ana i te ara: he tawainga ia na ona hoa tata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:42">89:42</a> Kua whakarewaina e koe te ringa matau o ona hoa whawhai: kua meinga e koe kia hari ona hoa whawhai katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:43">89:43</a> Ae, e ngore ana i a koe te mata o tana hoari: kihai ano koe i tautoko i a ia ki te tatauranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:44">89:44</a> Kua whakamutua e koe tona kororia, kua maka tona torona ki raro ki te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:45">89:45</a> Kua poroa e koe nga ra o tona taitamarikitanga: kua hipokina ia e koe ki te whakama. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:46">89:46</a> Kia pehea te roa, e Ihowa, e whakangaro ai koe i a koe, ake tonu atu? Kia pehea te roa e toro ana tou riri ano he ahi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:47">89:47</a> Kia mahara ki te poto rawa o toku taima: he aha i hanga ai e koe nga tangata katoa hei kore noa iho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:48">89:48</a> Ko wai tena tangata e ora nei, a e kore e kite i te mate? E mawhiti koia i a ia tona wairua i te kaha o te reinga? (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:49">89:49</a> E te Ariki, kei hea au arohatanga o mua i oatitia ai e koe ki a Rawiri i runga i tou pono?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:50">89:50</a> Maharatia, e te Ariki, te tawai ki au pononga; e mau nei ki toku uma te tawai a nga iwi nunui katoa:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:51">89:51</a> Te tawai a ou hoariri, e Ihowa, ta ratou tawai nei ki nga hikoinga o tau i whakawahi ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:52">89:52</a> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa ake ake. Amine, ae Amine.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:1">90:1</a> ¶ He inoi na Mohi, na te tangata a te Atua. E te Ariki, ko koe to matou nohoanga i nga whakatupuranga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:2">90:2</a> Kahore ano i whanau noa nga maunga, kahore i hanga e koe te whenua me te ao, ko koe te Atua no tua whakarere a ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:3">90:3</a> E whakahokia ana e koe te tangata kia mongamonga noa, a e mea ana, E hoki, e nga tama a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:4">90:4</a> Ki tau titiro hoki, he rite nga tau kotahi mano ki te ra onanahi, kua pahure atu nei, ki te mataaratanga hoki i te po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:5">90:5</a> Me te mea na te waipuke tau kahakinga i a ratou; he moe ratou: i te ata ano he tarutaru e tupu ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:6">90:6</a> I te ata e tupu ana, e pihi ana: i te ahiahi kua kotia, kua maroke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:7">90:7</a> ¶ Kua hemo nei hoki matou i tou riri: ka ohorere hoki i tou aritatanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:8">90:8</a> Kua maka e koe o matou kino ki tou aroaro, o matou mea huna ki te marama o tou mata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:9">90:9</a> Ka pau o matou ra katoa, me te riri ano koe: hemo ake o matou tau ano he korero e korerotia ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:10">90:10</a> Ko nga ra o o matou tau e whitu tekau tau; a ki te whai kaha, ka waru tekau tau; heoi he mahi mauiui, he pouri to ratou kaha; ka hohoro hoki te hatepea atu, a ka rere atu matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:11">90:11</a> Ko wai te matau ana ki te kaha o tou riri? Rite pu ki te wehi ki a koe tou riri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:12">90:12</a> ¶ Akona matou ki te tatau i o matou ra, kia anga ai te ngakau ki te whakaaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:13">90:13</a> Hoki mai, e Ihowa, kia pehea ake te roa? A kia puta ke he whakaaro mou ki au pononga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:14">90:14</a> Kia na matou i te ata i tau mahi tohu: kia hari ai matou, kia koa ai, i o matou ra katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:15">90:15</a> Whakaharitia matou, kia rite ki nga ra i whakawhiua ai matou e koe, ki nga tau i kite ai matou i te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:16">90:16</a> Kia puta mai tau mahi ki au pononga, me tou kororia ki a ratou tamariki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:17">90:17</a> A hei runga i a matou te ataahua o Ihowa, o to matou Atua: whakapumautia ano ki a matou te mahi a o matou ringa, ae ra, te mahi a o matou ringa, whakapumautia e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:1">91:1</a> ¶ Ko te tangata kei te wahi ngaro o te Runga Rawa tona kainga, ka noho ia i raro i te taumarumarutanga o te Kaha Rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:2">91:2</a> Ka kiia e ahau a Ihowa, Ko ia toku piringa, toku pa, toku Atua, ka whakawhirinaki ahau ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:3">91:3</a> Mana hoki koe e whakaora i te mahanga a te kaihopu manu, i te mate nanakia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:4">91:4</a> Ka hipokina koe e ia ki ona hou, a ka piri koe ki raro i ona pakau: ko tona pono hei whakangungu rakau, hei puapua mou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:5">91:5</a> E kore koe e wehi i te mea whakamataku i te po: i te pere e rere ana i te awatea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:6">91:6</a> I te mate uruta e rere ana i te pouri: i te whakangaromanga e whakangaro ana i te poutumarotanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:7">91:7</a> He mano te hinga ki tou taha, tekau hoki nga mano ki tou matau; otiia e kore e tata ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:8">91:8</a> Ka titiro kau ou kanohi, ka matakitaki ki te utu mo te hunga kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:9">91:9</a> ¶ Ko koe hoki, e Ihowa, toku piranga! kua waiho e koe te Runga Rawa hei nohoanga mou:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:10">91:10</a> Kahore he kino e pa ki a koe, kahore ano he whiu e tata ki tou teneti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:11">91:11</a> Ka korerotia iho hoki koe e ia ki ana anahera kia tiakina koe i ou ara katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:12">91:12</a> Ma ratou koe e hiki ake ki o ratou ringa, kei tutuki tou waewae ki te kohatu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:13">91:13</a> Ka haere koe i runga i te raiona, i te neke: ka takahia e koe ki raro te kuao raiona me te nakahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:14">91:14</a> Ka whakaora ahau i a ia, mona i aroha ki ahau; maku ia e whakateitei ake, mona i matau ki toku ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:15">91:15</a> Ka karanga ia ki ahau, a ka whakahoki kupu ahau ki a ia: ka tata ahau ki a ia i te wa o te he; maku ia e whakaora, maku ano ia e whakahonore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:16">91:16</a> Ka whakaroaina e ahau ona ra, a na noa ia: ka whakakitea hoki taku whakaoranga ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:1">92:1</a> ¶ He himene, he waiata mo te ra Hapati. He mea pai te whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, te himene atu ki tou ingoa, e te Runga Rawa:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:2">92:2</a> Te whakakite i tou atawhai i te ata, i tou pono i nga po katoa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:3">92:3</a> I runga i te aho tekau, i te hatere; i te tangi huatau a te hapa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:4">92:4</a> Nau hoki ahau, e Ihowa, i whakahari ki tau mahi: ka whakamanamana ahau ki nga meatanga a ou ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:5">92:5</a> Ano te nui o au mahi, e Ihowa! hohonu rawa ou whakaaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:6">92:6</a> Ko te tangata poauau, kahore ia e matau; kahore hoki tenei e mohiotia e te kuware.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:7">92:7</a> ¶ Kia pihi ake nga whakaarokore ano he tarutaru, a kia tupu nga kaimahi katoa i te kino; he ngaromanga tena no ratou ake ake;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:8">92:8</a> Ko koe ia, e Ihowa, kei runga rawa ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:9">92:9</a> Na, ko ou hoa whawhai, e Ihowa, na, ko ou hoa whawhai, ka ngaro; ka marara katoa nga kaimahi i te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:10">92:10</a> Otira ka ara i a koe toku haona, ka pera i to te kau maka: ka whakawahia ahau ki te hinu hou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:11">92:11</a> Ka kite hoki toku kanohi i taku i hiahia ai ki runga ki oku hoariri, ka rongo oku taringa i taku i hiahia ai o te hunga kino e whakatika ana mai ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:12">92:12</a> Ka rite te tupu o te tangata tika ki to te nikau; ka rite tona nui ki to te hita i Repanona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:13">92:13</a> Ko te hunga i whakatokia ki te whare o Ihowa ka tupu ki nga marae o to tatou Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:14">92:14</a> Ka whai hua tonu ratou ua hina: ki tonu i te wai, matomato tonu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:15">92:15</a> Hei whakakite i te tika o Ihowa: ko ia toku kohatu, kahore hoki ona he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:1">93:1</a> ¶ E kingi ana a Ihowa; he kororia tona kakahu; he kakahu to Ihowa, he mea whitiki ia ki te kaha: kua u hoki te ao, te taea te nekeneke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:2">93:2</a> No mua iho tou torona i whakapumautia ai: nonamata riro koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:3">93:3</a> Ko nga roma, e Ihowa, kua ara, nga roma nei, kua ara to ratou reo; ka ara nga ngaru o nga roma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:4">93:4</a> I runga ake i nga reo o nga wai maha, i nga tuatea nunui o te moana, ko Ihowa i runga, te mea kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:5">93:5</a> Pono atu au whakaaturanga: he huatau te tapu mo tou whare, e Ihowa, mo ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:1">94:1</a> ¶ E Ihowa, e te Atua, e te Kairapu utu; e te Atua, e te Kairapu utu, tiaho mai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:2">94:2</a> E ara, e te Kaiwhakawa o te whenua: hoatu te utu e rite ana ki te hunga whakakake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:3">94:3</a> Kia pehea te roa, e Ihowa, o te hunga kino nei, kia pehea te roa o te hunga kino e whakamanamana ana?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:4">94:4</a> Kei te korero whakatu ratou, kei te korero whakahi: kei te korero whakapehapeha ki a ratou nga kaimahi katoa i te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:5">94:5</a> Mongamonga noa tau iwi i a ratou, e Ihowa: e tukinotia ana e ratou tou kainga tupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:6">94:6</a> E patua ana e ratou te pouaru, te manene: e kohuru ana i te pani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:7">94:7</a> A e mea ana, E kore a Ihowa e kite; e kore e maharatia e te Atua o Hakopa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:8">94:8</a> Kia matau, e nga poauau o te iwi: a hea ano koutou whai mahara ai, e nga kuware?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:9">94:9</a> Ko te kaiwhakato o te taringa, e kore ranei ia e rongo? Ko te kaihanga o te kanohi, e kore ianei ia e kite?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:10">94:10</a> Ko te kaipapaki o nga iwi e kore ranei ia e papaki, ara ko te kaiwhakaako nei i te tangata kia mohio?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:11">94:11</a> E matau ana a Ihowa ki nga whakaaro o te tangata, he mea teka noa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:12">94:12</a> ¶ Ka hari te tangata e pakia ana e koe, e Ihowa: e whakaakona ana i roto i tau ture;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:13">94:13</a> Kia marie ai tona ngakau i a koe i nga ra o te he, a keria noatia iho te poka mo te tangata kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:14">94:14</a> E kore hoki a Ihowa e panga i tana iwi, e kore ano e whakarere i tona kainga tupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:15">94:15</a> Engari e hoki te whakawa ki te tika: a e arumia e nga tangata ngakau tika katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:16">94:16</a> Ko wai toku hei whakatika ake ki te hunga kino? Ko wai toku hei tu ake ki nga kaimahi i te hara?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:17">94:17</a> Mehemea kaua a Ihowa hei awhina moku, penei kua noho kupukore noa atu toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:18">94:18</a> I taku meatanga, Ka paheke toku waewae; na tau mahi tohu, e Ihowa, ahau i tautoko ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:19">94:19</a> I oku whakaaronga maha i roto i toku ngakau ko au whakamarie toku oranga ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:20">94:20</a> Tera ranei e whakahoa ki a koe te torona o te kino, e whakatakoto nei i te mahi nanakia hei ture?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:21">94:21</a> Kei te whakahuihui ratou ki te poke i te wairua o te tangata tika, e mea ana kia heke te toto harakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:22">94:22</a> Ko Ihowa ia toku pa teko: ko toku Atua hei kohatu piringa moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:23">94:23</a> A nana i whakahoki to ratou kino ki runga ki a ratou, a tera ia e whakangaro i a ratou i roto i o ratou kino: ma Ihowa, ma to tatou Atua ratou e whakangaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:1">95:1</a> ¶ Tena, kia waiata tatou ki a Ihowa: kia hari te hamama ki te kamaka o to tatou whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:2">95:2</a> Kia haere tatou me te whakawhetai atu ki tona aroaro: kia ngahau hoki a tatou himene ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:3">95:3</a> No te mea he Atua nui hoki a Ihowa, he Kingi nui i nga atua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:4">95:4</a> Kei tona ringa nga wahi hohonu o te whenua: a nana nga maunga teitei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:5">95:5</a> Nana te moana, nana ano i hanga, a na ona ringa i whai ahua ai te whenua maroke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:6">95:6</a> Haere mai tatou, kia koropiko, kia tuohu: kia tukua nga turi ki te aroaro o Ihowa, o to tatou Kaihanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:7">95:7</a> ¶ Ko ia hoki to tatou Atua; ko tatou tana iwi e hepara ai, nga hipi a tona ringa. Ki te rongo koutou ki tona reo aianei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:8">95:8</a> Kaua e whakapakeketia o koutou ngakau: kei pera me o te whakatoinga, me o te ra o te whakamatautauranga i te koraha;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:9">95:9</a> I ahau i whakamatautauria e o koutou matua, i ata mohiotia, i to ratou kitenga ano hoki i aku mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:10">95:10</a> E wha tekau nga tau i hoha ai ahau ki tenei whakatupuranga, na ka mea ahau; He iwi ngakau kotiti ke ratou, kahore hoki ratou e mohio ki aku ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:11">95:11</a> Na reira i riri ai ahau, i oati ai hoki; e kore ratou e tae ki toku okiokinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:1">96:1</a> ¶ Waiatatia he waiata hou ki a Ihowa: waiata, e te whenua katoa, ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:2">96:2</a> Waiata ki a Ihowa, whakapaingia tona ingoa: whakakitea tana whakaoranga i tenei ra, i tenei ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:3">96:3</a> Whakapuakina tona kororia i waenganui i nga tauiwi, ana mahi whakamiharo i waenganui i nga iwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:4">96:4</a> He nui hoki a Ihowa, he tika ano kia nui te whakamoemiti ki a ia: kia wehingia nuitia ai i nga atua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:5">96:5</a> He whakapakoko hoki nga atua katoa o nga iwi: na Ihowa ia i hanga nga rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:6">96:6</a> He honore, he kororia kei tona aroaro: kei tona wahi tapu te kaha me te ataahua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:7">96:7</a> Waiho atu i a Ihowa, e nga hapu katoa o nga iwi: waiho atu i a Ihowa te kororia me te kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:8">96:8</a> Waiho atu i a Ihowa te kororia e tika ana mo tona ingoa: maua mai he whakahere, haere mai hoki ki ona marae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:9">96:9</a> Koropiko ki a Ihowa i roto i te ataahua o te tapu: kia wehi ra ki tona aroaro, e te whenua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:10">96:10</a> ¶ Mea atu i waenganui o nga tauiwi, E kingi ana a Ihowa: ka u te whenua, te taea te whakangaueue; ka tika ana whakawa mo nga iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:11">96:11</a> Kia hari nga rangi, kia koa te whenua, kia haruru te moana, me nga mea e hua ana i roto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:12">96:12</a> Kia hari te mara, me nga mea katoa i runga: ko reira ano koa ai nga rakau katoa o te ngahere;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:13">96:13</a> Ki te aroaro o Ihowa, e haere mai ana hoki ia; e haere mai ana ia ki te whakawa mo te whenua: ka whakawa ia mo te ao i runga i te tika, mo nga iwi hoki i runga i tona pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:1">97:1</a> ¶ Ko Ihowa te Kingi, kia hari te whenua, kia koa nga tini moutere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:2">97:2</a> Ko te kapua me te pouri kei ona taha katoa: ko te tika, ko te whakawa, te turanga o tona torona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:3">97:3</a> He kapura e haere ana i mua i a ia, a pau ake ona hoariri a taka noa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:4">97:4</a> Marama tonu te ao i ana uira: i kite te whenua, a wiri ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:5">97:5</a> Rewa noa nga maunga, ano he ware pi, i te aroaro o Ihowa, i te aroaro o te Ariki o te whenua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:6">97:6</a> E whakapuakina ana e nga rangi tona tika: a e kitea ana e nga iwi katoa tona kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:7">97:7</a> Kia whakama katoa te hunga e mahi ana ki nga whakapakoko, e whakamanamana ana ki nga atua horihori: koropiko ki a ia, e nga atua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:8">97:8</a> ¶ I rongo a Hiona, a koa ana: whakamanamana ana nga tamahine o Hura, e Ihowa, ki au whakaritenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:9">97:9</a> Ko koe hoki, e Ihowa, kei runga noa ake i te whenua katoa: kua whakanuia koe ki runga noa ake i nga atua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:10">97:10</a> E te hunga e aroha ana ki a Ihowa, e kino ki te he: e tiakina ana e ia nga wairua o tana hunga tapu; e whakaorangia ana ratou e ia i nga ringa o te hunga kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:11">97:11</a> Kua oti te marama te whakato mo te hunga tika: me te koa mo te hunga ngakau tapatahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:12">97:12</a> Kia hari ki a Ihowa, e te hunga tika: whakamoemiti ki tona ingoa tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:1">98:1</a> ¶ He himene. Waiatatia ki a Ihowa he waiata hou; he mahi whakamiharo hoki ana: na tona ringa matau, na tona ringa tapu, i taea ai e ia te whakaora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:2">98:2</a> Kua whakakitea e Ihowa tana whakaoranga, kua whakapuakina e ia tona tika ki te aroaro o nga tauiwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:3">98:3</a> Kua mahara ia ki tana mahi tohu, ki tona pono ki te whare o Iharaira; a kua kite nga pito katoa o te whenua i te whakaoranga a to tatou Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:4">98:4</a> ¶ Kia hari te hamama, e te whenua katoa, ki a Ihowa: hamama, kia hari, ae ra, himene atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:5">98:5</a> Himene ki a Ihowa i runga i te hapa; i runga i te hapa, me te himene ano te reo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:6">98:6</a> I runga i te tetere, i te tangi ano o te koronete: kia hari te hamama ki te aroaro o Ihowa, o te Kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:7">98:7</a> Kia haruru te moana me nga mea e hua ana i roto, te ao me ona tangata e noho ana i runga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:8">98:8</a> Kia papaki nga ringa o nga roma, kia hari tahi nga pukepuke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:9">98:9</a> Ki te aroaro o Ihowa: e haere mai ana hoki ia ki te whakawa mo te whenua: ka whakawa ia mo te ao i runga i te tika, mo nga iwi hoki i runga i te pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:1">99:1</a> ¶ Ko Ihowa te Kingi; kia wiri nga iwi: e noho ana ia i waenganui i nga kerupima; kia ngaueue te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:2">99:2</a> He nui a Ihowa i Hiona: kei runga ake ia i nga iwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:3">99:3</a> Kia whakamoemiti ratou ki tou ingoa nui, whakamataku; he tapu ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:4">99:4</a> E matenui ana hoki te kaha o te kingi ki te whakawa tika; ko koe hei whakapumau i te pono: he whakawa tika, he hekore tau mahi i roto i a Hakopa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:5">99:5</a> Whakanuia a Ihowa, to tatou Atua: koropiko ki tona turanga waewae; he tapu ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:6">99:6</a> ¶ Ko Mohi raua ko Arona i roto i ana tohunga, me Hamuera i roto i te hunga e karanga ana ki tona ingoa: i karanga ratou ki a Ihowa, a whakahoki kupu ana mai ia ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:7">99:7</a> I korero ia ki a ratou i roto i te pou kapua: i pupuri ratou i ana whakaaturanga, i te tikanga i whakatakotoria e ia ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:8">99:8</a> E Ihowa, e to matou Atua, i whakahoki kupu koe ki a ratou: he Atua tohu koe i a ratou, otiia i rapu utu ano koe mo a ratou mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:9">99:9</a> Whakanuia a Ihowa, to tatou Atua, koropiko atu i tona maunga tapu: he tapu hoki a Ihowa, to tatou Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:1">100:1</a> ¶ He himene whakamoemiti. Kia hari te hamama ki a Ihowa, e nga whenua katoa:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:2">100:2</a> Mahi atu ki a Ihowa i runga i te koa, waiata haere ki tona aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:3">100:3</a> Kia matau ki a Ihowa, ko ia te Atua: nana tatou i hanga, ehara hoki i a tatou: ko tana iwi tatou, ko ana hipi e hepara ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:4">100:4</a> Tomokia ona tatau i runga i te whakawhetai, ona marae i runga i te whakamoemiti: whakawhetai atu ki a ia, whakapaingia tona ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:5">100:5</a> He pai hoki a Ihowa, pumau tonu tana mahi tohu: a kei tena whakatupuranga, kei tena whakatupuranga, tona pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:1">101:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. Ka waiatatia e ahau te mahi tohu me te whakawa tika: ka himene atu ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:2">101:2</a> Ka ata whakahaere ahau i ahau i runga i te ara tika. A hea koe haere mai ai ki ahau? Ka haereere ahau i roto i toku whare i runga i te ngakau tapatahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:3">101:3</a> E kore te mea tutua e waiho e ahau i mua i oku kanohi; e kino ana ahau ki te mahi a te hunga peka ke: e kore e piri ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:4">101:4</a> Ka mawehe atu i ahau te ngakau parori ke: e kore ahau e mohio ki te mea kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:5">101:5</a> Ko te tangata e ngautuara puku ana ki tona hoa ka whakangaromia e ahau: e kore ahau e aro ki te tangata kanohi whakakake, ki te tangata ngakau whakapakari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:6">101:6</a> Kei runga i nga mea pono o te whenua oku kanohi, kia noho ai ratou ki ahau: ko te tangata e haere ana i te ara tika, ka mahi tena ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:7">101:7</a> E kore e noho ki toku whare te kaimahi i te hianga: e kore e tu ki toku aroaro te tangata korero teka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:8">101:8</a> I tenei ata, i tenei ata, ka whakangaromia e ahau nga tangata kikino katoa o te whenua: kia hatepea atu ai i te pa o te Atua te hunga katoa e mahi ana i te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:1">102:1</a> ¶ He inoi na te ngakau mamae, i a ia e pehia ana, a maringi a wai ana tana tangi ki te aroaro o Ihowa. Whakarongo ki taku inoi, e Ihowa, kia puta atu taku tangi ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:2">102:2</a> Kaua e huna tou mata ki ahau i te ra e pouri ai ahau; whakatitahatia mai tou taringa ki ahau: hohoro te whakahoki kupu mai ki ahau i te ra e karanga ai ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:3">102:3</a> Ka memeha hoki oku ra ano he paoa: ka kaia oku wheua ano he motumotu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:4">102:4</a> Kua pakia toku ngakau, kua memenge, ano he tarutaru; i wareware ai ahau ki te kai i taku taro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:5">102:5</a> Piri tonu oku iwi ki toku kiri i toku reo aue.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:6">102:6</a> He rite ahau ki te matuku i te koraha, ki te koukou i te wahi mokemoke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:7">102:7</a> Mataara tonu ahau; toku rite kei te pihoihoi mokemoke i runga i te tuanui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:8">102:8</a> E tawai ana oku hoariri ki ahau i te ra roa; ko te hunga e porangirangi ana mai ki ahau, ko ahau ta ratou oati.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:9">102:9</a> Kainga ana e ahau te pungarehu ano he taro: whakananua iho toku wai inu ki te roimata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:10">102:10</a> I tou riri hoki, i tou weriweri; nau hoki ahau i hapai ake, a taia atu ano ahau e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:11">102:11</a> He rite oku ra ki te atarangi e whakawairua kau ana: a kua memenge ahau ano he tarutaru.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:12">102:12</a> ¶ Ko koe ia, e Ihowa, ka mau tonu ake ake, ka maharatia ano koe e nga whakatupuranga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:13">102:13</a> Tera koe e whakatika, e aroha ki a Hiona; kua taka mai hoki te wa, ae ra, te tino wa, hei atawhainga i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:14">102:14</a> E manakohia ana hoki e au pononga ona kohatu, e awangawanga ana ki tona puehu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:15">102:15</a> Penei ka wehingia te ingoa o Ihowa e nga tauiwi, tou kororia hoki e nga kingi katoa o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:16">102:16</a> Na Ihowa hoki i hanga a Hiona, kua kitea ia i tona kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:17">102:17</a> Kua tahuri ia ki te inoi a te rawakore: kihai i whakahawea ki ta ratou inoi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:18">102:18</a> Ka tuhituhia tenei mo to muri whakatupuranga: a ka whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa te iwi meake hanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:19">102:19</a> Mona i titiro iho i te tiketike o tona wahi tapu: i titiro iho a Ihowa i te rangi ki te whenua;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:20">102:20</a> Ki te whakarongo ki te aue a te herehere, ki te wewete i te hunga kua motuhia mo te mate;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:21">102:21</a> Kia whakapuakina ai te ingo o Ihowa i Hiona, me te whakamoemiti ki a ia i Hiruharama;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:22">102:22</a> I te huihuinga o nga iwi, o nga kingitanga, ki te mahi ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:23">102:23</a> ¶ Whakangoikoretia iho e ia toku kaha i te ara: kua torutoru i a ia oku ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:24">102:24</a> I mea ahau, E toku Atua, kaua ahau e tangohia i waenganui o oku ra: kei nga whakatupuranga katoa ou tau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:25">102:25</a> Nonamata te whenua i whakaturia ai e koe, a he mahi nga rangi na ou ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:26">102:26</a> Ko era e hemo atu, ko koe ia e mau tonu: ae ra, ka tawhitotia katoatia me he weweru; ka whakaputaia ketia ratou e koe ano he kakahu, a ka whakaputaia ketia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:27">102:27</a> Ko koe ia, ko koe tonu, kahore hoki he mutunga o ou tau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:28">102:28</a> Ka whai nohoanga nga tama a au pononga, ka pumau o ratou uri ki tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:1">103:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e toku wairua; e nga mea katoa i roto i ahau, whakapaingia tona ingoa tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:2">103:2</a> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e toku wairua, kei wareware hoki ki ana painga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:3">103:3</a> Ko ia te muru nei i ou kino katoa; te rongo a nei i ou mate katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:4">103:4</a> Ko ia te hoko nei i tou ora kei ngaro; te karauna nei i a koe ki te atawhai, ki te aroha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:5">103:5</a> Nana nei i makona ai tou mangai i nga mea papai; i hou ai tou taitamarikitanga, i rite ai ki to te ekara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:6">103:6</a> ¶ Ka puta i a Ihowa nga mahi tika, me te whakawa tika ki te hunga katoa e tukinotia ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:7">103:7</a> I whakaakona e ia ana ara ki a Mohi, ana mahi ki nga tama a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:8">103:8</a> Ki tonu a Ihowa i te aroha me te atawhai, he puhoi ki te riri, he nui hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:9">103:9</a> E kore ia e whakatupuehupehu tonu, e kore ano e mauahara ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:10">103:10</a> Kihai i rite ki o tatou hara ana meatanga ki a tatou: kihai ano i rite ki o tatou kino ana utu mai ki a tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:11">103:11</a> He rite hoki ki te rangi e tiketike ake ana i te whenua, pera tonu te nui o tana mahi tohu ki te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:12">103:12</a> Pera i te matara o te rawhiti i te uru, pera tonu tana whakamataratanga atu i a tatou mahi tutu i a tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:13">103:13</a> E aroha ana te matua ki ana tamariki, pera tonu to Ihowa aroha ki te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:14">103:14</a> E matau ana hoki ia ki to tatou ahua, e mahara ana he puehu tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:15">103:15</a> Ko te tangata ia, rite tonu ona ra ki o te tarutaru: kei te puawai o te mara, ko tona ngawhatanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:16">103:16</a> E rarungatia ana hoki e te hau, a kua kahore; kahore hoki e mohiotia a muri e tona wahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:17">103:17</a> Tena ko te mahi tohu a Ihowa no tua whakarere, a ake tonu ake, ki te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia: tona tika hoki ki nga uri o nga tamariki;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:18">103:18</a> Ki te hunga e pupuri ana i tana kawenata, ki te hunga hoki e mahara ana ki ana ako kia mahia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:19">103:19</a> ¶ Kua oti i a Ihowa tona torona te whakatu ki nga rangi; a e kawanatia ana nga mea katoa e tona kingitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:20">103:20</a> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e ana anahera, e hira nei te kaha, e whakarite nei i tana kupu, e whakarongo nei ki tona reo ina korero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:21">103:21</a> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e ana mano katoa, e ana minita e mahi nei i tana e pai ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:22">103:22</a> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e ana mahi katoa i nga wahi katoa o tona kingitanga: whakapaingia a Ihowa, e toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:1">104:1</a> ¶ Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e toku wairua. E Ihowa, e toku Atua, he nui rawa koe; he honore, he kororia ou kakahu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:2">104:2</a> E roropi nei i te marama ki a koe ano he kakahu, e hora nei i nga rangi ano he kakahu tauarai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:3">104:3</a> E whakanoho nei i nga kurupae o ona ruma ki nga wai: e mea nei i nga kapua hei hariata mona: e haere nei i runga i nga pakau o te hau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:4">104:4</a> E mea nei i nga hau hei karere mana, i te mura ahi hei kaimahi mana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:5">104:5</a> Nana nei i whakatu te whenua ki runga ki ona turanga, kei nekenekehia ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:6">104:6</a> Nau ano i hipoki ki te rire hei kakahu: tu ana nga wai i runga i nga maunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:7">104:7</a> Rere ana ratou i tau riri: tahuti tonu atu i te reo o tau whatitiri;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:8">104:8</a> Puke ake ana ra nga maunga, heke iho ana ma nga whawharua ki te wahi i whakaritea e koe mo ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:9">104:9</a> Kua whakatakotoria e koe he rohe kei koni mai ratou, kei hoki mai hei taupoki mo te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:10">104:10</a> ¶ Nana i tono nga puna ki roto ki nga awaawa, e rere nei i waenga o nga puke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:11">104:11</a> Hei wai mo nga kirehe katoa o te parae: na noa te matewai o nga kaihe mohoao.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:12">104:12</a> Kei reira nga nohoanga o nga manu o te rangi, e korihi nei i roto i nga manga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:13">104:13</a> He mea whakamakuku nana nga puke i ona ruma: ka makona te whenua i nga hua o au mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:14">104:14</a> Ko ia hei whakatupu i te tarutaru ma te kararehe, i te otaota hei mea ma te tangata; kia whakaputaina ake ai he taro i te whenua;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:15">104:15</a> He waina hei whakahari i te ngakau o te tangata, he hinu e piata ai tona mata, me te taro hei whakakaha i te ngakau o te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:16">104:16</a> Ki tonu i te wai nga rakau a Ihowa, nga hita o Repanona i whakatokia e ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:17">104:17</a> Hanga ake e nga manu he ohanga ki reira: te taaka, ko nga kauri tona whare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:18">104:18</a> Hei piringa nga puke tiketike mo nga koati mohoao: nga kohatu mo nga rapeti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:19">104:19</a> ¶ I hanga e ia te marama hei tohu taima: e matau ana te ra ki tona torengitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:20">104:20</a> Ko koe hei whakapouri, a kua po: na ngoki mai ana nga kirehe katoa o te ngahere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:21">104:21</a> Ko nga kuao raiona ngengere ana ratou, he mea kai, he rapu kai ma ratou i te Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:22">104:22</a> Ko te putanga mai o te ra ka poto atu ratou, takoto ana i o ratou kuhunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:23">104:23</a> Ko te tangata ka haere ki ana hanga, ki tana mahi, a ahiahi noa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:24">104:24</a> Ano te tini o au mahi, e Ihowa! he mohio rawa tau mahi i aua mea katoa; ki tonu te whenua i au taonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:25">104:25</a> Kei ko ra ko te moana, tona nui tuauriuri: kei reira nga mea ngokingoki e kore e taea te tatau, nga kirehe hoki, ana nonohi, ana nunui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:26">104:26</a> Kei reira nga kaipuke e teretere ana: kei reira taua rewiatana i hanga e koe hei takaro ki reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:27">104:27</a> E tatari katoa ana enei ki a koe, kia hoatu e koe te kai ma ratou i te wa e tika ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:28">104:28</a> Ko tau e hoatu ai ma ratou, kohikohia ana e ratou: te wherahanga o tou ringa, makona tonu ratou i te pai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:29">104:29</a> Ko te hunanga o tou mata, pororaru ana ratou: ka kapohia e koe to ratou manawa, ka marere ratou, a ka hoki ano ki to ratou puehu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:30">104:30</a> Ko tau tononga mai i tou wairua, kua hanga ratou; a whakahoutia ana e koe te mata o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:31">104:31</a> ¶ Kia whai kororia a Ihowa ake ake, kia hari a Ihowa ki ana mahi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:32">104:32</a> Tana tirohanga iho ki te whenua, ru ana: kua pa ki nga puke, na pongere ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:33">104:33</a> Ka waiata ahau ki a Ihowa i ahau e ora ana: ka himene ki toku Atua i ahau ano i te ao nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:34">104:34</a> Kia reka toku whakaaronga ki a ia, ka hari ahau ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:35">104:35</a> Kia moti nga tangata hara i runga i te whenua, ko te hunga kino kia poto katoa atu. Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e toku wairua. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:1">105:1</a> ¶ Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, karanga atu ki tona ingoa: whakapuakina ana mahi ki waenganui o nga iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:2">105:2</a> Waiata ki a ia, himene ki a ia: korerotia ana mahi whakamiharo katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:3">105:3</a> Whakamanamana ki tona ingoa tapu: kia hari te ngakau o te hunga e rapu ana i a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:4">105:4</a> Rapua a Ihowa me tona kaha: rapua tonutia tona mata, ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:5">105:5</a> Maharatia ana mahi whakamiharo i mahia e ia; ana merekara me nga whakaritenga a tona mangai,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:6">105:6</a> E nga uri o Aperahama, o tana pononga, e nga tama a Hakopa, e ana i whiriwhiri ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:7">105:7</a> Ko Ihowa ia, ko to tatou Atua; kei te whenua katoa ana whakaritenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:8">105:8</a> ¶ Mahara tonu ia ki tana kawenata ake ake, ki te kupu i kiia iho e ia ki te mano o nga whakatupuranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:9">105:9</a> Ki tana i whakarite ai ki a Aperahama, ki tana oati hoki ki a Ihaka;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:10">105:10</a> A whakapumautia iho e ia hei tikanga ki a Hakopa, hei kawenata mau tonu ki a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:11">105:11</a> I a ia ra i mea, Ka hoatu e ahau ki a koe te whenua o Kanaana hei wahi pumau mo koutou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:12">105:12</a> I te mea he hunga torutoru ratou: ae ra, he iti rawa, he manene ano ki reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:13">105:13</a> I a ratou e haereere ana i tenei iwi ki tera atu iwi, i tetahi rangatiratanga ki tetahi iwi ke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:14">105:14</a> Kihai ratou i tukua e ia kia tukinotia e te tangata: he whakaaro ano ki a ratou i riria ai e ia nga kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:15">105:15</a> I mea ia, Kei pa ki aku i whakawahi ai: kei kino ki aku poropiti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:16">105:16</a> I karangatia e ia te matekai ki te whenua: whati katoa i a ia te tokotoko, ara te taro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:17">105:17</a> I tonoa e ia he tangata i mua i a ratou; i hokona a Hohepa hei pononga:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:18">105:18</a> I whakamamaetia ona waewae ki te mekameka: takoto ana ia i te rino;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:19">105:19</a> A puta noa tana kupu: whakamatautauria ana ia e te kupu a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:20">105:20</a> I tono te kingi, a wetekina ana ia; ara te kingi o nga iwi, a tukua ana ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:21">105:21</a> A meinga ana ia e ia hei ariki mo tona whare, hei rangatira mo ona taonga katoa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:22">105:22</a> Hei herehere i ana rangatira ua pai ia, hei ako i ana kaumatua ki te whakaaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:23">105:23</a> I haere mai ano a Iharaira ki Ihipa: a noho ana a Hakopa ki te whenua o Hama.</p>
