 <p><a name="an_105:24">105:24</a> Na ka tino whakanuia e ia tana iwi: a ka meinga ratou kia kaha ake i o ratou hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:25">105:25</a> ¶ I whakakoarotia e ia to ratou ngakau kia kino ki tana iwi, kia mahi lhianga ki ana pononga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:26">105:26</a> I tonoa e ia a Mohi, tana pononga, raua ko Arona, ko tana i whiriwhiri ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:27">105:27</a> Whakaputaina ana e raua ana tohu i waenganui i a ratou, he merekara i te whenua o Hama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:28">105:28</a> I tukua e ia te pouri, a kua pouri: kihai ano ratou i whakakeke ki ana kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:29">105:29</a> I whakaputaia ketia e ia o ratou wai hei toto; a mate ake i a ia a ratou ngohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:30">105:30</a> I whakangahue ake to ratou whenua i te poroka, i roto i nga whare moenga o o ratou kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:31">105:31</a> I whai kupu ia, a puta ana mai nga pokai namu: me te kutu i o ratou kainga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:32">105:32</a> I tukua iho e ia ki a ratou te whatu hei ua, me te ahi mura ki to ratou whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:33">105:33</a> I pakia ano e ia a ratou waina me a ratou piki; a whatiwhatiia ana e ia nga rakau o o ratou kainga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:34">105:34</a> I korero ia, a puta ana mai te mawhitiwhiti me te moka, te taea te tatau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:35">105:35</a> A kainga katoatia ana nga otaota o to ratou whenua; pau ake nga hua o to ratou oneone.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:36">105:36</a> I whakamatea katoatia ano hoki e ia nga matamua o to ratou whenua, te muanga o to ratou kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:37">105:37</a> A whakaputaina mai ana ratou e ia, me te hiriwa, me te koura, kahore hoki he mea tuoi i roto i ana iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:38">105:38</a> Na hari ana a Ihipa i to ratou haerenga; i mau hoki to ratou wehi ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:39">105:39</a> I horahia e ia te kapua hei hipoki, me te ahi hei whakamarama i te po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:40">105:40</a> I inoi ratou, a homai ana e ia te koitareke; a ka makona ratou i te taro o te rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:41">105:41</a> I wahia e ia te kohatu, a ka pakaru mai nga wai: rere ana i nga wahi maroke, koia ano kei te awa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:42">105:42</a> I mahara hoki ia ki tana kuputapu, ki a Aperahama ano, ki tana pononga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:43">105:43</a> A whakaputaina mai ana e ia tana iwi i runga i te hari, ana i whiriwhiri ai i runga i te koa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:44">105:44</a> A homai ana e ia ki a ratou nga whenua o nga tauiwi: a riro ana i a ratou nga mauiuitanga o te iwi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:45">105:45</a> Kia puritia ai e ratou ana tikanga, kia mau ai ki ana ture. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:1">106:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa; he pai hoki ia: he pumau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:2">106:2</a> Me wai e korero nga mahi nunui a Ihowa: e whakakite katoa nga whakamoemiti ki a ia?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:3">106:3</a> Ka hari te hunga e mau ana ki te whakarite tika; me te kaimahi i te tika i nga wa katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:4">106:4</a> Maharatia mai ahau, e Ihowa, kia rite ki tau manako ki tau iwi: tirotirohia mai ahau i runga i tau whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:5">106:5</a> Kia kite ai ahau i te pai o au i whiriwhiri ai: kia koa ai, koa tahi me tau iwi; kia whakamanamana tahi ai me tou kainga tupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:6">106:6</a> ¶ Kua hara tahi matou me o matou matua, kua mahi matou i te kino, i te mea he.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:7">106:7</a> Kihai o matou matua i mohio ki au mea whakamiharo i Ihipa, kihai hoki i mahara ki te tini o au arohatanga; engari ia i whakatoi ratou ki a koe i te moana, ae, i te Moana Whero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:8">106:8</a> Otira whakaorangia ana ratou e ia, he whakaaro ki tona ingoa, kia matauria ai tona kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:9">106:9</a> I riria ano e ia te Moana Whero, a kua maroke: na arahina ana ratou e ia i nga rire, ano ko waenga koraha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:10">106:10</a> Na whakaorangia ake ratou e ia i te ringa o te tangata i kino ki a ratou; a hokona ana ratou i roto i te ringa o te hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:11">106:11</a> A taupokina ana e nga wai o ratou hoariri, hore rawa tetahi morehu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:12">106:12</a> Na whakapono ana ratou ki ana kupu: a waiata ana i te whakamoemiti ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:13">106:13</a> ¶ Hohoro tonu to ratou wareware ki ana mahi: kihai i taria e ratou tona whakaaro:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:14">106:14</a> Engari i whakaputa nui i o ratou hiahia i te tahora; whakamatautau ana ratou i te Atua i te koraha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:15">106:15</a> Na ka hoatu e ia ta ratou i inoi ai; otira i tukua atu e ia te hiroki ki to ratou wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:16">106:16</a> I hae hoki ratou ki a Mohi i te puni, ki a Arona ano, ki te tangata tapu a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:17">106:17</a> Ko te hamamatanga o te whenua, na horomia ana a Ratana; a taupokina iho te ropu o Apirama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:18">106:18</a> A mura ana te ahi i to ratou ropu; wera ana i te mura te hunga kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:19">106:19</a> I hanga e ratou he kuao kau ki Horepa, a koropiko ana ki te whakapakoko i whakarewaina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:20">106:20</a> Koia i whitia ai e ratou to ratou kororia mo te mea i rite ki te puru kai tarutaru.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:21">106:21</a> Wareware ake i a ratou te Atua, to ratou kaiwhakaora, i mahi nei i nga mea nunui ki Ihipa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:22">106:22</a> I nga mahi whakamiharo ki te whenua o Hama, i nga mea whakamataku ki te Moana Whero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:23">106:23</a> Na ka mea ia, kia whakangaromia ratou, me i kaua a Mohi, tana i whiriwhiri ai, te tu ki tona aroaro i te takiwa, hei papare ake i tona riri, kei huna ratou e ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:24">106:24</a> Ae ra, i whakahawea ratou ki te whenua ahuareka; kihai ratou i whakapono ki tana kupu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:25">106:25</a> Heoi amuamu ana i roto i o ratou teneti, kihai i whakarongo ki te reo o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:26">106:26</a> Na reira ka ara tona ringa ki a ratou, ki te turaki i a ratou i te koraha;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:27">106:27</a> Ki te turaki i o ratou uri i roto i nga iwi: ki te whakamarara i a ratou ki nga whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:28">106:28</a> I whakauru atu hoki ratou ki a Paarapeoro: a kai ana i nga patunga tapu ma nga mea mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:29">106:29</a> Koia i whakapataritari ai ratou i a ia ki a ratou hanga kia riri; a pakaru ana mai te mate uruta ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:30">106:30</a> Na ko te whakatikanga ake o Pinehaha, ki te whakaputa whakawa: a mutu iho te mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:31">106:31</a> I kiia ai ia he tika i nga whakatupuranga katoa ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:32">106:32</a> I whakapataritari ano ratou i a ia ki nga wai o Meripa; na hemanawa ana a Mohi mo ratou:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:33">106:33</a> Na ratou hoki i whakatoi tona wairua, i he ai te kupu a ona ngutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:34">106:34</a> ¶ Kihai ratou i whakangaro i nga iwi i kiia nei e Ihowa ki a ratou;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:35">106:35</a> Heoi uru ana ki roto ki nga tauiwi, a ako ana i a ratou mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:36">106:36</a> I mahi hoki ratou ki a ratou whakapakoko, i mahangatia ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:37">106:37</a> Ae, i patua e ratou a ratou tama me a ratou tamahine ma nga atua maori;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:38">106:38</a> I whakahekea hoki te toto harakore, nga toto o a ratou tama, o a ratou tamahine, i patua nei e ratou ma nga whakapakoko o Kanaana; a poke iho te whenua i te toto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:39">106:39</a> Na poke iho ratou i a ratou mahi: a puremu ana ki a ratou mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:40">106:40</a> Koia i mura ai te riri o Ihowa ki tana iwi; a whakarihariha ana ia ki tona kainga tupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:41">106:41</a> A tukua ana ratou e ia ki te ringa o nga tauiwi; waiho ana te hunga i kino ki a ratou hei rangatira mo ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:42">106:42</a> Na ka tukinotia ratou e o ratou hoariri: ka pehia ki raro i o ratou ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:43">106:43</a> He maha ana whakaoranga i a ratou: ko ratou ia i whakatoi ki a ia i o ratou whakaaro, a whakaititia ana i ta ratou kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:44">106:44</a> Ahakoa ra, i titiro ia ki to ratou matenga, i tona rongonga i ta ratou tangi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:45">106:45</a> I mahara hoki ia ki tana kawenata ki a ratou, a rite tonu ki te tini o ana mahi aroha te putanga ketanga o ona whakaaro:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:46">106:46</a> I meinga hoki ratou e ia kia arohaina e te hunga katoa i whakaraua atu ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:47">106:47</a> Whakaorangia matou, e Ihowa, e to matou Atua, kohikohia matou i roto i nga tauiwi: kia whakawhetai ai ki tou ingoa tapu, kia whakamanamana ai ki tou whakamoemiti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:48">106:48</a> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, te Atua o Iharaira, i tua whakarere ano, a ake ake. A kia mea katoa te iwi, Amine. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:1">107:1</a> ¶ Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, he pai hoki ia: he pumau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:2">107:2</a> Kia pena ano te korero a te hunga i hokona e Ihowa, i hokona nei e ia i roto i te ringa o te hoariri;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:3">107:3</a> I kohikohia nei i nga whenua, i te rawhiti, i te uru, i te raki, i te tonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:4">107:4</a> I haereere ratou i te koraha i te wahi mokemoke, te kitea tetahi pa hei nohoanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:5">107:5</a> I matekai ratou, i matewai: hemo noa to ratou wairua i roto i a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:6">107:6</a> Na ka tangi ratou ki a Ihowa i to ratou pouri: a whakaorangia ana ratou e ia i o ratou mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:7">107:7</a> A arahina ana e ia ra te ara tika; kia haere ai ki te pa hei nohoanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:8">107:8</a> Aue! me i whakapaingia e te tangata a Ihowa mo tona atawhai, mo ana mahi whakamiharo ki nga tama a te tangata!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:9">107:9</a> E whakamakonatia ana hoki e ia te wairua hiahia: ko te wairua hiakai, whakakiia ana e ia ki te pai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:10">107:10</a> ¶ Ko te hunga i noho i te pouri, i te atarangi o te mate: he mea here ki te mamae, ki te rino;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:11">107:11</a> Mo ratou i tutu ki nga kupu a te Atua, i whakahawea ki te whakaaro o te Runga Rawa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:12">107:12</a> Koia i pehia iho ai e ia o ratou ngakau ki te mahi: hinga iho ratou, kahore hoki he kaiawhina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:13">107:13</a> Na ka tangi ratou ki a Ihowa i to ratou pouri; a ka whakaorangia ratou e ia i o ratou mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:14">107:14</a> Whakaputaina mai ana ratou e ia i te pouri, i te atarangi o te mate; motumotuhia ana o ratou here.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:15">107:15</a> Aue! me i whakapaingia e te tangata a Ihowa mo tona atawhai, mo ana mahi whakamiharo ki nga tama a te tangata!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:16">107:16</a> Kua tukitukia hoki e ia nga tatau parahi: kua tapahia e ia nga tutaki rino, motu rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:17">107:17</a> ¶ Ko nga kuware, na a ratou mahi tutu, na o ratou kino, i pakia ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:18">107:18</a> Ka wetiweti to ratou wairua ki nga kai katoa; a ka whakatata ratou ki nga kuwaha o te mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:19">107:19</a> Na ka tangi ki a Ihowa i to ratou pouri, a ka whakaorangia ratou e ia i o ratou mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:20">107:20</a> Tukua mai ana e ia tana kupu, a rongoatia ana ratou: a whakaputaina ana ratou i o ratou ngaromanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:21">107:21</a> Aue! me i whakapaingia e te tangata a Ihowa mo tona atawhai, mo ana mahi whakamiharo ki nga tama a te tangata!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:22">107:22</a> Kia tukua ano e ratou te whakahere, ara te whakamoemiti; kia whakapuaki i ana mahi i runga i te hari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:23">107:23</a> ¶ Ko te hunga e haere ana ki raro, ki te moana, i runga kaipuke, a e whai mahi ana i nga wai nunui,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:24">107:24</a> Ko ratou e kite i nga mahi a Ihowa, i ana mahi whakamiharo i te rire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:25">107:25</a> Puta kau tana kupu, kua maranga te tupuhi, mana e whakatutu ona ngaru.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:26">107:26</a> Ka kake ratou ki runga ki te rangi, ka heke ano ki raro ki te rire: ngohe noa o ratou wairua i te pawera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:27">107:27</a> Ka tiu ratou, ka hurorirori ano he tangata e haurangi ana; a kahore he mahara i toe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:28">107:28</a> Heoi ka tangi ki a Ihowa i to ratou hemanawa: a whakaorangia ana ratou i o ratou mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:29">107:29</a> Meinga ana e ia te tupuhi kia marino, ona ngaru kia mariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:30">107:30</a> Na ka koa ratou, no te mea ka marie: a ka kawea ratou e ia ki te tauranga i hiahia ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:31">107:31</a> Aue! me i whakapaingia e te tangata a Ihowa mo tona atawhai, mo ana mahi whakamiharo ki nga tama a te tangata!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:32">107:32</a> Kia whakanui hoki ratou i a ia i roto i te whakaminenga o te iwi; kia whakamoemiti ki a ia i roto i te nohoanga kaumatua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:33">107:33</a> ¶ Ko ia hei mea i nga awa hei koraha, i nga puputanga wai hei oneone maroke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:34">107:34</a> I te whenua whai hua, kia titohea, mo te hara o te hunga e noho ana i reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:35">107:35</a> Ko ia hei mea i te koraha hei harotoroto wai, i te whenua maroke hei puputanga wai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:36">107:36</a> A whakanohoia iho e ia te hunga matekai ki reira, hanga ai i tetahi pa hei nohoanga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:37">107:37</a> Hei rui mara, hei whakato mara waina, e tupu ai, e maha ai nga hua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:38">107:38</a> Ko ia ano hei manaaki i a ratou, no ka nui rawa; kahore hoki e tukua kia torutoru haere a ratou kararehe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:39">107:39</a> Na kua iti haere ano ratou, kua piko i te tukino, i te he, i te pouri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:40">107:40</a> E ringihia ana e ia te whakahawea ki runga ki nga rangatira: e meinga ana kia hehe i te ururua, i te wahi kahore nei he ara;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:41">107:41</a> Otira kei te whakateitei ia i te rawakore ki runga i te mamae, kei te mea i ona hapu kia rite ki te kahui hipi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:42">107:42</a> Ka kite nga tangata tika, a ka hari; ko nga he katoa hoki, kipia ake te mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:43">107:43</a> Ko te tangata whakaaro nui ka mahara ki enei mea, a ka mohio ratou ki te aroha o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:1">108:1</a> ¶ He waiata, he himene na Rawiri. Pumau tonu toku ngakau, e te Atua; ka waiata ahau, ae ra, ka himene ahau, me toku kororia ano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:2">108:2</a> E ara, e te hatere, e te hapa: ka ara wawe ano ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:3">108:3</a> Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa, i waenganui i nga iwi: ka himene ki a koe i waenganui i nga tauiwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:4">108:4</a> He nui atu hoki tau mahi tohu i nga rangi, a ko tou pono tutuki noa atu ki nga kapua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:5">108:5</a> Kia whakanuia koe, e te Atua, ki runga atu i nga rangi: hei runga atu i te whenua katoa tou kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:6">108:6</a> ¶ Kia puta tau i aroha ai, ma tou ringa matau matou e whakaora, a whakahokia mai he kupu ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:7">108:7</a> Kua korero te Atua i runga i tona tapu: Ka hari ahau, ka kotikoti i Hekeme, ka roherohe i te raorao o Hukota.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:8">108:8</a> Noku Kireara; noku a Manahi; ko Eparaima ano hoki te kaha o toku matenga; ko Hura taku hepeta.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:9">108:9</a> Ko Moapa taku oko horoi; ka maka e ahau toku hu ki runga ki Eroma: ka whakamanamana ahau ki Pirihitia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:10">108:10</a> Ma wai ahau e kawe ki te pa tuwatawata? Ko wai nana ahau i arahi ki Eroma?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:11">108:11</a> He teka ianei kua panga matou e koe, e te Atua? kahore hoki koe, e te Atua, e haere tahi me o matou taua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:12">108:12</a> Homai ki a matou he awhina ki te hoariri: he teka kau noa hoki te awhina a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:13">108:13</a> Ma te Atua tatou ka toa ai: mana hoki e takahi ki raro o tatou hoa whawhai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:1">109:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. E te Atua, e whakamoemiti nei ahau, kei wahangu koe:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:2">109:2</a> Kua puaki hoki te mangai o te tangata kino me te mangai o te tangata tinihanga, ki te he moku: he teka o ratou arero, e korero nei moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:3">109:3</a> I karapotia hoki ahau e ratou ki nga kupu mauahara, a i whawhai takekore ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:4">109:4</a> Mo toku aroha he riri ta ratou whakautu: ko ahau ia, he inoi taku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:5">109:5</a> E homai ana e ratou ki ahau he kino mo te pai, he mauahara mo toku aroha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:6">109:6</a> ¶ Meinga he tangata kino hei rangatira mona; kia tu he hoariri ki tona ringa matau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:7">109:7</a> Kia tau te he ki a ia, ina whakawakia: kia waiho ano tana inoi hei hara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:8">109:8</a> Kia torutoru ona ra; kia riro tana mahi tirotiro i tetahi atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:9">109:9</a> Kia pania ana tamariki, kia pouarutia hoki tana wahine.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:10">109:10</a> Kia kopikopiko noa ana tamariki, pinono ai: kia rapu kai hoki ma ratou i o ratou wahi mokemoke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:11">109:11</a> Kia haoa e te kaituku moni ana mea katoa; kia pahuatia hoki e nga tangata iwi ke ana mauiuitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:12">109:12</a> Kaua tetahi hei hoatu noa i te aroha ki a ia: kaua hoki tetahi hei atawhai i ana pani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:13">109:13</a> Kia hatepea putia ona uri: a i to muri whakatupuranga kia horoia rawatia atu o ratou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:14">109:14</a> Kia maharatia e Ihowa te kino o ona matua: kei murua hoki te hara o tona whaea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:15">109:15</a> Kia mau tonu ki te aroaro o Ihowa: kia hatepea atu ai e ia te maharatanga ki a ratou i runga i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:16">109:16</a> Mona kihai i mahara ki te mahi tohu: heoi tukino ana ia i te ware, i te rawakore, i te hunga ngakau maru, kia patua ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:17">109:17</a> Ae ra, i pai ia ki te kanga, a kua tae mai ki a ia: kihai ia i aro ki te manaaki, heoi kua mamao tera i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:18">109:18</a> I kakahu ia i te kanga ki a ia, ano ko tona kakahu: na kua tae tera ki roto ki a ia ano he wai, me he hinu hoki ki roto ki ona wheua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:19">109:19</a> Waiho ki a ia hei kakahu hipoki mona, hei whitiki hoki e whitikiria tonutia ai ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:20">109:20</a> Na hei utu tena ma Ihowa ki oku hoariri, ki te hunga hoki e korero kino nei ki toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:21">109:21</a> ¶ Kia puta tau mahi moku, e te Atua, e te Ariki, he whakaaro ki tou ingoa: na te mea he pai tau mahi tohu, whakaorangia ahau,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:22">109:22</a> He ware hoki ahau, he rawakore, kua mamae hoki toku ngakau i roto i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:23">109:23</a> Ka riro ahau me te atarangi e whakawairua kau ana: e peipeia ana ahau me he mawhitiwhiti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:24">109:24</a> Hurorirori kau oku turi i te nohopuku; a e kohia ana te ngako o oku kikokiko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:25">109:25</a> Kua waiho ahau hei tawainga ma ratou: ka kite ratou i ahau, ka ruru o ratou matenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:26">109:26</a> Awhinatia ahau, e Ihowa, e toku Atua: kia rite ki tou aroha tau whakaora i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:27">109:27</a> Kia matau ai ratou ko tou ringa itene: a nau tenei, e Ihowa, i mea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:28">109:28</a> Ma ratou e kanga, mau ia e manaaki: kia whakama ratou ina whakatika; ko tau pononga ia kia hari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:29">109:29</a> Kia whakakakahuria oku hoariri ki te whakama, a ko to ratou numinumi hei koroka hipoki mo ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:30">109:30</a> Ka tino whakawhetai toku mangai ki a Ihowa, ae ra, ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a ia i waenganui o te mano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:31">109:31</a> E tu hoki ia ki te ringa matau o te rawakore, hei whakaora i a ia i te hunga e whakahe ana i tona wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:1">110:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. I mea a Ihowa ki toku Ariki: Hei toku matau koe noho ai, kia meinga ra ano e ahau ou hoariri hei turanga waewae mou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:2">110:2</a> Ma Ihowa e tono mai te tokotoko o tou kaha i Hiona: hei rangatira koe i waenganui i ou hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:3">110:3</a> Ka kakama tou iwi ki te tapae atu i a ratou i te ra o tou kaha: i te ataahua o nga mea tapu, no te kopu mai o te ata, kei a koe te tomairangi o tou whanaketanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:4">110:4</a> Kua oati a Ihowa, e kore ano tana e puta ke; Hei tohunga koe ake ake, no te tikanga o Merekihereke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:5">110:5</a> ¶ Kei tou matau te Ariki, ka maru i a ia nga kingi i te ra e riri ai ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:6">110:6</a> E whakawa ia i waenganui i nga tauiwi; e whakakiia e ia nga whenua ki te tupapaku: ka maru i a ia nga upoko i nga whenua maha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:7">110:7</a> Ka inu wai ia i te awa i te ara: a ka ara tona matenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:1">111:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Ka whakapaua toku ngakau ki te whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, i te runanga o te hunga tika, i te whakaminenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:2">111:2</a> He nui nga mahi a Ihowa; e whakatakina ana e te hunga katoa e manako ana ki aua mea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:3">111:3</a> He mea honore, he mea kororia tana mahi: tu tonu tona tika ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:4">111:4</a> Kua meinga e ia kia maharatia ana mahi whakamiharo: he atawhai a Ihowa, he aroha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:5">111:5</a> E homai ana e ia he kai ma te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia: ka mahara tonu ia ki tana kawenata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:6">111:6</a> ¶ Kua whakakitea e ia ki tana iwi te kaha o ana mahi, i tana hoatutanga i to nga tauiwi hei kainga tupu mo ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:7">111:7</a> Ko nga mahi a ona ringa he pono, he whakawa tika: pono tonu ana akoranga katoa,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:8">111:8</a> U tonu ake ake, e mahia ana i runga i te pono, i te tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:9">111:9</a> I tonoa mai e ia he whakaoranga mo tana iwi: kua kiia iho e ia tana kawenata mo ake tonu atu; he tapu tona ingoa, e wehingia ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:10">111:10</a> Ko te timatanga o te whakaaro nui he wehi ki a Ihowa: he ngarahu nui to te hunga katoa nana era mahi; mau te whakamoemiti ki a ia, ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:1">112:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Ka hari te tangata e wehi ana i a Ihowa, e aro nui ana ki ana whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:2">112:2</a> Ka nui ona uri ki runga ki te whenua; ka manaakitia te whakatupuranga o te hunga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:3">112:3</a> Kei tona whare te rawa, te taonga: ka pumau tonu tona tika, ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:4">112:4</a> Ka maea ake te marama i roto i te pouri ki te hunga tika: he atawhai ia, he aroha, he tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:5">112:5</a> He pono ka whiwhi painga te tangata he atawhai, he ohaoha tana mahi: ka u ana kupu i te whakawakanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:6">112:6</a> ¶ E kore hoki ia e whakangaueuetia ake ake: ka maharatia tonutia te tangata tika ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:7">112:7</a> E kore ia e mataku i te rongo kino: e u ana tona ngakau, e whakawhirinaki ana ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:8">112:8</a> Ka u tona ngakau, e kore ia e wehi, kia kite ra ano ia i tana i hiahia ai ki ona hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:9">112:9</a> Kua tuwhaina e ia, kua hoatu ki te hunga rawakore: pumau tonu tona tika ake ake; ka ara tona haona i runga i te kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:10">112:10</a> Ka kite te tangata kino, a ka pouri; ka pakiri ona niho, memeha iho: pirau iho te hiahia o te hunga kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:1">113:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Whakamoemititia, e nga pononga a Ihowa, whakamoemititia te ingoa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:2">113:2</a> Kia whakapaingia te ingo o Ihowa aianei a ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:3">113:3</a> Kia whakamoemititia te ingoa o Ihowa i te putanga mai o te ra, a tae noa ki tona torengitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:4">113:4</a> Kei runga rawa a Ihowa i nga iwi katoa: kei runga ake i nga rangi tona kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:5">113:5</a> Ko wai te rite ana ki a Ihowa, ki to tatou Atua, kei runga nei tona nohoanga,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:6">113:6</a> E whakaiti nei i a ia ki te titiro iho ki nga mea kei te rangi, kei te whenua?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:7">113:7</a> E whakaara ake ana ia i te iti i roto i te puehu, e whakateitei ake ana i te rawakore i roto i te puranga paru;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:8">113:8</a> Kia whakanohoia ai e ia ki roto ki nga rangatira, ki nga rangatira o tana iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:9">113:9</a> Nana hoki te pakoko i whai whare ai, hei whaereere e koa ana ki ana tamariki. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:1">114:1</a> ¶ I te putanga mai o Iharaira i Ihipa, o te whare o Hakopa i te iwi reo ke,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:2">114:2</a> Ko Hura tona wahi tapu, ko Iharaira tona rangatiratanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:3">114:3</a> I kite te moana, a whati ana: i whakahokia ki muri a Horano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:4">114:4</a> Pekepeke ana nga maunga ano he hipi toa, nga pukepuke ano he reme.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:5">114:5</a> I ahatia koe, e te moana, i whati ai koe e Horano, i whakahokia ai koe ki muri?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:6">114:6</a> E nga maunga, i pekepeke ai koutou ano he hipi toa; e nga pukepuke, ano he reme?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:7">114:7</a> E wiri, e te whenua, i te aroaro o te Ariki; i te aroaro o te Atua o Hakopa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:8">114:8</a> I meinga ai te toka hei hopua wai; te kiripaka hei puna wai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:1">115:1</a> ¶ Aua ki a matou, e Ihowa, aua ki a matou, engari me hoatu te kororia ki tou ingoa: whakaaroa tou aroha, tou pono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:2">115:2</a> Kia mea koia nga tauiwi: Kei hea ianei to ratou Atua?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:3">115:3</a> Kei te rangi ia to matou Atua; kua meatia e ia nga mea katoa i pai ai ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:4">115:4</a> He hiriwa a ratou whakapakoko, he koura, he mahi na te ringa tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:5">115:5</a> He mangai o ratou, a kahore e korero: he kanohi o ratou, a kahore e kite:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:6">115:6</a> He taringa o ratou, a kahore e rongo: he ihu o ratou, a kahore e hongi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:7">115:7</a> He ringa o ratou, a kahore e whawha: he waewae o ratou, a kahore e haere: kahore hoki o ratou korokoro e korero.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:8">115:8</a> Ka rite ki a ratou o ratou kaihanga; ae ra, te hunga katoa ano e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:9">115:9</a> ¶ E Iharaira, whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa: ko ia to ratou awhina, to ratou whakangungu rakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:10">115:10</a> E te whare o Arona, whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa: ko ia to ratou awhina, to ratou whakangungu rakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:11">115:11</a> E te hunga e wehi ana i a Ihowa, whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa: ko ia to ratou awhina, to ratou whakangungu rakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:12">115:12</a> Kua mahara a Ihowa ki a tatou, mana tatou e manaaki: mana e manaaki te whare o Iharaira, mana e manaaki te whare o Arona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:13">115:13</a> Ka manaakitia e ia te hunga e wehi ana ki a Ihowa, te iti, te rahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:14">115:14</a> Ka tapiritia ano e Ihowa ki a koutou, ki a koutou tahi ko a koutou tamariki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:15">115:15</a> He manaakitanga koutou na Ihowa, na te kaihanga o te rangi, o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:16">115:16</a> Ko nga rangi, he rangi no Ihowa; ko te whenua ia, he mea homai nana ki nga tama a te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:17">115:17</a> E kore nga tupapaku e whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa: me te hunga katoa ano e heke ana ki te wahangutanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:18">115:18</a> Ko matou ia ka whakapai ki a Ihowa aianei a ake ake. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:1">116:1</a> ¶ E aroha ana ahau ki a Ihowa: mona i whakarongo ki toku reo, ki aku inoi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:2">116:2</a> I tahuri mai tona taringa ki ahau: mo reira ka karanga ahau ki a ia i ahau e ora ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:3">116:3</a> I karapotia ahau e nga whakawiringa a te mate: mau pu ahau i nga mamae o te reinga, i kite ahau i te pawera, i te pouri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:4">116:4</a> Na ko taku karangatanga ki te ingoa o Ihowa; Tena ra, e Ihowa, whakaorangia toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:5">116:5</a> He atawhai a Ihowa, he tika: ae, he aroha to tatou Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:6">116:6</a> E tiakina ana e Ihowa te hunga kuware: i whakaititia ahau, a nana ahau i whakaora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:7">116:7</a> E hoki, e toku wairua, ki tou okiokinga; kua atawhaitia hoki koe e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:8">116:8</a> Nau hoki toku wairua i whakaora kei mate, oku kanohi kei whai roimata, oku waewae kei paheke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:9">116:9</a> Tera ahau e haereere i te aroaro o Ihowa i te whenua o te ora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:10">116:10</a> ¶ I whakapono ahau, koia ahau i korero ai: he nui toku whakawhiunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:11">116:11</a> I mea ahau i toku ohoreretanga, He teka kau nga tangata katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:12">116:12</a> He aha taku e whakahoki ai ki a Ihowa mo ana atawhainga katoa i ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:13">116:13</a> Ka mau ahau ki te kapu o te whakaoranga, ka karanga ki te ingoa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:14">116:14</a> Ka whakamana e ahau aku kupu taurangi ki a Ihowa i te aroaro o tana iwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:15">116:15</a> He mea utu nui ki ta Ihowa titiro te matenga o tana hunga tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:16">116:16</a> E Ihowa, he pono ko ahau tau pononga; ko ahau tau pononga, ko te tama a tau pononga wahine; nau i wewete oku here.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:17">116:17</a> Ka tukua e ahau te patunga tapu, ara te whakawhetai: ka karanga ki te ingoa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:18">116:18</a> Ka whakamana e ahau aku kupu taurangi ki a Ihowa, ae, ki te aroaro o tana iwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:19">116:19</a> Ki nga marae o te whare o Ihowa, ki waenganui ou, e Hiruharama. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:1">117:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa, e nga tauiwi katoa: whakamoemititia ia, e nga iwi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:2">117:2</a> He nui hoki tana mahi tohu ki a tatou: e mau ana hoki te pono o Ihowa ake ake. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:1">118:1</a> ¶ Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa; he pai hoki ia, he pumau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:2">118:2</a> Kia mea a Iharaira, He pumau tonu tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:3">118:3</a> Kia mea te whare o Arona, He pumau tonu tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:4">118:4</a> Kia mea te hunga e wehi ana i a Ihowa, He pumau tonu tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:5">118:5</a> I karanga ahau ki a Ihowa i roto i te pouri: i whakahoki kupu mai a Ihowa ki ahau, i whakatu hoki i ahau ki te wahi whanui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:6">118:6</a> Kei ahau a Ihowa; e kore ahau e wehi: he aha ta te tangata e mea ai ki ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:7">118:7</a> Kei ahau a Ihowa kei roto i oku kaiawhina: no reira tera ahau e kite i taku i hiahia ai ki te hunga e kino ana ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:8">118:8</a> Ko te whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa, pai atu i te whakaaro ki te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:9">118:9</a> Ko te whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa, pai atu i te okioki ki nga rangatira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:10">118:10</a> I karapotia ahau e nga iwi katoa: ka ngaro ratou i ahau i runga i te ingoa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:11">118:11</a> I karapotia ahau e ratou: ae, i karapotia ahau e ratou: ka ngaro ratou i ahau i runga i te ingoa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:12">118:12</a> Me te mea he pi ratou e mui ana ki ahau; kua pirau ratou ano he ahi tataramoa: i ngaro hoki ratou i ahau i runga i te ingoa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:13">118:13</a> Kaha pu tau turaki i ahau, kia hinga ai ahau: na Ihowa ia ahau i awhina mai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:14">118:14</a> Ko Ihowa toku kaha, taku himene, ko ia ano toku whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:15">118:15</a> He reo hari, he reo whakaoranga, kei nga tapenakara o te hunga tika: he maia nga mahi a te ringa matau o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:16">118:16</a> Kua whakanuia te matau o Ihowa: he maia nga mahi a te ringa matau o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:17">118:17</a> E kore ahau e mate, engari tera ahau e ora, hei whakapuaki i nga mahi a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:18">118:18</a> I pakia rawatia ahau e Ihowa: otiia kihai ahau i tukua e ia kia mate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:19">118:19</a> ¶ Whakatuwheratia ki ahau nga kuwaha o te tika: ka tomo ahau ki roto, ka whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:20">118:20</a> Ko te kuwaha tenei o Ihowa: ka tomo te hunga tika ki reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:21">118:21</a> Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe, mou i whakahoki kupu mai ki ahau, kua meinga hoki ko koe hei whakaora moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:22">118:22</a> Ko te kohatu i kapea e nga kaihanga, kua meinga hei upoko mo te kokonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:23">118:23</a> Na Ihowa tenei: he mea miharo ki o tatou kanohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:24">118:24</a> Ko te ra tenei i hanga e Ihowa kia whakamanamana, kia koa tatou i reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:25">118:25</a> Whakaorangia ra aianei, e Ihowa: tena ra, e Ihowa, homai he ngahuru ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:26">118:26</a> Kia whakapaingia te tangata e haere mai ana i runga i te ingoa o Ihowa: kua whakapaingia koutou e matou i roto i te whare o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:27">118:27</a> Ko Ihowa te Atua, a nana i homai te marama ki a tatou: herea te patunga tapu ki nga aho, ki nga haona ra ano o te aata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:28">118:28</a> Ko koe toku Atua, maku koe e whakamoemiti: toku Atua, maku koe e whakanui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:29">118:29</a> Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa; he pai hoki ia: he pumau tonu tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:1">119:1</a> ¶ AREPE Ka hari te hunga he tapatahi nei i te ara, e haere nei i te ture a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:2">119:2</a> Ka hari te hunga e mau ana ki ana whakaaturanga; e whakapaua ana o ratou ngakau ki te rapu i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:3">119:3</a> Ae, e kore ratou e mahi i te kino; e haere ana ratou i ana ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:4">119:4</a> ¶ Kua oti matou te whakahau ki au akoranga, kia ata puritia e matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:5">119:5</a> Aue, me i whakatikaia toku ara ki te pupuri i au akoranga!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:6">119:6</a> Ko reira ahau ka kore ai e whakama: i ahau ka whai whakaaro nei ki au whakahau katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:7">119:7</a> ¶ Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe i runga i te ngakau tika, ina ako ahau i au whakaritenga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:8">119:8</a> Ka puritia e ahau au tikanga: kaua ahau e whakarerea rawatia. PETA</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:9">119:9</a> ¶ He aha te mea e ma ai i te taitamariki tona ara? kia rite ki tau kupu tana whakamaharatanga iho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:10">119:10</a> ¶ Kua whakapaua e ahau toku ngakau ki te rapu i a koe: kaua ahau e tukua kia kotiti ke i au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:11">119:11</a> ¶ Kua whakatakotoria e ahau tau kupu ki roto ki toku ngakau, kei hara ahau ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:12">119:12</a> ¶ E Ihowa, ka whakapaingia koe: whakaakona ahau ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:13">119:13</a> ¶ Kua whakapuakina e oku ngutu nga whakaritenga katoa a tou mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:14">119:14</a> Ko toku koa i te ara o au whakaaturanga, me te mea mo nga taonga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:15">119:15</a> Ka whakaaroaro ahau ki au ako, a ka whai mahara ki au huarahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:16">119:16</a> He oranga ngakau ki ahau au tikanga: e kore ahau e wareware ki tau kupu. KIMERE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:17">119:17</a> ¶ Kia atawhai ki tau pononga, kia ora ai ahau; kia puritia ai hoki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:18">119:18</a> ¶ Whakatirohia oku kanohi kia kite ai ahau i nga mea whakamiharo i roto i tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:19">119:19</a> ¶ He manene ahau i runga i te whenua: kaua au whakahau e huna ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:20">119:20</a> ¶ Ka ngawha toku wairua i te matenui atu ki au whakaritenga i nga wa katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:21">119:21</a> ¶ Kua riria e koe te hunga whakakake kua oti nei te kanga, e kotiti ke nei i au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:22">119:22</a> ¶ Parea atu i ahau te tawai me te whakahawea: kua mau hoki ahau ki au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:23">119:23</a> ¶ I noho ano hoki nga rangatira ki te korero kino moku: otira e whakaaro ana tau pononga ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:24">119:24</a> ¶ Ko au whakaaturanga ano toku oranga ngakau, oku hoa whakatakoto whakaaro. TARETE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:25">119:25</a> ¶ Piri tonu toku wairua ki te puehu; whakahauoratia ahau kia rite ki atu kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:26">119:26</a> ¶ I whakaaturia e ahau oku ara, a whakahoki kupu ana koe ki ahau: whakaakona ahau ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:27">119:27</a> Meinga ahau kia matau ki te ara o au ako: kia whakaaroaro ai ahau ki au mahi whakamiharo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:28">119:28</a> ¶ E maturuturu iho ana toku wairua i te pouri: kia rite ki tau kapu tau whakau ake i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:29">119:29</a> Whakamataratia atu i ahau te ara o te teka: kia atawhai mai hoki, a homai tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:30">119:30</a> ¶ Kua whiriwhiria e ahau te ara o te pono: ka waiho e ahau au whakaritenga ki toku aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:31">119:31</a> Piri tonu ahau ki au whakaaturanga: e Ihowa, kei whakama ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:32">119:32</a> Ka oma ahau i te ara o au whakahau, ina whakanuia e koe toku ngakau. HE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:33">119:33</a> ¶ E Ihowa, whakaakona ahau ki te ara o au tikanga: a ka mau i ahau taea noatia te mutunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:34">119:34</a> Homai he matauranga ki ahau, a ka mau i ahau tau ture; ka whakapaua toku ngakau ki te pupuri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:35">119:35</a> ¶ Meinga ahau kia haere i te ara o au whakahau; ko taku hoki tena e whakaahuareka nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:36">119:36</a> Whakaangahia toku ngakau ki au whakaaturanga; kaua hoki ki te apo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:37">119:37</a> ¶ Whakatahuritia ketia oku kanohi kei kite i te horihori: whakahauorangia ahau i tau ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:38">119:38</a> ¶ Whakapumautia tau kupu ki tau pononga, e wehi nei ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:39">119:39</a> ¶ Parea atu toku tawainga, e wehi nei ahau: he pai hoki au whakaritenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:40">119:40</a> ¶ Nana, kua matenui ahau ki au ako: whakahauorangia ahau i runga i tou tika. WHAU</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:41">119:41</a> ¶ Kia puta ano au mahi tohu ki ahau, e Ihowa: ara tau whakaoranga, kia rite ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:42">119:42</a> Penei ka whai kupu maku ki toku kaitawai; noku ka whakawhirinaki ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:43">119:43</a> ¶ Kaua e tangohia rawatia i toku mangai te kupu o te pono: e tumanako nei hoki ahau ki au whakaritenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:44">119:44</a> Penei ka puritia e ahau tau ture ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:45">119:45</a> ¶ A ka haereere noa ahau; kua rapua hoki e ahau au akoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:46">119:46</a> Ka korerotia ano e ahau au whakaaturanga ki te aroaro o nga kingi, e kore ano e whakama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:47">119:47</a> A ka waiho e ahau hei oranga ngakau moku au whakahau e aroha nei ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:48">119:48</a> Ka toro atu hoki oku ringa ki au whakahau e aroha nei ahau, ka whakaaroaro ano ki au tikanga. TAINE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:49">119:49</a> ¶ Maharatia te kupu ki tau pononga, no te mea kua meinga ahau e koe kia tumanako atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:50">119:50</a> ¶ Ko toku oranga ngakau tenei i ahau e tangi nei: na tau kupu nei hoki ahau i whakahauora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:51">119:51</a> ¶ Nui rawa te whakahi ki ahau o te hunga whakakake: heoi kihai ahau i peka ke i tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:52">119:52</a> ¶ I mahara ahau ki au whakaritenga, e Ihowa, o tua iho; a marie ana toku ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:53">119:53</a> ¶ Mau pu ahau i te pawera, mo te hunga kino kua whakarere nei i tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:54">119:54</a> ¶ Ko au tikanga aku e himene ai i te whare i noho manene ai ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:55">119:55</a> ¶ I mahara ahau ki tou ingoa i te po, e Ihowa: a puritia ana e ahau tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:56">119:56</a> I ahau tenei, he mau noku ki au ako. KETE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:57">119:57</a> ¶ Ko Ihowa toku wahi: kua mea nei ahau, ka pupuri ahau i au kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:58">119:58</a> ¶ I whakapaua toku ngakau ki te inoi ki a koe kia pai mai: kia rite ki tau kupu tau mahi tohu ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:59">119:59</a> ¶ I whakaaro ahau ki oku ara: a anga ana oku waewae ki au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:60">119:60</a> I hohoro ahau, a kihai i whakaroa ki te pupuri i au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:61">119:61</a> ¶ Karapotia putia ana ahau e nga here a te hunga kino: kihai ia ahau i wareware ki tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:62">119:62</a> ¶ I waenganui po ka ara ahau ki te whakawhetai ki a koe mo au whakaritenga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:63">119:63</a> ¶ He hoa ahau no te hunga katoa e wehi ana i a koe; no te hunga ano e pupuri ana i au ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:64">119:64</a> ¶ Ki tonu, e Ihowa, te whenua i tau mahi tohu: whakaakona ahau ki au tikanga. TETE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:65">119:65</a> ¶ Pai rawa tau hanga ki tau pononga, e Ihowa; rite tonu ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:66">119:66</a> Whakaakona ahau ki te ngarahu pai, ki te matauranga: kua whakapono hoki ahau ki au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:67">119:67</a> ¶ I ahau kiano i whakawhiua, i he ahau: tena ko tenei ka puritia e ahau tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:68">119:68</a> ¶ He pai koe, he pai hoki au mahi: whakaakona ahau ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:69">119:69</a> ¶ Kua titoa e te hunga whakakake he teka moku: ka whakapaua toku ngakau ki te pupuri i au ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:70">119:70</a> He ngako rawa to ratou ngakau, koia ano kei te taupa: ko ahau ia, he oranga ngakau ki ahau tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:71">119:71</a> ¶ Marie ano ahau kia pehia e te pouri; i ako ai ahau i au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:72">119:72</a> ¶ Ko te ture a tou mangai pai ke atu ki ahau i nga mano o te koura, o te hiriwa. IOTA</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:73">119:73</a> ¶ Na ou ringa ahau i hanga, i whakawhaiahua: homai he matauranga ki ahau, kia ako ai ahau ki au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:74">119:74</a> ¶ Ka hari te hunga e wehi ana i a koe ina kite i ahau: noku i tumanako ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:75">119:75</a> ¶ E matau ana ahau, e Ihowa, he tika au whakaritenga; a he pono nou i pehia ai toku ngakau e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:76">119:76</a> ¶ Tena ra, waiho tau mahi tohu hei whakamarie moku; kia rite ki tau kupu ki tau pononga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:77">119:77</a> Kia puta ki ahau au mahi aroha, kia ora ai ahau; ko tau ture hoki toku oranga ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:78">119:78</a> ¶ Kia whakama te hunga whakakake; no te mea kahore he take i he ai ta ratou hanga ki ahau; ko ahau ia ka whakaaroaro ki au akoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:79">119:79</a> Ko te hunga e wehi ana ki a koe me anga ki ahau, a ka mohio ratou ki au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:80">119:80</a> ¶ Kia tapatahi toku ngakau ki au tikanga; kei whakama ahau. KAPA</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:81">119:81</a> ¶ E matenui ana toku wairua ki tau whakaoranga: otiia ka tumanako ahau ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:82">119:82</a> Matawaia ana oku kanohi, he meatanga ki tau kupu, i ahau e mea ana, Ahea koe whakamarie ai i ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:83">119:83</a> ¶ Kua rite nei hoki ahau ki te koki i roto i te paoa: he ahakoa e kore ahau e wareware ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:84">119:84</a> ¶ E hia nga ra o tau pononga? a hea koe whakarite whakawa ai mo te hunga e tukino nei i ahau?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:85">119:85</a> ¶ Kua keri poka te hunga whakakake moku; he mea kahore e rite ki tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:86">119:86</a> Pono tonu au whakahau katoa: e tukino takekore ana ratou i ahau; awhinatia mai ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:87">119:87</a> Wahi iti kua moti ahau i a ratou i runga i te whenua: otira kihai i mahue i ahau au akoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:88">119:88</a> ¶ Kia rite ki tou aroha tau whakahauora i ahau: a ka puritia e ahau nga whakaaturanga a tou mangai. RAMERE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:89">119:89</a> ¶ Pumau tonu tau kupu, e Ihowa, ake ake i runga i te rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:90">119:90</a> Kei nga whakatupuranga katoa tou pono: whakaungia ana e koe te whenua, a e tu nei ano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:91">119:91</a> E tu nei ano inaianei, pera tonu me tau i whakarite ai, he pononga hoki nga mea katoa nau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:92">119:92</a> ¶ Me kaua tau ture hei oranga mo toku ngakau, kua ngaro ahau i reira i toku auetanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:93">119:93</a> ¶ E kore rawa ahau e wareware ki au ako, he mea whakahauora hoki nau ena i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:94">119:94</a> ¶ Nau ahau, mau ahau e whakaora: kua rapua hoki e ahau au ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:95">119:95</a> ¶ Kua tatari te hunga kino ki ahau kia whakamatea: ka whakaaro ia ahau ki au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:96">119:96</a> ¶ Kua kitea e ahau te mutunga o nga mea tino tika katoa: he whanui rawa ia tau whakahau. MEME</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:97">119:97</a> ¶ Ano toku aroha ki tau ture! Ko taku tena e whakaaroaro ai i te roa o te ra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:98">119:98</a> ¶ Nau i hira ake ai oku whakaaro i o oku hoariri, na au whakahau, e piri tonu nei ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:99">119:99</a> Nui atu oku mahara i o oku kaiwhakaako katoa: noku i whakaaroaro tonu ki au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:100">119:100</a> Tera atu toku mohio i to nga kaumatua, no te mea i pupuri ahau i au ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:101">119:101</a> ¶ Kua kaiponuhia mai e ahau oku waewae i nga ara kino katoa, kia pupuri ai ahau i tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:102">119:102</a> ¶ Kihai ahau i titaha i au whakaritenga; nau hoki ahau i ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:103">119:103</a> ¶ Ano te reka o au kupu ki toku ngao; ae ra, reka atu i te honi ki toku mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:104">119:104</a> Na au ako ahau i whai mohio ai: na reira ahau i kino ai ki nga ara teka katoa. NUNU</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:105">119:105</a> ¶ He rama tau kupu ki oku waewae, he marama ki toku ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:106">119:106</a> ¶ Kua oati ahau, a ka whakamana ano e ahau: kia puritia e ahau au whakaritenga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:107">119:107</a> ¶ He nui te mamae o toku ngakau: whakahauorangia ahau, e Ihowa, kia rite ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:108">119:108</a> ¶ Manakohia, e Ihowa, nga ohaohatanga a toku mangai, whakaakona hoki ahau ki au whakaritenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:109">119:109</a> ¶ Kei toku ringa tonu toku wairua, heoi kahore ahau e wareware ki tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:110">119:110</a> Kua whakatakotoria e te hunga kino he mahanga moku: heoi kahore ahau i peka ke i au ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:111">119:111</a> ¶ Ka waiho e ahau au whakaaturanga hei kainga tupu moku ake ake: ko toku koanga ngakau hoki ena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:112">119:112</a> Kua whakaanga e ahau toku ngakau ki te mahi tonu i au tikanga: a te mutunga ra ano. HAMEKE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:113">119:113</a> ¶ E kino ana ahau ki te hunga whakaaro ruarua; ko tau ture ia taku e aroha ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:114">119:114</a> ¶ Ko toku piringa koe, ko toku whakangungu rakau: e tumanako ana ahau ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:115">119:115</a> ¶ Mawehe atu i ahau, e te hunga kino; ka whakaritea hoki e ahau nga whakahau a toku Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:116">119:116</a> ¶ Kia rite ki tau kupu tau tautoko ake i ahau, kia ora ai ahau: kaua hoki ahau e tukua kia whakama ki taku e tumanako atu nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:117">119:117</a> Tautokona ake ahau, kia ora ai ahau, a ka whai whakaaro tonu ahau ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:118">119:118</a> ¶ Kua whakahaweatia e koe te hunga katoa e kotiti ke ana i au tikanga; he horihori hoki to ratou tinihanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:119">119:119</a> Ka whakakahoretia e koe te hunga kino katoa o te whenua, ano he para mata: koia ahau i aroha ai ki au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:120">119:120</a> Wiri ana oku kikokiko i te wehi ki a koe; e mataku ana hoki ahau ki au whakaritenga. AINE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:121">119:121</a> ¶ He whakawa tika, he tika taku mahi: kaua ahau e tukua ki oku kaitukino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:122">119:122</a> Ko koe hei tuara mo tau pononga mo te pai: kei tukinotia ahau e te hunga whakakake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:123">119:123</a> ¶ Matawaia ana oku kanohi i te meatanga ki tau whakaora, ki te kupu hoki o tau tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:124">119:124</a> ¶ Kia rite ki tou aroha tau mahi ki tau pononga: whakaakona hoki ahau ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:125">119:125</a> He pononga ahau nau; homai he mahara ki ahau, kia matau ai ki au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:126">119:126</a> ¶ Kua rite te wa hei mahinga ma Ihowa; kua whakakahoretia hoki e ratou tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:127">119:127</a> ¶ Na reira i arohaina rawatia ai e ahau au whakahau i te koura, ae, i te tino koura.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:128">119:128</a> Na reira tika tonu ki ahau au ako katoa mo nga mea katoa: kino iho ano ahau ki nga ara teka katoa. PE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:129">119:129</a> ¶ He mea whakamiharo au whakaaturanga: i mau ai toku wairua ki reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:130">119:130</a> ¶ Ko te whakapuakanga o au kupu he homai marama; na reira i homai he mahara ki nga kuware.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:131">119:131</a> ¶ I hamama toku mangai, i kihakiha: he matenui noku ki au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:132">119:132</a> ¶ Tahuri mai ki ahau, tohungia hoki ahau: kia rite ki tau hanga ki te hunga e aroha ana ki tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:133">119:133</a> ¶ Whakatikaia oku hikoinga ki runga i tau kupu: kaua hoki tetahi he e tukua hei rangatira moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:134">119:134</a> ¶ Whakaorangia ahau i te tukino a te tangata: a ka puritia e ahau au ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:135">119:135</a> ¶ Kia marama mai tou mata ki tau pononga: whakaakona hoki ahau ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:136">119:136</a> ¶ Heke noa nga awa wai o oku kanohi; mo ratou kahore i pupuri i tau ture. TARI</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:137">119:137</a> ¶ He tika koe, e Ihowa, he tika ano au whakaritenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:138">119:138</a> He tika, he pono rawa au whakaaturanga i whakahaua mai e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:139">119:139</a> ¶ Ka ngaro ahau i toku ngakau whakapuke, mo au kupu ka wareware nei i oku hoariri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:140">119:140</a> ¶ Hore rawa he para o tau kupu: koia i arohaina ai e tau pononga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:141">119:141</a> ¶ He iti ahau, e whakahaweatia ana: heoi kahore ahau e wareware ki au ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:142">119:142</a> ¶ He tika pumau tonu tou tika; he pono hoki tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:143">119:143</a> ¶ Kua pa mai ki ahau te pouri me te mamae: ko au whakahau ia toku oranga ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:144">119:144</a> Pumau tonu te tika o au whakaaturanga: homai he mahara ki ahau, a ka ora ahau. KOPO</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:145">119:145</a> ¶ I whakapaua toku ngakau ki te karanga; whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau, e Ihowa; ka mau i ahau au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:146">119:146</a> I karanga ahau ki a koe: whakaorangia ahau, a ka puritia e ahau au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:147">119:147</a> ¶ Kiano te ata i puao noa, kua karanga ahau: i tumanako ahau ki au kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:148">119:148</a> I hohoro oku kanohi i nga mataaratanga ki te whakaaroaro ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:149">119:149</a> ¶ Whakarongo ki toku reo, kia rite ki tou aroha: kia rite, e Ihowa, ki tau i whakarite ai tau whakahauora i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:150">119:150</a> ¶ E whakatata mai ana te hunga e whai ana i te whanoke: kei tawhiti atu ratou i tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:151">119:151</a> E tata ana mai koe, e Ihowa: he pono katoa au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:152">119:152</a> ¶ Nonamata ahau i matau ai ki au whakaaturanga, he mea whakapumau nau no tua whakarere. REHE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:153">119:153</a> ¶ Whakaaro mai ki toku mate, a whakaorangia ahau: kahore hoki ahau e wareware ki tau ture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:154">119:154</a> Tohea taku tohe, whakaorangia hoki ahau: kia rite ki tau kupu tau whakahauoranga i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:155">119:155</a> ¶ Kei tawhiti atu i te hunga kino te whakaoranga: kahore hoki ratou e rapu ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:156">119:156</a> ¶ E Ihowa, he nui au mahi tohu: kia rite ki au whakaritenga tau whakahauora i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:157">119:157</a> ¶ He tokomaha oku kaitukino, oku hoariri: heoi kahore ahau i peka ke i au whakaaturanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:158">119:158</a> ¶ I kite ahau i nga kaimahi i te kino, a pouri iho: no ratou kahore e pupuri i tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:159">119:159</a> ¶ Tirohia mai toku aroha ki au ako: kia rite ki tou aroha, e Ihowa, tau whakahauora i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:160">119:160</a> ¶ Ko te huinga katoatanga o tau kupu he pono; pumau katoa anao au whakaritenga tika ake ake. HINE</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:161">119:161</a> ¶ Hore he rawa i tukinotia ai ahau e nga rangatira: otiia e wehi ana toku ngakau i tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:162">119:162</a> ¶ E hari ana ahau ki tau kupu: ano he tangata kua whiwhi ki te taonga nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:163">119:163</a> ¶ E kino ana ahau, e whakarihariha ana ki te korero teka: ko tau ture ia taku i aroha ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:164">119:164</a> ¶ Takiwhitu aku whakamoemiti ki a koe i te ra tahi mo au whakaritenga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:165">119:165</a> ¶ He rangimarie nui to te hunga e aroha ana ki tau ture: e kore hoki o ratou waewae e tutuki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:166">119:166</a> ¶ A kua tumanako ahau ki tau whakaora, e Ihowa, kua mahi ahau i au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:167">119:167</a> ¶ Kua puritia e toku wairua au whakaaturanga, ae, e arohaina nuitia ana e ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:168">119:168</a> Kua puritia e ahau au ako me au whakaaturanga: kei tou aroaro hoki oku ara katoa. TAU</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:169">119:169</a> ¶ Tukua atu taku tangi kia tata atu ki tou aroaro, e Ihowa: homai he mahara ki ahau, kia rite ki tau kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:170">119:170</a> Kia tae atu taku inoi ki tou aroaro: kia rite ki tau kupu whakaora i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:171">119:171</a> ¶ Kia whakapuaki oku ngutu i te whakamoemiti: e whakaako ana hoki koe i ahau ki au tikanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:172">119:172</a> ¶ Ma toku arero e korero tau kupu: he tika hoki au whakahau katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:173">119:173</a> ¶ Kia rite tou ringa ki te awhina i ahau; kua whiriwhiria hoki e ahau ko au ako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:174">119:174</a> Kua matenui ahau ki tau whakaora, e Ihowa: ko tau ture hoki toku oranga ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:175">119:175</a> ¶ Kia ora toku wairua, a ka whakamoemiti ia ki a koe: kia awhinatia hoki ahau e au whakaritenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:176">119:176</a> ¶ Kua kotiti ke ahau me he hipi ngaro: rapua tau pononga, kahore hoki ahau e wareware ki au whakahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:1">120:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. I tangi, ahau ki a Ihowa i toku matenga; a i whakahoki kupu mai ia ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:2">120:2</a> E Ihowa, whakaorangia toku wairua i te ngutu teka, i te arero hianga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:3">120:3</a> Ko te aha e hoatu ki a koe? ko te aha hoki e tapiritia atu mau, e te arero hianga?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:4">120:4</a> Ko nga pere koi a te hunga nunui, me nga waro hunipa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:5">120:5</a> ¶ Aue, toku mate, to te manene i Meheke, toku hoki e noho nei i nga teneti o Kerara!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:6">120:6</a> Kua roa te nohoanga tahitanga o toku wairua ki te tangata e kino ana ki te ata noho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:7">120:7</a> Mo te ata noho ahau, engari ka korero ahau, ka anga ratou ka whawhai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:1">121:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Ka anga atu oku kanohi ki nga maunga; no reira nei te awhina moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:2">121:2</a> No Ihowa te awhina moku, no te kaihanga o te rangi, o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:3">121:3</a> E kore ia e tuku i tou waewae kia nekehia; e kore tou kaitiaki e moe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:4">121:4</a> Ina, e kore te kaitiaki o Iharaira e parangia, e moe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:5">121:5</a> Ko Ihowa tou kaitiaki, ko Ihowa tou whakamarumaru i tou matau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:6">121:6</a> E kore koe e pakia e te ra i te awatea, e te marama ranei i te po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:7">121:7</a> Ma Ihowa koe e tiaki i roto i nga kino katoa; mana e tiaki tou wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:8">121:8</a> Ma Ihowa e tiaki tou haerenga atu, me tou haerenga mai aianei a ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:1">122:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Rawiri. I koa ahau i ta ratou meatanga mai ki ahau; Tatou ka haere ki te whare o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:2">122:2</a> E tu ana o matou waewae ki ou tatau, e Hiruharama:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:3">122:3</a> Ko te hanganga o Hiruharama, rite tonu ki to te pa kua tuhonohonoa ki a ia ano..</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:4">122:4</a> Haereere ana ki reira nga iwi, nga iwi o Ihowa, ki to Iharaira whakaaturanga, ki te whakawhetai ki te ingoa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:5">122:5</a> Kua whakaturia hoki ki reira nga torona whakawa, nga torona o te whare o Rawiri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:6">122:6</a> ¶ Inoia he ata noho mo Hiruharama: ka whiwhi ki te pai te hunga e aroha ana ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:7">122:7</a> Kia mau te rongo ki ou taiepa, me te pai ki ou whare kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:8">122:8</a> He mea mo oku teina, mo oku hoa, taku e mea nei, Kia mau te rongo ki roto ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:9">122:9</a> He whakaaro ki te whare o Ihowa, o to tatou Atua, ka rapu ahau i te pai mou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:1">123:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Ka anga atu oku kanohi ki a koe, e koe e noho mai nei i nga rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:2">123:2</a> Ina, pera tonu nga kanohi o nga pononga e titiro nei ki te ringa o to ratou rangatira, nga kanohi hoki o te kotiro ki te ringa o tona rangatira wahine; me o matou kanohi e titiro nei ki a Ihowa, ki to matou Atua, kia tohu ra ano ia i a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:3">123:3</a> Tohungia matou, e Ihowa, tohungia matou: kua tino kapi hoki matou i te whakahawea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:4">123:4</a> Kapi tonu to matou wairua i te whakahi a te hunga e noho noa ana, i te whakahawea a te hunga whakakake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:1">124:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Rawiri. Me kaua a Ihowa i a tatou, he ki tenei ma Iharaira:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:2">124:2</a> Me kaua a Ihowa i a tatou, i te whakatikanga mai o te tangata ki a tatou;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:3">124:3</a> Penei kua horomia oratia tatou e ratou, i te muranga o to ratou riri ki a tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:4">124:4</a> Kua ngaro tatou i nga wai, kua taupokina o tatou wairua e te ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:5">124:5</a> Penei kua taupokina o tatou wairua e nga wai whakakake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:6">124:6</a> ¶ Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, kihai nei i tuku i a tatou hei ngaunga ma o ratou niho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:7">124:7</a> Kua mawhiti o tatou wairua, me he manu i roto i te mahanga a nga kaihopu; kua motu te mahanga, a mawhiti ana tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:8">124:8</a> Kei te ingoa o Ihowa he awhina mo tatou, kei te kaihanga i te rangi, i te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:1">125:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Ko te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a Ihowa ka rite ki Maunga Hiona, e kore nei e taea te whakangaueue, pumau tonu ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:2">125:2</a> Me nga maunga e taiawhio nei i Hiruharama, te karapoti a Ihowa i tona iwi, aianei a ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:3">125:3</a> E kore hoki te tokotoko a te whakaarokore e waiho tonu i runga i te wahi o te hunga tika: kei totoro te ringa o te hunga tika ki te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:4">125:4</a> ¶ Kia pai tau mahi, e Ihowa, ki te hunga pai, ki te hunga he tika nei o ratou ngakau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:5">125:5</a> Ko te hunga ia e peka ke ana ki o ratou ara kopikopiko, ma Ihowa ratou e arahi tahi atu me nga kaimahi i te kino. Kia mau te rongo ki a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:1">126:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. I ta Ihowa whakahokinga mai i nga pononga o Hiona i rite matou ki te hunga e moehewa ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:2">126:2</a> Katahi to matou mangai ka ki i te kata, to matou arero hoki i te waiata: katahi ka korerotia i roto i nga tauiwi, He nui nga mahi a Ihowa ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:3">126:3</a> He mea nunui a Ihowa i mea ai mo tatou, a e koa ana tatou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:4">126:4</a> ¶ E Ihowa, whakahokia matou i te whakarau: kia pera me nga awa o te tonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:5">126:5</a> Ko te hunga e rui ana i runga i te roimata, ka kokoti i runga i te hari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:6">126:6</a> Ahakoa haere tangi atu ia me te kawe i ana purapura hei whakatokanga; tera ia e haere hari mai ano me te mau mai i ana paihere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:1">127:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Horomona. Ki te kore e hanga e Ihowa te whare, he maumau mahi ta nga kaihanga; ki te kore e tiakina e Ihowa te pa, maumau mataara noa te kaitiaki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:2">127:2</a> He maumau to koutou ara wawe, to koutou noho roa i te po, ta koutou kai i te taro o te mauiui: ko tana moe tena ka homai nei ki tana e aroha ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:3">127:3</a> Na he taonga pumau na Ihowa nga tamariki, ko nga hua ano o te kopu tana utu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:4">127:4</a> E rite ana ki nga pere i te ringaringa o te tangata kaha te whanau o te taitamarikitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:5">127:5</a> Ka hari te tangata kua ki nei tana papa pere i a ratou: e kore ratou e whakama, ina korero ki o ratou hoariri i te kuwaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:1">128:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Ka hari nga tangata katoa e wehi ana i a Ihowa: e haere ana i ana ara.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:2">128:2</a> E kai hoki koe i te mahinga a ou ringa: e hari koe, a ka tau te pai ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:3">128:3</a> E rite tau wahine ki te waina hua, i roto rawa i tou whare: au tamariki ki nga mahuri oriwa, i nga taha o tau tepu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:4">128:4</a> Na he pera te manaaki mo te tangata e wehi ana i a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:5">128:5</a> Ka Manaakitia koe e Ihowa i Hiona; a e kite koe i te pai o Hiruharama i nga ra katoa e ora ai koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:6">128:6</a> Ae, e kite koe i nga tamariki a au tamariki. Kia mau te rongo ki a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:1">129:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. He ki tenei ma Iharaira, Ka maha a ratou tukinotanga i ahau o toku tamarikitanga ake;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:2">129:2</a> Ka maha a ratou tukinotanga i ahau o toku tamarikitanga ake; heoi kihai ahau i taea e ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:3">129:3</a> I parautia toku tuara e nga kaiparau; he roa a ratou parautanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:4">129:4</a> He tika ta Ihowa: motu pu i a ia nga aho a te hunga kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:5">129:5</a> ¶ Kia whakama, kia whakahokia ki muri, te hunga katoa e kino nei ki Hiona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:6">129:6</a> Kia rite ratou ki te tarutaru i nga tuanui, e memenge nei i te mea kiano i tupu ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:7">129:7</a> E kore nei e ki te ringa o te kaikoti, te uma hoki o te kaipaihere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:8">129:8</a> E kore ano te hunga e haere ana i te taha e mea, Kia tau ki a koutou te manaaki a Ihowa: ko ta matou manaaki tenei ki a koutou i runga i te ingoa o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:1">130:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. I karanga ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa, i roto i nga hohonu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:2">130:2</a> E te Ariki, whakarongo mai ki toku reo: kia anga mai ou taringa ki toku reo inoi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:3">130:3</a> Me i maharatia e koe nga kino, e Ihowa, ko wai, e te Ariki, e tu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:4">130:4</a> Otira he muru hara tau, e wehingia ai koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:5">130:5</a> ¶ E tatari ana ahau ki a Ihowa; e tatari ana toku wairua: e tumanako ana hoki ahau ki tana kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:6">130:6</a> Ko te taringa o toku wairua i te Ariki nui atu i to te hunga e whanga ana ki te ata; ae, i to te hunga e whanga ana ki te ata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:7">130:7</a> E Iharaira, kia tumanako ki a Ihowa, kei a Ihowa hoki te mahi tohu, a kei a ia te hokonga nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:8">130:8</a> A mana a Iharaira e hoko i roto i ona he katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:1">131:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Rawiri. E Ihowa, ehara toku i te ngakau whakapehapeha: ehara ano oku i te kanohi whakakake: kahore hoki ahau e rahurahu ki nga mea nunui, e kore nei e taea e ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:2">131:2</a> He pono kua meinga e ahau toku wairua kia tau, a kia mahaki, pera i to te tamaiti kua wehea i te u o tona whaea: he rite toku wairua ki te tamaiti katahi nei ka wehe i te u.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:3">131:3</a> E Iharaira, kia tumanako ki a Ihowa: aianei a ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:1">132:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. E Ihowa, maharatia a Rawiri, me ona mamaetanga ngakau katoa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:2">132:2</a> Tana oati ki a Ihowa, tana kupu taurangi ki te Mea Nui o Hakopa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:3">132:3</a> E kore rawa ahau e tae ki toku whare e noho ai ahau, e eke ranei ki runga ki toku moenga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:4">132:4</a> E kore ahau e tuku i oku kanohi kia moe, i oku kamo kia nenewha;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:5">132:5</a> Kia kitea ra ano e ahau he wahi mo Ihowa, he nohoanga mo te Mea Nui o Hakopa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:6">132:6</a> Na i rangona e matou ki Eparata, i kitea ki nga mara o te ngahere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:7">132:7</a> Ka haere matou ki roto ki ona tapenakara; ka koropiko ki tona turanga waewae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:8">132:8</a> E ara, e Ihowa, ki tou okiokinga, a koe, me te aaka o tou kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:9">132:9</a> Kia whakakakahuria au tohunga ki te tika; kia hamama tau hunga tapu i te hari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:10">132:10</a> Whakaaro ki a Rawiri, ki tau pononga: kaua e whakapeaua atu te mata o tau i whakawahi ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:11">132:11</a> ¶ Kua oati pono a Ihowa ki a Rawiri, e kore ia e tahuri ke i tena; Ka whakanohoia e ahau tetahi hua o tou kopu ki tou torona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:12">132:12</a> Ki te puritia e au tama taku kawenata, me taku whakaaturanga e ako ai ahau ki a ratou, ka noho ano a ratou tama ki tou torona ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:13">132:13</a> Kua whiriwhiria hoki e Ihowa a Hiona; kua hiahiatia e ia hei nohoanga mona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:14">132:14</a> Ko toku okiokinga tenei ake ake; ko konei ahau noho ai, kua hiahiatia hoki e ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:15">132:15</a> Ka manaakitia rawatia e ahau tana kai; ka whakamakonatia e ahau ona rawakore ki te taro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:16">132:16</a> Ka whakakakahuria hoki e ahau ona tohunga ki te whakaoranga; a ka hamama tona hunga tapu i te hari.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:17">132:17</a> Ka meinga e ahau kia pihi ki reira te haona o Rawiri: kua whakapaia e ahau he rama mo taku i whakawahi ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:18">132:18</a> Ka whakakakahuria e ahau ona hoariri ki te whakama; a ka matomato tona karauna i runga i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:1">133:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Rawiri. Na, ano te pai, ano te ahuareka o te nohoanga o nga teina, o nga tuakana i runga i te whakaaro kotahi!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:2">133:2</a> Tona rite kei te hinu utu nui i runga i te upoko, i heke iho nei ki te pahau, ae ki te pahau o Arona; i heke iho nei ki te remu o ona kakahu:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:3">133:3</a> Kei te tomairangi ano o Heremona, kei tera i heke iho ki nga maunga o Hiona: i whakahaua iho hoki e Ihowa te manaaki mo reira, te ora mo ake tonu atu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:1">134:1</a> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na, whakapaingia a Ihowa, e nga pononga katoa a Ihowa, e tu nei i te whare o Ihowa i te po.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:2">134:2</a> Totoro ake o koutou ringa ki te wahi tapu, whakapaingia hoki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:3">134:3</a> Ma Ihowa koe e manaaki i roto i Hiona, mana, ma te kaihanga o te rangi, o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:1">135:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Whakamoemititia te ingoa o Ihowa; whakamoemititia ia, e nga pononga a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:2">135:2</a> E koutou e tu nei i roto i te whare o Ihowa, i nga marae o te whare o to tatou Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:3">135:3</a> Whakamoemititia a Ihowa; he pai hoki a Ihowa; himene atu ki tona ingoa; he mea ahuareka hoki tena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:4">135:4</a> Kua whiriwhiria hoki e Ihowa a Hakopa mana, a Iharaira hei tino taonga mona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:5">135:5</a> ¶ E matau ana hoki ahau he nui a Ihowa: kei runga atu hoki to tatou Ariki i nga atua katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:6">135:6</a> Ko nga mea katoa i pai ai a Ihowa, kua oti i a ia, i te rangi, i te whenua, i nga moana, i nga wahi hohonu katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:7">135:7</a> Nana i pupu ake ai nga kohu i nga pito o te whenua: i hanga e ia nga uira mo te ua; e whakaputaina mai ana e ia te hau i roto i ona whare taonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:8">135:8</a> Nana nei i patu nga matamua o Ihipa, a te tangata, a te kararehe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:9">135:9</a> I tonoa e ia he tohu, he merekara ki waenganui ou, e Ihipa: ki runga ki a Parao ratou ko ana pononga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:10">135:10</a> Nana i patu nga iwi maha, i whakamate nga kingi rarahi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:11">135:11</a> A Hihona kingi o nga Amori, a Oka kingi o Pahana, me nga rangatiratanga katoa o Kanaana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:12">135:12</a> A homai ana e ia to ratou whenua hei kainga pumau, hei kainga pumau mo Iharaira, mo tana iwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:13">135:13</a> E Ihowa, pumau tonu tou ingoa, me tou maharatanga, e Ihowa, ki nga whakatupuranga katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:14">135:14</a> Ka whakawa hoki a Ihowa mo tana iwi; a ka puta ke tona whakaaro ki ana pononga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:15">135:15</a> ¶ He hiriwa, he koura nga whakapakoko a nga tauiwi, he mahi na te ringa tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:16">135:16</a> He mangai o ratou, a kahore e korero: he kanohi o ratou, a kahore e kite:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:17">135:17</a> He taringa o ratou, a kahore e rongo: kahore ano he manawa i o ratou mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:18">135:18</a> Ka rite ki a ratou te hunga nana ratou i hanga; ae, me nga tangata katoa e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:19">135:19</a> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e te whare o Iharaira; whakapaingia a Ihowa, e te whare o Arona;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:20">135:20</a> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e te whare o Riwai; whakapaingia a Ihowa, e te hunga katoa e wehi ana i a Ihowa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:21">135:21</a> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa i roto i Hiona, e noho nei i Hiruharama. Whakapaingia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:1">136:1</a> ¶ Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, he pai hoki ia: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:2">136:2</a> Whakawhetai ki te Atua o nga atua: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:3">136:3</a> Whakawhetai ki te Ariki o nga ariki: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:4">136:4</a> E mahi nei tona kotahi i nga merekara nunui: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:5">136:5</a> I tohunga rawa nei ki te hanga i nga rangi: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:6">136:6</a> I whakatakoto nei i te whenua ki runga ki nga wai: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:7">136:7</a> Ki te kaihanga i nga whakamarama nunui: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:8">136:8</a> I te ra hei tohutohu i te awatea: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:9">136:9</a> I te marama me nga whetu hei tohutohu i te po: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:10">136:10</a> ¶ Ki te kaipatu i Ihipa, ara i a ratou matamua: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:11">136:11</a> A arahina mai ana a Iharaira i waenganui i a ratou: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:12">136:12</a> Na te ringa kaha me te takakau maro: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:13">136:13</a> I tapahi nei i te Moana Whero a motu rawa: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:14">136:14</a> A meinga ana a Iharaira kia haere ra waenganui: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:15">136:15</a> A hurihia ana a Parao me ana mano ki te Moana Whero: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:16">136:16</a> I arahi nei i tana iwi ra te koraha: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:17">136:17</a> I patu nei i nga kingi nunui: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:18">136:18</a> I whakamate nei i nga kingi rongo nui: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:19">136:19</a> I a Hihona kingi o nga Amori: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:20">136:20</a> I a Oka kingi o Pahana: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:21">136:21</a> A homai ana to ratou whenua hei kainga pumau: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:22">136:22</a> Hei kainga pumau mo Iharaira, mo tana pononga: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:23">136:23</a> ¶ I mahara nei ki a tatou i to tatou itinga; he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:24">136:24</a> A whakaorangia ana tatou i o tatou hoariri: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:25">136:25</a> Ko ia te kaihomai i te kai ma nga kikokiko katoa: he mau tonu hoki tana inahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:26">136:26</a> Whakawhetai ki te Atua o te rangi: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:1">137:1</a> ¶ I te taha o nga wai o Papurona, noho ana tatou i reira, ae, tangi ana tatou, ia tatou i mahara ai ki Hiona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:2">137:2</a> Whakairia ake e tatou a tatou hapa ki runga ki nga wirou i waenganui o reira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:3">137:3</a> No te mea i tono i reira te hunga nana tatou i herehere ki etahi waiata i a tatou, me te hunga nana tatou i tukino i tono mai he hari i a tatou, i mea mai, Waiatatia mai ki a matou tetahi o nga waiate o Hiona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:4">137:4</a> Me pehea matou ka waiata ai i te waiata a Ihowa i te whenua tauhou?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:5">137:5</a> Ki te wareware ahau ki a koe, e Hiruharama, kia wareware toku ringa matau ki tana mahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:6">137:6</a> Ki te kore ahau e mahara ki a koe, kia piri toku arero ki toku ngao; ki te kore ahau e whakanui i Hiruharama ki runga ake i taku mea i tino hari ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:7">137:7</a> ¶ E Ihowa, maharatia nga tama a Eroma i te ra o Hiruharama; ta ratou meatanga, Whakahoroa, whakahoroa, a taea rawatia ano tona turanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:8">137:8</a> E te tamahine o Papurona, meake nei whakangaromia, ka hari te tangata e utua ai koe mo tau i mea ai ki a matou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:9">137:9</a> Ka hari te tangata e hopu ana, e ta ana i au mea nohinohi ki runga ki te kohatu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:1">138:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. Ka whakapaua toku ngakau ki te whakawhetai ki a koe: ka himene atu ahau ki a koe i te aroaro o nga atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:2">138:2</a> Ka koropiko atu ahau ki te ritenga o tou temepara tapu, a ka whakamoemiti ki tou ingoa, mo tou aroha me tou pono: kua whakanuia hoki e koe tau kupu ki runga ake i tou ingoa katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:3">138:3</a> I whakahoki kupu mai koe ki ahau i te ra i karanga ai ahau: a whakahirihiritia ana e koe toku wairua ki te kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:4">138:4</a> Ka whakamoemiti nga kingi katoa o te whenua ki a koe, e Ihowa, kua rongo hoki ratou ki nga kupu a tou mangai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:5">138:5</a> Ae, e waiata ratou mo nga ara o Ihowa: he nui hoki te kororia o Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:6">138:6</a> ¶ Ahakoa hoki kei runga rawa a Ihowa, e titiro iho ana ano ia ki te hunga papaku: tena ko te tangata whakakake, i tawhiti ano kua matauria e ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:7">138:7</a> Ahakoa haere ahau i waenganui o te he, mau ahau e whakahauora: ka totoro tou ringa ki te riri o oku hoa whawhai, ma tou ringa matau ano ahau e whakaora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:8">138:8</a> Ma Ihowa e whakaoti aku mea: e Ihowa, e mau ana tau mahi tohu ake ake; kaua e whakarerea nga mahi a ou ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:1">139:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He Himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, kua tirotirohia ahau e koe, kua mohiotia ano e koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:2">139:2</a> E matau ana koe ki toku nohoanga iho, ki toku whakatikanga ake; e mohio ana koe ki oku whakaaro i tawhiti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:3">139:3</a> E kitea putia ana e koe toku ara me toku takotoranga iho; e matatau ana hoki koe ki oku ara katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:4">139:4</a> Kahore rawa hoki he kupu i toku arero, i toe i a koe te mohio, e Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:5">139:5</a> Kua hanga a muri, a mua, oku e koe: kua pa ano tou ringa ki ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:6">139:6</a> He mea whakamiharo rawa, kei tawhiti atu hoki i ahau, tenei matauranga: kei runga noa atu, e kore e taea e ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:7">139:7</a> ¶ Me haere ahau ki hea i tou wairua? Me oma ranei ahau ki hea i tou aroaro?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:8">139:8</a> Ki te kake ahau ki te rangi, kei reira koe: ki te wharikitia e ahau toku moenga i roto i te reinga, kei reira ano koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:9">139:9</a> Ki te tango ahau ki nga pakau o te ata, a ka noho ki nga topito o te moana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:10">139:10</a> Kei reira ano tou ringa hei arahi i ahau, tou matau hei pupuru i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:11">139:11</a> Ki te mea ahau, He pono, tera ahau e hipokina e te pouri, a ko te marama i tetahi taha oku, i tetahi taha, ka meinga he po;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:12">139:12</a> Ahakoa te pouri kahore e huna mai i a koe, engari ka marama te po ano ko te ao: ki a koe rite tahi te pouri me te marama.</p>
