 <p><a name="an_139:13">139:13</a> I a koe hoki oku whatumanawa: nau hoki ahau i hipoki i roto i te kopu o toku whaea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:14">139:14</a> Ka whakawhetai ahau ki a koe; he mea whakawehi, he mea whakamiharo toku hanganga; he mahi whakamiharo au mahi, mohio rawa ano toku wairua ki tena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:15">139:15</a> Kihai i huna oku wahi i a koe, i ahau e hanga ngarotia ana, e ata whakairohia ana i nga wahi hohonu rawa o te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:16">139:16</a> I kite ou kanohi i ahau, kahore ano kia ahua noa: i tuhituhia katoatia ano hoki oku wahi ki tau pukapuka, i nga rangi i whakaahua ai, i te mea kahore ano tetahi i oti noa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:17">139:17</a> ¶ Kia pehea mai hoki te matenui o ou whakaaro ki ahau, e te Atua; koia ano te ranea, ina huihuia!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:18">139:18</a> Ki te taua e ahau, maha atu i te onepu: ka oho ake ahau, kei a koe tonu ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:19">139:19</a> He pono ka patua e koe, e te Atua, te tangata kino: mawehe koia atu i ahau, e nga tangata toto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:20">139:20</a> He kino hoki a ratou kupu mou: e whakahua noa ana ou hoariri i tou ingoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:21">139:21</a> Kahore ianei ahau, e Ihowa, e kino ki te hunga e kino ana ki a koe? e whakarihariha hoki ki te hunga e whakatika ana ki a koe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:22">139:22</a> He tino kino taku kino ki a ratou: waiho iho ratou e ahau hei hoariri moku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:23">139:23</a> Tirohia iho ahau, e te Atua, kia matau hoki koe ki toku ngakau: whakamatautauria ahau, kia matau hoki koe ki oku whakaaro:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:24">139:24</a> Kia kite mehemea kei ahau tetahi ara o te kino, ka arahi ai i ahau i te ara pumau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:1">140:1</a> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na Rawiri. Whakaorangia ahau, e Ihowa, i te tangata kino: araia atu i ahau te tangata tutu:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:2">140:2</a> E whakaaro kino nei i o ratou ngakau: e whakamine nei i a ratou i nga wa katoa ki te whawhai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:3">140:3</a> Kua whakakoia to ratou arero, ano he nakahi: kei raro i o ratou ngutu te wai whakamate o te neke. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:4">140:4</a> Tiakina ahau, e Ihowa, i nga ringa o te hunga kino: araia atu i ahau te tangata tutu, kua mea nei kia tutea oku hikoinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:5">140:5</a> Kua huna e te hunga whakakake te mahanga moku, me nga aho; kua horahia e ratou he kupenga ki te taha o te ara: kua whakapikoa e ratou he rore moku. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:6">140:6</a> I mea ahau ki a Ihowa, Ko koe toku Atua: whakarongo, e Ihowa, ki toku reo inoi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:7">140:7</a> E Ihowa, e te Ariki, e te kaha o toku whakaoranga, nau i hipoki toku upoko i te ra o te tatauranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:8">140:8</a> ¶ Aua e whakaaetia, e Ihowa, nga hiahia o te tangata kino: kei taea tona whakaaro koroke; kei whakakake ratou. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:9">140:9</a> Tena ko te upoko o te hunga e whakapae nei i ahau, kia hipokina ratou e te kino o o ratou ngutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:10">140:10</a> Kia taka he waro mura ki runga ki a ratou: kia panga ratou ki te ahi, ki roto ki nga poka hohonu, kei whakatika ake ano ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:11">140:11</a> E kore te tangata korero kino e whakapumautia ki runga ki te whenua: ma te kino e aruaru te tangata tutu, kia turakina atu ia ki raro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:12">140:12</a> E matau ana ano ahau ma Ihowa e tohe te whakawa a te tangata e tukinotia ana, te mea hoki e rite ana ma nga rawakore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:13">140:13</a> He pono ka whakawhetai te hunga pai ki tou ingoa: ka noho te hunga tika ki tou aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:1">141:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, kua tangi nei ahau ki a koe; hohoro mai ki ahau: whakarongo ki toku reo ua karanga ahau ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:2">141:2</a> Kia whakatikaia taku inoi ki tou aroaro, hei whakakakara; te toronga atu hoki o oku ringa ano ko te whakahere o te ahiahi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:3">141:3</a> Homai he kaitiaki mo toku mangai, e Ihowa: tiakina te kuwaha o oku ngutu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:4">141:4</a> Kaua e whakaangahia toku ngakau ki te mea kino, ki te mahi i nga mahi hianga i roto i nga kaimahi i te kino: kaua ano ahau e kai i a ratou mea papai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:5">141:5</a> ¶ Ma te tangata tika ahau e patu: he mahi aroha tena; mana ahau e riri; he hinu tena ki runga ki te upoko; kaua ia e paopaongia e toku upoko: ahakoa hoki i roto i to ratou kino ka inoi tonu ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:6">141:6</a> E turakina ana o ratou kaiwhakawa ki te taha o te kohatu; a ka rongo ratou i aku kupu; he reka hoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:7">141:7</a> Pera i tetahi e haehae ana, e wawahi ana i te whenua, e titaritaria ana o matou wheua ki te waha o te reinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:8">141:8</a> Otiia e tau ana oku kanohi, e Ihowa, e te Ariki, ki a koe: ko koe toku whakawhirinakitanga; kaua toku wairua e waiho pani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:9">141:9</a> Tiakina ahau kei mau i nga mahanga i whakatakotoria e ratou moku, i nga rore hoki a nga kaimahi i te kino.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:10">141:10</a> Kia taka te hunga kino ki roto ki a ratou kupenga ano: ko ahau ia kia mawhiti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:1">142:1</a> ¶ He Makiri na Rawiri; he inoi i a ia i roto i te ana. He karanga ta toku reo ki a Ihowa; he inoi ta toku reo ki a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:2">142:2</a> Horahia ana taku inoi ki tona aroaro; whakaaturia ana e ahau toku mate ki tona aroaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:3">142:3</a> I te ngaromanga o toku wairua i roto i ahau i matau koe ki toku ara: kua whakatakotoria pukutia e ratou te mahanga moku i te ara i haere ai ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:4">142:4</a> ¶ Titiro ki toku taha matau, kia kite; kahore hoki tetahi tangata e mohio ana ki ahau; kahore he piringa moku; kahore tetahi e mahara ana ki toku wairua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:5">142:5</a> I karanga ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa: i mea, Ko koe toku piringa, toku wahi i te whenua o te hunga ora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:6">142:6</a> Tahuri mai ki taku karanga: kua whakaititia rawatia hoki ahau: whakaorangia ahau i oku kaitukino: he kaha rawa hoki ratou i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:7">142:7</a> Whakaputaina toku wairua i te herehere, kia whakamoemiti ai ahau ki tou ingoa: ka karapotia ahau e te hunga tika; nou ka atawhai nei i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:1">143:1</a> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, whakarongo ki taku inoi, kia titaha mai tou taringa ki aku inoi: whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau i runga i tou pono, i runga i tou tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:2">143:2</a> A kaua e anga e whakawa ki tau pononga: ki tau titiro hoki kahore tetahi mea ora e tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:3">143:3</a> Kua tukinotia hoki toku wairua e te hoariri; patua iho e ia toku ora ki raro ki te whenua: meinga ana ahau e ia kia noho i nga wahi pouri, kia rite ki nga tupapaku onamata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:4">143:4</a> Na reira i ngaro ai toku wairua i roto i ahau: moti rawa toku ngakau i roto i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:5">143:5</a> E mahara ana ahau ki nga ra onamata; e whakaaro ana ki au mahi katoa: e whakaaroaro ana ahau ki nga meatanga a ou ringa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:6">143:6</a> Totoro tonu atu oku ringa ki a koe: e hiainu ana toku wairua ki a koe, ano he whenua mauiui. (Hera.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:7">143:7</a> ¶ Hohoro te whakahoki kupu mai ki ahau, e Ihowa; ka hemo toku wairua: kei huna tou mata ki ahau; kei rite ahau ki te hunga e heke ana ki te poka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:8">143:8</a> Meinga kia rongo ahau ki tou aroha i te ata; e whakawhirinaki ana hoki ahau ki a koe: meinga kia matau ahau ki te ara e haere ai ahau; kua ara nei hoki toku wairua ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:9">143:9</a> Whakaorangia ahau, e Ihowa, i oku hoariri: ka kuhu nei ahau ki roto ki a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:10">143:10</a> Whakaakona ahau ki te mea i tau e pai ai; ko koe hoki toku Atua: he pai tou wairua; arahina ahau ki te whenua o te tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:11">143:11</a> Whakahauorangia ahau, e Ihowa, he whakaaro ki tou ingoa; whakaarohia tou tika, ka whakaputa ake i toku wairua i roto i te pouri.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:12">143:12</a> Aroha mai hoki, a huna oku hoariri: whakangaromia katoatia ano nga kaitukino o toku wairua: he pononga hoki ahau nau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:1">144:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri. Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, toku kamaka, e whakaako nei i oku ringa ki te whawhai, i oku maihao ki te tatau;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:2">144:2</a> Ko te atawhai moku, ko toku pa, ko toku pourewa me toku kaiwhakaora; ko toku whakangungu rakau, ko taku e whakawhirinaki ai; ko te kaipehi hoki o toku iwi ki raro i ahau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:3">144:3</a> E Ihowa, he aha te tangata i maharatia ai ia e koe? Te tama ranei a te tangata i whakaaroa ai ia e koe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:4">144:4</a> Ko te rite o te tangata kei te mea memeha noa: ona ra me te mea he atarangi e rere atu ana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:5">144:5</a> Whakapikoa iho ou rangi e Ihowa, a heke iho: pa ki nga maunga, a ka pongere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:6">144:6</a> Kokiritia mai he uira hei whakamarara i a ratou: koperea mai au pere, kia whati ai ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:7">144:7</a> Totoro iho tou ringa i runga: tangohia ahau, whakaorangia ahau i nga wai nunui, i te ringa o nga tangata ke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:8">144:8</a> E korero teka nei to ratou mangai, a he ringa matau teka to ratou ringa matau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:9">144:9</a> ¶ Ka waiatatia e ahau he waiata hou ki a koe, e te Atua: ka himene atu ahau ki a koe i runga i te hatere aho tekau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:10">144:10</a> Ko ia te kaihomai i te whakaoranga ki nga kingi, te kaiwhakaora i a Rawiri, i tana pononga, i te hoari whakamate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:11">144:11</a> Tangohia ahau, whakaorangia hoki i nga ringa o nga tangata ke, e korero teka nei o ratou mangai, a he ringa matau teka to ratou ringa matau.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:12">144:12</a> A, kia rite a matou tama i to ratou taitamarikitanga ki nga mahuri e tupu ake ana; a matou tamahine hoki ki nga kohatu kokonga, whakapaipai rawa, no te whare rangatira te tauira;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:13">144:13</a> Kia ki a matou pakoro, mo te tiki noa atu i tena mea, i tena mea: kia mano, kia tini nga hua o a matou hipi i o matou parae;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:14">144:14</a> Kia taimaha a matou kau i nga pikaunga; kia kahore he pakarutanga mai ki roto, he whatinga atu hoki ki waho, a kia kahore he aue i o matou huarahi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:15">144:15</a> Ka hari te iwi e pena ana: ae, ka hari te iwi ko Ihowa nei to ratou Atua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:1">145:1</a> ¶ Na Rawiri, he whakamoemiti. Ka whakanui ahau i a koe, e toku Atua, e te Kingi: ka whakapai ki tou ingoa ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:2">145:2</a> Ka whakapai ahau ki a koe i nga ra katoa: ka whakamoemiti ki tou ingoa ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:3">145:3</a> He nui a Ihowa, kia nui ano te whakamoemiti ki a ia: e kore e taea tona nui te rapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:4">145:4</a> Ma tetahi whakatupuranga e whakamoemiti au mahi, tae noa atu ki tetahi whakatupuranga; e korero hoki au mahi nunui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:5">145:5</a> Ka korerotia e ahau te kororia, te honore o tou nui, me au mahi whakamiharo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:6">145:6</a> Ka korerotia ano e te tangata te kaha o au mahi whakamataku: maku ano e korero tou nui.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:7">145:7</a> Ka whakapuakina e ratou te mahara ki te nui o tou pai: ka waiatatia ano tou tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:8">145:8</a> He atawhai a Ihowa, he aroha: he puhoi ki te riri, he nui tana mahi tohu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:9">145:9</a> He pai a Ihowa ki nga mea katoa; kei runga ano tona aroha i ana mahi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:10">145:10</a> ¶ E whakamoemititia koe, e Ihowa, e au mahi katoa: e whakapaingia e tou hunga tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:11">145:11</a> Ma ratou e korero te kororia o tou kingitanga, e kauwhau hoki tou kaha;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:12">145:12</a> Kia mohiotia ai e nga tama a te tangata ana mahi nunui, me te kororia o te maruwehi o tona kingitanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:13">145:13</a> He kingitanga mutungakore tou kingitanga; kei nga whakatupuranga katoa tou rangatiratanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:14">145:14</a> E tautokona ana e Ihowa te hunga katoa e hinga ana: e whakaarahia ake ana hoki e ia te hunga katoa kua whakapikoa iho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:15">145:15</a> E tatari ana ki a koe nga kanohi o te katoa; a e hoatu ana e koe ki a ratou ta ratou kai i te wa e tika ai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:16">145:16</a> E whakatuwhera ana koe i tou ringa, a makona iho i a koe te hiahia o nga mea ora katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:17">145:17</a> He tika nga ara katoa o Ihowa: he tapu hoki ana mahi katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:18">145:18</a> E tata ana a Ihowa ki te hunga katoa e karanga ana ki a ia: ki te hunga katoa e karanga pono ana ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:19">145:19</a> Ka whakamana e ia te hiahia o te hunga e wehi ana i a ia: e whakarongo hoki ia ki ta ratou tangi, a ka whakaora i a ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:20">145:20</a> Ko Ihowa hei tiaki i te hunga katoa e aroha ana ki a ia: ko te hunga kino katoa ia e ngaro i a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:21">145:21</a> Ma toku mangai e korero te whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa: kia whakapai ano hoki nga kikokiko katoa ki tona ingoa tapu ake ake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:1">146:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. E toku wairua, whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:2">146:2</a> I ahau e ora nei ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a Ihowa; ka himene ahau ki toku Atua i ahau i te ao nei.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:3">146:3</a> Kei whakawhirinaki ki nga rangatira, ki te tama ranei a te tangata, kahore nei he awhina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:4">146:4</a> Ko te putanga atu o tona wairua, hoki ana ia ki tona oneone; kore iho ona whakaaro i taua ra pu ano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:5">146:5</a> ¶ Ka hari te tangata ko te Atua nei o Hakopa tona kaiawhina: ko tana e tumanako ai ko Ihowa, ko tona Atua;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:6">146:6</a> Ko te kaihanga o te rangi, o te whenua, o te moana, o nga mea katoa o reira; e pupuri nei i te pono ake ake;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:7">146:7</a> E tohe nei i te whakawa a te hunga e tukinotia ana: e whangai nei i te hunga mate hiakai: ko Ihowa hei wewete i nga herehere:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:8">146:8</a> Ko Ihowa hei whakatitiro i nga matapo: ko Ihowa hei whakaara i te hunga kua whakapikoa iho: e aroha ana a Ihowa ki te hunga tika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:9">146:9</a> Ko Ihowa hei tiaki i nga manene; ko ia hei tautoko i te pani, i te pouaru: ko te ara ia o te hunga kino, ka huripokitia e ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:10">146:10</a> Ko Ihowa hei kingi ake ake, ae, ko tou Atua, e Hiona, tae noa ki nga whakatupuranga katoa. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:1">147:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa; he pai hoki te himene ki to tatou Atua: ahuareka rawa, ataahua tonu te whakamoemiti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:2">147:2</a> Ko Ihowa hei hanga i Hiruharama: mana hoki nga whati o Iharaira e kohikohi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:3">147:3</a> Ko ia hei rongoa i te hunga ngakau maru: mana e takai o ratou wahi mamae.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:4">147:4</a> E taua ana e ia nga whetu, te maha: e huaina ana hoki e ia o ratou ingoa katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:5">147:5</a> He nui to tatou Ariki, he nui hoki tona kaha: e kore e taea tona matauranga te whakaaro.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:6">147:6</a> Ko Ihowa te kaitautoko mo te hunga mahaki: ka turakina e ia te hunga kino ki te whenua.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:7">147:7</a> Waiata, whakawhetai ki a Ihowa: himene i runga i te hapa ki to tatou Atua:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:8">147:8</a> Ko ia nei te kaiuwhi i te rangi ki nga kapua, te kaihanga i te ua mo te whenua: e whakatupu ana ia i te tarutaru ki runga ki nga maunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:9">147:9</a> E homai ana e ia he kai ma te kirehe: ma nga pi raweni hoki ina tangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:10">147:10</a> E kore ia e ahuareka ki te kaha o te hoiho: e kore ia e manako ki nga waewae o te tangata.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:11">147:11</a> E manako ana a Ihowa ki te hunga e wehi ana i a ia, ki te hunga e tumanako ana ki tona aroha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:12">147:12</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa, e Hiruharama: whakamoemititia tou Atua, e Hiona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:13">147:13</a> Nana nei hoki i whakakaha nga tutaki o ou tatau: manaakitia ana e ia au tamariki i roto i a koe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:14">147:14</a> Nana ano i mau ai te rongo i roto i ou rohe: nana koe i makona ai i te witi pai rawa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:15">147:15</a> E tukua ana e ia tana kupu ki te whenua: tere rawa te rere o tana kupu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:16">147:16</a> E homai ana e ia te hukarere ano he huruhuru hipi: e whakatitaritaria ana te haupapa ano he pungarehu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:17">147:17</a> Maka mai ana e ia tana hauhunga ano he maramara: ko wai e tu i mua i tana matao?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:18">147:18</a> E tukua ana e ia tana kupu, a whakarewaina ana aua mea: ka meinga tana hau kia pupuhi, rere ana nga wai.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:19">147:19</a> E whakakitea ana e ia tana kupu ki a Hakopa; ana tikanga, me ana whakaritenga ki a Iharaira.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:20">147:20</a> Kahore i pera tana hanga ki tetahi iwi; kihai ano ana whakaritenga i mohiotia e ratou. whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:1">148:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa i runga i nga rangi: whakamoemititia ia i nga wahi tiketike.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:2">148:2</a> Whakamoemititia ia, e ana anahera katoa: whakamoemititia ia, e ana mano whaioio.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:3">148:3</a> Whakamoemititia ia, e te ra, e te marama: whakamoemititia ia, e nga whetu whakamarama katoa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:4">148:4</a> Whakamoemititia ia, e nga rangi o nga rangi, e nga wai hoki o runga atu i nga rangi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:5">148:5</a> Kia whakamoemititia e ratou te ingoa o Ihowa: nana hoki i whakahau, a kua hanga ratou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:6">148:6</a> Nana hoki aua mea i whakapumau ake ake: i whakatakotoria e ia he tikanga e kore e taka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:7">148:7</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa, i runga i te whenua, e nga tarakona, e nga rire katoa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:8">148:8</a> E te kapura, e te whatu; e te hukarere, e te kohu; e te tupuhi, e mahi nei i tana kupu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:9">148:9</a> E nga maunga, e nga puke katoa; e nga rakau hua, e nga hita katoa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:10">148:10</a> E nga kirehe, e nga kararehe katoa; e nga mea ngokingoki, e nga manu whai pakau:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:11">148:11</a> E nga kingi o te whenua, e nga iwi katoa; e nga rangatira, e nga kaiwhakawa katoa o te whenua:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:12">148:12</a> E nga taitama, e nga taitamahine; e nga koroheke ratou ko nga tamariki:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:13">148:13</a> Kia whakamoemititia e ratou te ingoa o Ihowa: nona anake hoki te ingoa e nui ana; kei runga ake i te whenua, i te rangi, tona kororia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:14">148:14</a> Ko ia hoki te kaiwhakaara o te haona o tana iwi; e whakamoemititia ana e ana tangata tapu katoa; e nga tama a Iharaira, e te iwi e tata ana ki a ia. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:1">149:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Waiatatia ki a Ihowa he waiata hou, me te whakamoemiti ki a ia i te whakaminenga o te hunga tapu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:2">149:2</a> Kia hari a Iharaira ki tona kaihanga: kia koa nga tama a Hiona ki to ratou Kingi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:3">149:3</a> Kia whakamoemiti ratou ki tona ingoa me te kanikani ano: kia himene ratou ki a ia i runga i te timipera, i te hapa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:4">149:4</a> E manako ana hoki a Ihowa ki tana iwi: mana e whakaataahua te hunga mahaki ki te whakaoranga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:5">149:5</a> Kia koa te hunga tapu i runga i te kororia: kia hamama ratou i te hari i runga i o ratou moenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:6">149:6</a> ¶ Kia whai whakamoemiti o ratou mangai ki te Atua, kia whai hoari matarua to ratou ringa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:7">149:7</a> Hei rapu utu i nga tauiwi, hei whiu i nga iwi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:8">149:8</a> Hei herehere i o ratou kingi ki te makameka, i o ratou tangata nunui ki nga here rino;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:9">149:9</a> Hei whakaputa ki a ratou i te whakaritenga kua oti te tuhituhi: No tona hunga tapu katoa tenei honore. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:1">150:1</a> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Whakamoemititia te Atua i tona wahi tapu: whakamoemititia ia i te kikorangi o tona kaha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:2">150:2</a> Whakamoemititia ia mo ana mahi nunui: kia rite ki te hira o tona nui te whakamoemiti ki a ia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:3">150:3</a> Whakamoemititia ia i runga i te tangi o te tetere: whakamoemititia ia i runga i te hatere, i te hapa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:4">150:4</a> Whakamoemititia ia i runga i te timipera, i te kanikani: whakamoemititia ia i runga i nga mea aho, i nga okana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:5">150:5</a> Whakamoemititia ia i runga i te himipora tangi nui: whakamoemititia ia i runga i te himipora tangi tiori.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:6">150:6</a> E nga mea katoa e whai manawa ana, whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.</p> 
 <p></p><hr>
